# HEB 3.0 + 4.0 Combined Upgrade — Complete CC Deployment Package

## MISSION
Upgrade the existing `hive-engine-builder` repo from HEB 2.0 to HEB 3.0+4.0 **in place**. Same repo, same Vercel project, same domains (`heb.hive.baby` + `hiveenginebuilder.hive.baby`). This is a single combined deploy that adds:

### HEB 3.0 Layer (Fleet Management)
- Engine Adoption — register existing hand-built engines into HEB management
- Fleet Operations — health dashboard, batch operations, rollback, deploy freeze, quota monitor
- Diff-Based Updates — Claude generates surgical patches for existing engines
- 22-Point Governance Audit — full QB compliance scanning with scored/graded reports
- Template Library — extract successful engines as reusable templates
- Staging Pipeline — dev branch preview deploys before production promotion
- Self-Improving Learner — tracks deploy outcomes, learns patterns, feeds hints into generation
- Engine Dependencies — cross-engine API/data/auth dependencies, topological deploy ordering
- Foundry — external developer submission pipeline with governance gating
- Monetization Wiring — auto-configure Stripe products, pricing tiers, webhook routes
- Scaling Config — Vercel scaling rules, regions, edge runtime, cron jobs per engine
- Engine Memory — persistent conversation history per engine

### HEB 4.0 Layer (Workshop + Factory)
- Brainstorm Mode — messy input to structured blueprint (Define)
- Live Preview — staging iframe with viewport/language switching (Gemba Walk)
- Break Mode — flag issues visually, fix queue, auto-fix (Andon Cord)
- Intent Memory — records WHY decisions were made, not just what (Org Learning)
- Ship It Gate — 22-point pre-flight that physically locks until passing (Poka-Yoke)
- The Factory — autonomous 11-step production pipeline (Autonomation)
- Batch Intent — one instruction applied intelligently across fleet (Heijunka)
- The Learner — deploy outcomes feed back into generation quality (Kaizen)

## PRESERVE FROM HEB 2.0
Keep these existing files/routes untouched:
- `app/page.tsx` (chat interface)
- `app/api/build-engine/route.ts`
- `app/api/list-engines/route.ts`
- `app/api/delete-engine/route.ts`
- `app/api/chat/route.ts`
- `app/api/update-engine/route.ts` (if it exists — HEB 3.0 adds a new version)
- All existing styling, layout, config files unless explicitly replaced below

## DEPLOYMENT SEQUENCE

1. **Freeze**: Set `DEPLOY_FROZEN=true` on the HEB Vercel project env vars
2. **Backup**: `git checkout -b heb-2.0-backup && git push origin heb-2.0-backup`
3. **Branch**: `git checkout main && git checkout -b heb-3.0-4.0-upgrade`
4. **Add all 66 files below** to the repo at the paths specified
5. **Update `package.json`**: Add these dependencies:
   ```json
   {
     "@neondatabase/serverless": "^0.10.0",
     "uuid": "^9.0.0"
   }
   ```
   And devDependencies:
   ```json
   {
     "@types/uuid": "^9.0.0"
   }
   ```
6. **Build test**: `npm install && npm run build` — fix any TypeScript errors
7. **Merge**: `git checkout main && git merge heb-3.0-4.0-upgrade`
8. **Push**: `git push origin main` — Vercel auto-deploys
9. **Unfreeze**: Set `DEPLOY_FROZEN=false`
10. **Verify endpoints** (all require `x-heb-secret` header):

**HEB 3.0 endpoints:**
- `GET /api/fleet-health` — fleet status
- `GET /api/templates` — empty array initially
- `GET /api/learner` — learner stats
- `POST /api/adopt-engine` — adopt single engine
- `POST /api/bulk-adopt` — adopt all engines
- `POST /api/audit-engine` — governance audit
- `POST /api/update-engine` — diff-based update
- `GET /api/engine-memory` — memory entries
- `POST /api/staging` — staging deploy
- `POST /api/promote` — promote staging to production
- `POST /api/rollback` — rollback deployment
- `POST /api/batch` — batch operations
- `GET /api/dependencies` — engine dependency graph
- `POST /api/foundry` — foundry submissions
- `GET /api/monetization` — monetization config
- `GET /api/scaling` — scaling config

**HEB 4.0 endpoints:**
- `POST /api/workshop/brainstorm` — brainstorm to blueprint
- `POST /api/workshop/generate` — SSE code generation stream
- `POST /api/workshop/preview` — staging preview deploy
- `POST /api/workshop/break-mode` — flag and fix issues
- `GET /api/workshop/decisions` — intent memory decisions
- `POST /api/workshop/ship-it` — pre-flight + ship
- `POST /api/workshop/factory` — factory status polling
- `POST /api/workshop/batch` — batch intent operations
- `GET /api/workshop/learner` — learner hints and stats

**Pages:**
- `/build` — HEB 3.0 Creator Console (7 tabs: Build, Fleet, Adopt, Update, Foundry, Learner, Settings)
- `/workshop` — HEB 4.0 Workshop (4 tabs: Workshop, Fleet, Batch, Learner)

## File: `ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md`

```markdown
# ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md — HEB 3.0

## Purpose
This document defines the structural grammar every Hive engine MUST follow. The Hive Engine Builder (HEB 3.0) enforces this grammar during build, adopt, audit, and update operations. No engine exists outside this grammar.

## GrapplerHook

Every engine must include a GrapplerHook metadata block pointing to QueenBee.MasterGrappler:

```typescript
export const GRAPPLER_HOOK = {
  engineSlug: '<engine-slug>',
  engineName: '<Engine Display Name>',
  version: '1.0.0',
  grapplerTarget: 'QueenBee.MasterGrappler',
  governanceVersion: '3.0',
  capabilities: ['<capability-1>', '<capability-2>'],
  dependencies: [],
  metadata: {
    author: 'Hive',
    license: 'proprietary',
    createdAt: '<ISO-8601>',
    updatedAt: '<ISO-8601>',
  },
};
```

Location: `lib/grappler-hook.ts` or `config/grappler-hook.ts`

## Required Files

Every engine must include:

| File | Purpose |
|---|---|
| `ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md` | This governance document |
| `README.md` | What the engine does, how to use it, how to deploy |
| `lib/grappler-hook.ts` | GrapplerHook metadata → QueenBee.MasterGrappler |
| FirstVisitCard component | First-time user experience with zero-friction onboarding |
| AutoDemo component | Self-running demo showing what the engine does |
| LanguageSelector component | 9-language multilingual ribbon (EN/AR/FR/ES/DE/ZH/JA/PT/HI) |

## Governance Rules

1. **Zero-friction onboarding** — No login walls or paywalls until paid tiers are chosen
2. **Invisible AI tone** — Warm, competent, non-robotic
3. **Studio templating** — Consistent templates from Hive Core
4. **Sunk cost architecture** — Every action increases user investment
5. **Universal portability** — Users can export/import any document or data type
6. **Legal-grade metadata** — Every artifact includes metadata for auditability
7. **Narrative continuity** — Consistent story across all engines and outputs
8. **Cross-engine referrals** — Engines subtly recommend other engines
9. **Clarity rituals** — Weekly digest emails with optional opt-outs
10. **Anticipation routines** — Core adoption multiplier
11. **Hallucination containment** — Pattern-bound, humble, non-speculative output
12. **Operational forwardability** — Outputs assignable to departments/roles with lifecycle tracking
13. **Free-text examples** — Faded rotating background examples in every input box
14. **Viral loop** — Every output includes a viral sharing mechanism
15. **Work artifact output** — Structured, reviewable, approvable, shareable, auditable artifacts
16. **Universal urgency** — Ethical urgency generation
17. **Global language agnosticism** — Works in any language
18. **Security headers** — HSTS, X-Frame-Options, CSP, X-Content-Type-Options

## Output Standards

All engine outputs must be:
- Delightful, instant, beautifully formatted
- Zero-friction, cognitively effortless
- Structured, unambiguous, jargon-free, noise-free
- Polished and reputation-enhancing
- Reviewable, approvable, shareable, and auditable

## Pricing Models

| Model | Description | Optional Support |
|---|---|---|
| `free` | Always free | ✅ ($20/$40/$60 one-time) |
| `free-with-support` | Free with prominent support option | ✅ |
| `dollar-per-year` | $1/year | ✅ |
| `monthly` | Monthly subscription | ❌ |
| `enterprise` | Unlimited per department, no seat limits | ❌ |

## Engine Lifecycle

```
Build/Adopt → Governance Audit → Register → Deploy → Monitor → Update → Re-audit
```

Every engine follows this lifecycle under HEB 3.0 management. No engine may drift from governance over time.

## File: `README.md`

```markdown
# 🐝 HEB 3.0 — The Engine Building Engine

**Hive Engine Builder 3.0** is the creator-only engine factory for the Hive ecosystem. It builds, adopts, manages, monitors, and self-improves all Hive engines from a single command center.

## What HEB 3.0 Does

| Capability | Description |
|---|---|
| **Build** | Free-text → full Next.js engine → GitHub repo → Vercel project → DNS → live URL |
| **Adopt** | Bring existing hand-built engines (HiveClarity, HiveClock, etc.) under HEB management |
| **Update** | Natural-language surgical code updates via AI-powered diff engine |
| **Fleet** | Health monitoring, quota tracking, batch operations across all engines |
| **Staging** | Preview deploys on dev branches before promoting to production |
| **Rollback** | Instant rollback to any previous Vercel deployment |
| **Governance** | 22-point QB governance audit with weighted scoring (A–F grades) |
| **Templates** | Extract templates from existing engines, instantiate for new builds |
| **Foundry** | External developer submission pipeline with auto-scan and governance gating |
| **Learner** | Deploy outcome tracking, pattern analysis, AVOID/PREFER prompt hints |
| **Dependencies** | Engine-to-engine dependency graph with cycle detection and topological deploy ordering |
| **Monetization** | Stripe product/pricing wiring per engine (free, $1/yr, monthly, enterprise) |
| **Scaling** | Per-engine Vercel scaling config (regions, timeouts, memory, cron, edge runtime) |

## Architecture

```
app/
  api/

    bulk-adopt/      POST — adopt all Hive engines at once (SSE)
    chat/            POST — legacy chat route [preserved from HEB 2.0]
    delete-engine/   DELETE — remove engine [preserved from HEB 2.0]
    dependencies/    GET/POST/DELETE — engine dependency graph
    fleet-health/    GET — fleet health + quota status
    foundry/         GET/POST/PATCH — external submissions
    learner/         GET — deploy insights and prompt hints
    list-engines/    GET — list all managed engines [preserved from HEB 2.0]
    monetization/    GET/POST — Stripe monetization config
    promote/         POST — promote staging to production (SSE)
    rollback/        POST — rollback to previous deployment
    scaling/         GET/POST — Vercel scaling config
    staging/         GET/POST — create and check staging deploys (SSE)
    templates/       GET/POST — template library
    update-engine/   POST — AI diff-based update (SSE)
  build/
    page.tsx         Creator Console UI (7 tabs: Build, Fleet, Adopt, Update, Foundry, Learner, Settings)
lib/

  auth.ts            Creator-only auth gate (HEB_CREATOR_SECRET)
  db.ts              Neon PostgreSQL layer (9 tables, auto-init)
  deploy-learner.ts  Deploy outcome tracking + pattern analysis
  diff-engine.ts     AI-powered surgical code updates
  engine-deps.ts     Dependency graph + topological sorting
  fleet.ts           Fleet health, quota, batch ops, rollback, deploy freeze
  foundry.ts         External submission pipeline

  scaling.ts         Vercel scaling configuration
  staging.ts         Preview deploy + promote pipeline
  template-library.ts Template extraction + instantiation
  types-v3.ts        Complete TypeScript type system
```

## Environment Variables

| Variable | Required | Purpose |
|---|---|---|
| `HEB_CREATOR_SECRET` | ✅ | Creator auth gate (requests without it get 404) |
| `ANTHROPIC_API_KEY` | ✅ | Claude API for code generation and diff engine |
| `GITHUB_TOKEN` | ✅ | GitHub API for repo creation and code push |
| `DATABASE_URL` | ✅ | Neon PostgreSQL connection string |
| `VERCEL_TOKEN` | ⚠️ | Vercel API for project creation and deploy (set this!) |
| `CLOUDFLARE_API_TOKEN` | ⚠️ | Cloudflare API for DNS record creation |
| `CLOUDFLARE_ZONE_ID` | ⚠️ | Cloudflare zone for hive.baby domain |
| `STRIPE_SECRET_KEY` | ⚠️ | Stripe API for monetization config |
| `GITHUB_OWNER` | ✅ | GitHub org/user for new repos (saggarsonny-boop) |

## Auth Model

All routes and the /build page are gated behind `HEB_CREATOR_SECRET`. Unauthenticated requests receive a **404** (not 401/403) to hide the existence of the endpoints. Auth is checked via:
- `Authorization: Bearer <secret>` header
- `x-heb-secret: <secret>` header
- `?secret=<secret>` query parameter
- `heb_creator` cookie (set via /api/auth, used by UI)

## Governance Checklist (22 points, 67 total weight)

Every generated and adopted engine is scored against:
ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md (5), GrapplerHook (5), README (3), FirstVisitCard (4), AutoDemo (3), Zero-friction onboarding (5), Multilingual ribbon (4), Invisible AI tone (3), Studio templating (3), Sunk cost architecture (2), Data export (3), Legal metadata (3), Narrative continuity (2), Cross-engine referrals (2), Clarity rituals (2), Anticipation routines (2), Hallucination containment (5), Operational forwardability (2), Free-text examples (3), Viral loop (3), Work artifact output (3), Universal urgency (1).

Grades: A (≥85%) | B (≥70%) | C (≥55%) | D (≥40%) | F (<40%)

## Safe Deploy Protocol

HEB 3.0 respects the existing safe deploy protocol:
- **Deploy freeze**: Toggle via fleet.ts — blocks all deploys when active
- **Quota monitor**: Daily limits (500 API calls, 20 deploys, 10 repos) with midnight reset
- **Staging**: Preview deploys on dev branch before promoting to production
- **Rollback**: Instant rollback to any previous Vercel deployment via alias

## Creator URL

`https://heb.hive.baby/build` — requires HEB_CREATOR_SECRET

## File: `app/api/adopt-engine/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Adopt Engine API (SSE streaming)
import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import { adoptEngine } from '@/lib/adopt';
import type { StreamEvent } from '@/lib/types-v3';

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const body = await req.json();
  const { slug, engineName, repoUrl, domain } = body;

  if (!slug || !repoUrl) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'slug and repoUrl are required' }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
  }

  const encoder = new TextEncoder();
  const stream = new ReadableStream({
    async start(controller) {
      const send = (event: StreamEvent) => {
        controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(`data: ${JSON.stringify(event)}\n\n`));
      };

      try {
        const result = await adoptEngine(
          { slug, engineName: engineName || slug, repoUrl, domain },
          send
        );
        send({ phase: 'complete', status: 'done', message: 'Engine adopted', data: result });
      } catch (err: any) {
        send({ phase: 'error', status: 'error', message: err.message });
      }

      controller.close();
    },
  });

  return new Response(stream, {
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream',
      'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
      Connection: 'keep-alive',
    },
  });
}

```

## File: `app/api/audit-engine/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Governance Audit API
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import { scanRepo } from '@/lib/repo-scanner';
import { runGovernanceAudit } from '@/lib/governance-audit';
import { getEngine } from '@/lib/db';

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const { slug } = await req.json();
  if (!slug) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'slug required' }, { status: 400 });

  const engine = await getEngine(slug);
  if (!engine) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Engine not found' }, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const scan = await scanRepo(engine.repo_url);
    const audit = await runGovernanceAudit(slug, scan);
    return NextResponse.json(audit);
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

```

## File: `app/api/auth/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Auth API (set creator cookie)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const { secret } = await req.json();
  const expected = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;

  if (!expected || secret !== expected) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not Found' }, { status: 404 });
  }

  const res = NextResponse.json({ success: true });
  res.cookies.set('heb_creator', secret, {
    path: '/',
    maxAge: 86400,
    sameSite: 'strict',
    secure: true,
    httpOnly: true,
  });

  return res;
}

```

## File: `app/api/batch/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Batch Operations API (SSE streaming)
import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import { executeBatch } from '@/lib/fleet';
import type { StreamEvent, BatchOperation } from '@/lib/types-v3';

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const body = await req.json();
  const { operation, engineSlugs, params } = body as {
    operation: BatchOperation['operation'];
    engineSlugs: string[];
    params?: Record<string, any>;
  };

  if (!operation || !engineSlugs?.length) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'operation and engineSlugs[] are required' }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
  }

  const encoder = new TextEncoder();
  const stream = new ReadableStream({
    async start(controller) {
      const send = (event: StreamEvent) => {
        controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(`data: ${JSON.stringify(event)}\n\n`));
      };

      try {
        const results = await executeBatch(
          { operation, engineSlugs, params: params || {}, results: [] },
          send
        );
        send({ phase: 'complete', status: 'done', message: `Batch complete: ${results.length} engines processed`, data: results });
      } catch (err: any) {
        send({ phase: 'error', status: 'error', message: err.message });
      }

      controller.close();
    },
  });

  return new Response(stream, {
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream',
      'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
      Connection: 'keep-alive',
    },
  });
}

```

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Bulk Adopt All Hive Engines (SSE streaming)
import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import { bulkAdopt } from '@/lib/adopt';
import type { StreamEvent } from '@/lib/types-v3';

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const encoder = new TextEncoder();
  const stream = new ReadableStream({
    async start(controller) {
      const send = (event: StreamEvent) => {
        controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(`data: ${JSON.stringify(event)}\n\n`));
      };

      try {
        const results = await bulkAdopt(send);
        send({ phase: 'complete', status: 'done', message: `Bulk adopt complete: ${results.length} engines`, data: results });
      } catch (err: any) {
        send({ phase: 'error', status: 'error', message: err.message });
      }

      controller.close();
    },
  });

  return new Response(stream, {
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream',
      'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
      Connection: 'keep-alive',
    },
  });
}

```

## File: `app/api/dependencies/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Engine Dependencies API
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import {
  buildDependencyGraph,
  addEngineDependency,
  removeEngineDependency,
  getDeployOrderFor,
  checkDependenciesDeployed,
  getDependencyEnvVars,
} from '@/lib/engine-deps';

// GET: Dependency graph or deploy order
export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const url = new URL(req.url);
  const slug = url.searchParams.get('slug');
  const action = url.searchParams.get('action') || 'graph';

  try {
    if (action === 'deploy-order' && slug) {
      const order = await getDeployOrderFor(slug);
      return NextResponse.json({ slug, deployOrder: order });
    }

    if (action === 'check' && slug) {
      const result = await checkDependenciesDeployed(slug);
      return NextResponse.json(result);
    }

    if (action === 'env-vars' && slug) {
      const vars = await getDependencyEnvVars(slug);
      return NextResponse.json({ slug, envVars: vars });
    }

    const graph = await buildDependencyGraph();
    return NextResponse.json(graph);
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

// POST: Add dependency
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const { fromSlug, toSlug, type, envVarKey } = await req.json();
  if (!fromSlug || !toSlug) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'fromSlug and toSlug required' }, { status: 400 });
  }

  try {
    await addEngineDependency({
      fromEngine: fromSlug,
      toEngine: toSlug,
      type: type || 'runtime',
      envVarKey,
    });
    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, message: `${fromSlug} → ${toSlug} dependency added` });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

// DELETE: Remove dependency
export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const { fromSlug, toSlug } = await req.json();
  if (!fromSlug || !toSlug) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'fromSlug and toSlug required' }, { status: 400 });
  }

  try {
    await removeEngineDependency(fromSlug, toSlug);
    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, message: `${fromSlug} → ${toSlug} dependency removed` });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

## File: `app/api/engine-memory/route.ts`

```typescript
// =============================================================================
// HEB 3.0 — ENGINE MEMORY API
// GET:  Retrieve memory for an engine (query params: slug, type, search, stats)
// POST: Add a memory entry (annotation, chat message, design decision)
// DELETE: Delete a specific entry or all memory for an engine
// =============================================================================

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import {
  getMemory,
  addMemory,
  deleteMemory,
  deleteEngineMemory,
  searchMemory,
  searchMemoryAcrossEngines,
  getMemoryStats,
  getAllEngineMemoryStats,
  assembleContext,
  formatContextForPrompt,
  recordAnnotation,
  recordDesignDecision,
  recordChatMessage,
  MemoryEntryType
} from '@/lib/engine-memory';

const SECRET = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;

function unauthorized() {
  return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not found' }, { status: 404 });
}

function checkAuth(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  if (!SECRET) return false;
  const cookie = req.cookies.get('heb_creator')?.value;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-creator-secret');
  const auth = req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return cookie === SECRET || header === SECRET || auth === SECRET;
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// GET — Read memory
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!checkAuth(req)) return unauthorized();

  const url = new URL(req.url);
  const slug = url.searchParams.get('slug');
  const action = url.searchParams.get('action') || 'list';

  try {
    // Global stats — no slug needed
    if (action === 'all-stats') {
      const stats = await getAllEngineMemoryStats();
      return NextResponse.json({ stats });
    }

    // Cross-engine search
    if (action === 'search-all') {
      const query = url.searchParams.get('q');
      if (!query) {
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing q parameter' }, { status: 400 });
      }
      const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('limit') || '20');
      const results = await searchMemoryAcrossEngines(query, limit);
      return NextResponse.json(results);
    }

    // Everything below requires a slug
    if (!slug) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing slug parameter' }, { status: 400 });
    }

    // Stats for one engine
    if (action === 'stats') {
      const stats = await getMemoryStats(slug);
      return NextResponse.json({ slug, ...stats });
    }

    // Full-text search within one engine
    if (action === 'search') {
      const query = url.searchParams.get('q');
      if (!query) {
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Missing q parameter' }, { status: 400 });
      }
      const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('limit') || '20');
      const results = await searchMemory(slug, query, limit);
      return NextResponse.json(results);
    }

    // Assembled context (what Claude would see)
    if (action === 'context') {
      const engineName = url.searchParams.get('name') || slug;
      const maxTokens = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('max_tokens') || '30000');
      const ctx = await assembleContext(slug, engineName, maxTokens);
      const formatted = formatContextForPrompt(ctx);
      return NextResponse.json({ ...ctx, formatted_prompt: formatted });
    }

    // Default: list entries
    const types = url.searchParams.get('types')?.split(',') as MemoryEntryType[] | undefined;
    const limit = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('limit') || '100');
    const offset = parseInt(url.searchParams.get('offset') || '0');
    const since = url.searchParams.get('since') || undefined;

    const entries = await getMemory(slug, { types, limit, offset, since });
    return NextResponse.json({ slug, entries, count: entries.length });

  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error('Engine memory GET error:', err);
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// POST — Add memory entry
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!checkAuth(req)) return unauthorized();

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const { slug, type, content, role, reasoning, metadata } = body;

    if (!slug || !content) {
      return NextResponse.json(
        { error: 'Missing required fields: slug, content' },
        { status: 400 }
      );
    }

    let id: string;

    switch (type) {
      case 'annotation':
        id = await recordAnnotation(slug, content, metadata || {});
        break;

      case 'design_decision':
        id = await recordDesignDecision(slug, content, reasoning || '', metadata || {});
        break;

      case 'chat_message':
        id = await recordChatMessage(slug, role || 'creator', content, metadata || {});
        break;

      default:
        // Generic add — any valid type
        const entryType: MemoryEntryType = type || 'annotation';
        id = await addMemory(
          slug,
          entryType,
          role || 'creator',
          content,
          metadata || {}
        );
    }

    return NextResponse.json({ id, slug, type: type || 'annotation', stored: true });

  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error('Engine memory POST error:', err);
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// DELETE — Remove memory
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export async function DELETE(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!checkAuth(req)) return unauthorized();

  const url = new URL(req.url);
  const id = url.searchParams.get('id');
  const slug = url.searchParams.get('slug');
  const purge = url.searchParams.get('purge') === 'true';

  try {
    // Delete single entry by id
    if (id) {
      const deleted = await deleteMemory(id);
      return NextResponse.json({ deleted, id });
    }

    // Purge all memory for an engine
    if (slug && purge) {
      const count = await deleteEngineMemory(slug);
      return NextResponse.json({ purged: true, slug, entries_deleted: count });
    }

    return NextResponse.json(
      { error: 'Provide either id (single delete) or slug+purge=true (purge all)' },
      { status: 400 }
    );

  } catch (err: any) {
    console.error('Engine memory DELETE error:', err);
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

```

## File: `app/api/foundry/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Foundry (External Submissions) API
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import { submitToFoundry, reviewSubmission, listSubmissions, deployFoundrySubmission } from '@/lib/foundry';
import type { StreamEvent } from '@/lib/types-v3';

// GET: List submissions (optional ?status= filter)
export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const status = new URL(req.url).searchParams.get('status') as any;
  try {
    const submissions = await listSubmissions(status || undefined);
    return NextResponse.json(submissions);
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

// POST: Submit engine to Foundry
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const body = await req.json();
  const { action } = body;

  // Deploy approved submission
  if (action === 'deploy') {
    const { submissionId } = body;
    if (!submissionId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'submissionId required' }, { status: 400 });

    const encoder = new TextEncoder();
    const stream = new ReadableStream({
      async start(controller) {
        const send = (event: StreamEvent) => {
          controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(`data: ${JSON.stringify(event)}\n\n`));
        };
        try {
          const result = await deployFoundrySubmission(submissionId, send);
          send({ phase: 'complete', status: 'done', message: 'Foundry engine deployed', data: result });
        } catch (err: any) {
          send({ phase: 'error', status: 'error', message: err.message });
        }
        controller.close();
      },
    });

    return new Response(stream, {
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream', 'Cache-Control': 'no-cache', Connection: 'keep-alive' },
    });
  }

  // Submit new engine
  const { repoUrl, submittedBy, notes } = body;
  if (!repoUrl || !submittedBy) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'repoUrl and submittedBy required' }, { status: 400 });
  }

  try {
    const submission = await submitToFoundry(repoUrl, submittedBy, notes);
    return NextResponse.json(submission);
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

// PATCH: Review submission (approve/reject/request-changes)
export async function PATCH(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const { submissionId, action, reviewNotes } = await req.json();
  if (!submissionId || !action) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'submissionId and action required' }, { status: 400 });
  }

  try {
    const result = await reviewSubmission(submissionId, { action, reviewNotes });
    return NextResponse.json(result);
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

```

// HEB 3.0 — Scaling Config API
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import { configureScaling, getScalingConfig, applyScalingPreset, SCALING_PRESETS } from '@/lib/scaling';
import type { StreamEvent } from '@/lib/types-v3';

// GET: Get scaling config for engine
export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const url = new URL(req.url);
  const slug = url.searchParams.get('slug');

  if (!slug) {
    return NextResponse.json({ presets: Object.keys(SCALING_PRESETS) });
  }

  try {
    const config = await getScalingConfig(slug);
    return NextResponse.json(config || { message: 'No scaling config — using defaults' });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

// POST: Configure scaling
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const body = await req.json();
  const { slug, preset, config } = body;

  if (!slug) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'slug required' }, { status: 400 });

  const encoder = new TextEncoder();
  const stream = new ReadableStream({
    async start(controller) {
      const send = (event: StreamEvent) => {
        controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(`data: ${JSON.stringify(event)}\n\n`));
      };

      try {
        let result;
        if (preset) {
          result = await applyScalingPreset(slug, preset, send);
        } else {
          result = await configureScaling(slug, config || {}, send);
        }
        send({ phase: 'complete', status: 'done', message: 'Scaling configured', data: result });
      } catch (err: any) {
        send({ phase: 'error', status: 'error', message: err.message });
      }

      controller.close();
    },
  });

  return new Response(stream, {
    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream', 'Cache-Control': 'no-cache', Connection: 'keep-alive' },
  });
}

## File: `app/api/templates/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Template Library API
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import { listTemplates, extractTemplate, instantiateTemplate, BUILT_IN_TEMPLATES } from '@/lib/template-library';

// GET: List all templates (built-in + extracted)
export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  try {
    const dbTemplates = await listTemplates();
    return NextResponse.json({
      builtIn: BUILT_IN_TEMPLATES,
      extracted: dbTemplates,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

// POST: Extract template from engine OR instantiate a template
export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const body = await req.json();
  const { action } = body;

  if (action === 'extract') {
    const { slug } = body;
    if (!slug) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'slug required' }, { status: 400 });
    try {
      const template = await extractTemplate(slug);
      return NextResponse.json(template);
    } catch (err: any) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
    }
  }

  if (action === 'instantiate') {
    const { templateId, variables } = body;
    if (!templateId || !variables) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'templateId and variables required' }, { status: 400 });
    }
    try {
      const files = await instantiateTemplate(templateId, variables);
      return NextResponse.json({ files });
    } catch (err: any) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
    }
  }

  return NextResponse.json({ error: 'action must be "extract" or "instantiate"' }, { status: 400 });
}

```

## File: `app/api/update-engine/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 3.0 — Update Engine via Diff (SSE streaming)
import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';
import { requireCreator } from '@/lib/auth';
import { computeDiff, applyPatches } from '@/lib/diff-engine';
import { recordDeployOutcome } from '@/lib/deploy-learner';
import { getEngine } from '@/lib/db';
import type { StreamEvent } from '@/lib/types-v3';

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const authErr = requireCreator(req);
  if (authErr) return authErr;

  const body = await req.json();
  const { slug, instruction } = body;

  if (!slug || !instruction) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'slug and instruction are required' }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
  }

  const engine = await getEngine(slug);
  if (!engine) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'Engine not found' }), {
      status: 404,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
  }

  const encoder = new TextEncoder();
  const stream = new ReadableStream({
    async start(controller) {
      const send = (event: StreamEvent) => {
        controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(`data: ${JSON.stringify(event)}\n\n`));
      };

      const startTime = Date.now();
      let success = false;
      let errorMsg = '';

      try {
        // 1. Compute diff
        send({ phase: 'diff', status: 'running', message: 'Analyzing instruction and computing code changes...' });
        const plan = await computeDiff(slug, engine.repo_url, instruction, send);
        send({ phase: 'diff', status: 'done', message: `${plan.patches.length} file(s) to change — risk: ${plan.risk}`, data: plan });

        // 2. Safety check
        if (plan.risk === 'high') {
          send({ phase: 'safety', status: 'running', message: 'High-risk change detected — applying with extra caution' });
        }

        // 3. Apply patches
        send({ phase: 'apply', status: 'running', message: 'Pushing changes to GitHub...' });
        const owner = engine.repo_url.split('/').slice(-2)[0];
        const repo = engine.repo_url.split('/').pop()!;
        await applyPatches(owner, repo, plan.patches, `HEB 3.0 update: ${instruction.slice(0, 60)}`, 'deploy');
        send({ phase: 'apply', status: 'done', message: 'Code pushed — Vercel auto-deploy triggered' });

        // 4. Record outcome
        success = true;
        send({ phase: 'complete', status: 'done', message: `Engine "${engine.name}" updated successfully`, data: {
          filesChanged: plan.patches.length,
          risk: plan.risk,
          affectedRoutes: plan.affectedRoutes,
        }});
      } catch (err: any) {
        errorMsg = err.message;
        send({ phase: 'error', status: 'error', message: err.message });
      }

      // Record deploy outcome for learner
      try {
        await recordDeployOutcome({
          engineSlug: slug,
          deployId: `update-${Date.now()}`,
          trigger: 'update-engine',
          success,
          duration: Date.now() - startTime,
          error: errorMsg || undefined,
          codeSnapshot: instruction,
        });
      } catch {}

      controller.close();
    },
  });

  return new Response(stream, {
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream',
      'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
      Connection: 'keep-alive',
    },
  });
}

```

## File: `app/build/page.tsx`

```tsx
'use client';

import { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';

// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Creator Console (Main Build Page)
// Tabs: Build | Fleet | Adopt | Update | Foundry | Learner | Settings
// ============================================================

type Tab = 'build' | 'fleet' | 'adopt' | 'update' | 'foundry' | 'learner' | 'settings';

interface LogEntry {
  time: string;
  phase: string;
  status: string;
  message: string;
  data?: any;
}

interface Engine {
  slug: string;
  name: string;
  domain: string;
  repo_url: string;
  status: string;
  governance_score: number | null;
  governance_grade: string | null;
  created_at: string;
}

// === Auth Gate ===
function AuthGate({ onAuth }: { onAuth: () => void }) {
  const [secret, setSecret] = useState('');
  const [error, setError] = useState('');

  const handleAuth = async () => {
    const res = await fetch('/api/auth', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ secret }),
    });
    if (res.ok) {
      onAuth();
    } else {
      setError('Access denied');
    }
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ minHeight: '100vh', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'center', background: '#0a0a0a' }}>
      <div style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 12, padding: 40, maxWidth: 400, width: '100%' }}>
        <h2 style={{ color: '#f5c518', marginBottom: 8, fontSize: 20 }}>🐝 HEB 3.0</h2>
        <p style={{ color: '#888', marginBottom: 24, fontSize: 14 }}>Engine Building Engine — Creator Access</p>
        <input
          type="password"
          placeholder="Creator secret"
          value={secret}
          onChange={e => { setSecret(e.target.value); setError(''); }}
          onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleAuth()}
          style={{ width: '100%', padding: '10px 14px', background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14, marginBottom: 12, boxSizing: 'border-box' }}
        />
        {error && <p style={{ color: '#ff4444', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 12 }}>{error}</p>}
        <button onClick={handleAuth} style={{ width: '100%', padding: '10px 14px', background: '#f5c518', color: '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: 8, fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 14 }}>
          Enter
        </button>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}

// === SSE Hook ===
function useSSE() {
  const [logs, setLogs] = useState<LogEntry[]>([]);
  const [isRunning, setIsRunning] = useState(false);

  const execute = useCallback(async (url: string, body: any) => {
    setLogs([]);
    setIsRunning(true);

    try {
      const res = await fetch(url, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify(body),
      });

      if (!res.ok) {
        const err = await res.json();
        setLogs([{ time: now(), phase: 'error', status: 'error', message: err.error || 'Request failed' }]);
        setIsRunning(false);
        return;
      }

      const reader = res.body?.getReader();
      const decoder = new TextDecoder();
      if (!reader) return;

      let buffer = '';
      while (true) {
        const { done, value } = await reader.read();
        if (done) break;
        buffer += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
        const lines = buffer.split('\n');
        buffer = lines.pop() || '';
        for (const line of lines) {
          if (line.startsWith('data: ')) {
            try {
              const event = JSON.parse(line.slice(6));
              setLogs(prev => [...prev, { time: now(), ...event }]);
            } catch {}
          }
        }
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      setLogs(prev => [...prev, { time: now(), phase: 'error', status: 'error', message: err.message }]);
    }

    setIsRunning(false);
  }, []);

  return { logs, isRunning, execute, clearLogs: () => setLogs([]) };
}

function now() { return new Date().toLocaleTimeString(); }

// === Log Panel Component ===
function LogPanel({ logs, title }: { logs: LogEntry[]; title?: string }) {
  const endRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);
  useEffect(() => { endRef.current?.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' }); }, [logs]);

  const statusColor = (s: string) => {
    if (s === 'done') return '#4ade80';
    if (s === 'error') return '#ff4444';
    return '#f5c518';
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ background: '#0d0d0d', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 16, marginTop: 16, maxHeight: 400, overflowY: 'auto', fontFamily: 'monospace', fontSize: 13 }}>
      {title && <div style={{ color: '#666', marginBottom: 8, fontSize: 11, textTransform: 'uppercase', letterSpacing: 1 }}>{title}</div>}
      {logs.length === 0 && <div style={{ color: '#444' }}>Waiting for events...</div>}
      {logs.map((l, i) => (
        <div key={i} style={{ marginBottom: 4, display: 'flex', gap: 8 }}>
          <span style={{ color: '#555', minWidth: 70 }}>{l.time}</span>
          <span style={{ color: statusColor(l.status), minWidth: 14 }}>
            {l.status === 'done' ? '✓' : l.status === 'error' ? '✗' : '⟳'}
          </span>
          <span style={{ color: '#ccc' }}>{l.message}</span>
        </div>
      ))}
      <div ref={endRef} />
    </div>
  );
}

// === Build Tab ===
function BuildTab() {
  const [prompt, setPrompt] = useState('');
  const { logs, isRunning, execute } = useSSE();

  const handleBuild = () => {
    if (!prompt.trim() || isRunning) return;
    execute('/api/build-engine', { prompt: prompt.trim() });
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3 style={{ color: '#f5c518', marginBottom: 4 }}>Build New Engine</h3>
      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 16 }}>Describe the engine you want to build. HEB will generate code, create a repo, deploy to Vercel, configure DNS, and return a live URL.</p>
      <textarea
        value={prompt}
        onChange={e => setPrompt(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="e.g., Build me a Family Rituals Engine that helps families create and track meaningful daily and weekly rituals..."
        rows={4}
        style={{ width: '100%', padding: 14, background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14, resize: 'vertical', boxSizing: 'border-box', fontFamily: 'inherit' }}
      />
      <button
        onClick={handleBuild}
        disabled={isRunning || !prompt.trim()}
        style={{ marginTop: 12, padding: '10px 24px', background: isRunning ? '#555' : '#f5c518', color: '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: 8, fontWeight: 600, cursor: isRunning ? 'default' : 'pointer', fontSize: 14 }}
      >
        {isRunning ? '⟳ Building...' : '🔨 Build Engine'}
      </button>
      {logs.length > 0 && <LogPanel logs={logs} title="Build Log" />}
    </div>
  );
}

// === Fleet Tab ===
function FleetTab() {
  const [engines, setEngines] = useState<Engine[]>([]);
  const [health, setHealth] = useState<any>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const loadData = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const [engRes, healthRes] = await Promise.all([
        fetch('/api/list-engines'),
        fetch('/api/fleet-health'),
      ]);
      if (engRes.ok) setEngines(await engRes.json());
      if (healthRes.ok) setHealth(await healthRes.json());
    } catch {}
    setLoading(false);
  };

  useEffect(() => { loadData(); }, []);

  const gradeColor = (g: string | null) => {
    if (!g) return '#555';
    if (g === 'A') return '#4ade80';
    if (g === 'B') return '#a3e635';
    if (g === 'C') return '#f5c518';
    if (g === 'D') return '#fb923c';
    return '#ff4444';
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center', marginBottom: 16 }}>
        <h3 style={{ color: '#f5c518', margin: 0 }}>Fleet Dashboard</h3>
        <button onClick={loadData} style={{ padding: '6px 16px', background: '#222', color: '#ccc', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 6, cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 13 }}>
          ↻ Refresh
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Quota */}
      {health?.quota && (
        <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(3, 1fr)', gap: 12, marginBottom: 20 }}>
          {Object.entries(health.quota).map(([key, val]: any) => (
            <div key={key} style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 12 }}>
              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 11, textTransform: 'uppercase', marginBottom: 4 }}>{key.replace(/([A-Z])/g, ' $1')}</div>
              <div style={{ color: val.remaining < val.limit * 0.2 ? '#ff4444' : '#fff', fontSize: 20, fontWeight: 600 }}>
                {val.used}/{val.limit}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {loading ? (
        <div style={{ color: '#888' }}>Loading fleet data...</div>
      ) : engines.length === 0 ? (
        <div style={{ color: '#888' }}>No engines registered. Use the Adopt tab to bring in existing engines.</div>
      ) : (
        <div style={{ display: 'grid', gap: 8 }}>
          {engines.map(eng => (
            <div key={eng.slug} style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 16, display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr auto auto auto', alignItems: 'center', gap: 16 }}>
              <div>
                <div style={{ color: '#fff', fontWeight: 600, fontSize: 15 }}>{eng.name}</div>
                <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 12, marginTop: 2 }}>{eng.domain || eng.slug}</div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 12 }}>{eng.repo_url.split('/').pop()}</div>
              <div style={{ color: gradeColor(eng.governance_grade), fontWeight: 700, fontSize: 18, minWidth: 30, textAlign: 'center' }}>
                {eng.governance_grade || '—'}
              </div>
              <div style={{
                padding: '4px 10px',
                borderRadius: 12,
                fontSize: 11,
                fontWeight: 600,
                background: eng.status === 'active' ? 'rgba(74,222,128,0.15)' : 'rgba(255,68,68,0.15)',
                color: eng.status === 'active' ? '#4ade80' : '#ff4444',
              }}>
                {eng.status}
              </div>
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// === Adopt Tab ===
function AdoptTab() {
  const [slug, setSlug] = useState('');
  const [repoUrl, setRepoUrl] = useState('');
  const [domain, setDomain] = useState('');
  const { logs, isRunning, execute, clearLogs } = useSSE();

  const handleAdopt = () => {
    if (!slug.trim() || !repoUrl.trim() || isRunning) return;
    execute('/api/adopt-engine', { slug: slug.trim(), repoUrl: repoUrl.trim(), domain: domain.trim() || undefined });
  };

  const handleBulkAdopt = () => {
    if (isRunning) return;
    clearLogs();
    execute('/api/bulk-adopt', {});
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3 style={{ color: '#f5c518', marginBottom: 4 }}>Adopt Existing Engine</h3>
      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 16 }}>
        Bring an existing hand-built engine into HEB management. Scans the repo, runs governance audit, and registers it.
      </p>

      <button
        onClick={handleBulkAdopt}
        disabled={isRunning}
        style={{ marginBottom: 20, padding: '10px 24px', background: '#1a3a1a', color: '#4ade80', border: '1px solid #2a5a2a', borderRadius: 8, fontWeight: 600, cursor: isRunning ? 'default' : 'pointer', fontSize: 14 }}
      >
        ⚡ Bulk Adopt All Hive Engines
      </button>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gap: 12, marginBottom: 16 }}>
        <input placeholder="Engine slug (e.g., hive-clarity)" value={slug} onChange={e => setSlug(e.target.value)}
          style={{ padding: '10px 14px', background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14 }} />
        <input placeholder="Repo URL (e.g., https://github.com/saggarsonny-boop/hive-clarity)" value={repoUrl} onChange={e => setRepoUrl(e.target.value)}
          style={{ padding: '10px 14px', background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14 }} />
        <input placeholder="Domain (e.g., clarity.hive.baby) — optional" value={domain} onChange={e => setDomain(e.target.value)}
          style={{ padding: '10px 14px', background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14 }} />
      </div>

      <button onClick={handleAdopt} disabled={isRunning || !slug.trim() || !repoUrl.trim()}
        style={{ padding: '10px 24px', background: isRunning ? '#555' : '#f5c518', color: '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: 8, fontWeight: 600, cursor: isRunning ? 'default' : 'pointer', fontSize: 14 }}>
        {isRunning ? '⟳ Adopting...' : '📥 Adopt Engine'}
      </button>

      {logs.length > 0 && <LogPanel logs={logs} title="Adopt Log" />}
    </div>
  );
}

// === Update Tab ===
function UpdateTab() {
  const [slug, setSlug] = useState('');
  const [instruction, setInstruction] = useState('');
  const { logs, isRunning, execute } = useSSE();

  const handleUpdate = () => {
    if (!slug.trim() || !instruction.trim() || isRunning) return;
    execute('/api/update-engine', { slug: slug.trim(), instruction: instruction.trim() });

  return (
    <div>
      <h3 style={{ color: '#f5c518', marginBottom: 4 }}>Update Engine</h3>
      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 16 }}>
        Describe what you want to change. HEB will compute a surgical diff, push it, and trigger a safe deploy.

      <input placeholder="Engine slug" value={slug} onChange={e => setSlug(e.target.value)}
        style={{ width: '100%', padding: '10px 14px', background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14, marginBottom: 12, boxSizing: 'border-box' }} />

      <textarea value={instruction} onChange={e => setInstruction(e.target.value)}
        placeholder="e.g., Add a dark mode toggle to the top right of the page that persists in localStorage..."
        rows={4}
        style={{ width: '100%', padding: 14, background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14, resize: 'vertical', boxSizing: 'border-box', fontFamily: 'inherit' }} />

      <button onClick={handleUpdate} disabled={isRunning || !slug.trim() || !instruction.trim()}
        style={{ marginTop: 12, padding: '10px 24px', background: isRunning ? '#555' : '#f5c518', color: '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: 8, fontWeight: 600, cursor: isRunning ? 'default' : 'pointer', fontSize: 14 }}>
        {isRunning ? '⟳ Updating...' : '✏️ Update Engine'}
      </button>

      {logs.length > 0 && <LogPanel logs={logs} title="Update Log" />}
    </div>
  );
}

// === Foundry Tab ===
function FoundryTab() {
  const [submissions, setSubmissions] = useState<any[]>([]);
  const [repoUrl, setRepoUrl] = useState('');
  const [submittedBy, setSubmittedBy] = useState('');
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  const load = async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/foundry');
      if (res.ok) setSubmissions(await res.json());
    } catch {}
    setLoading(false);
  };

  useEffect(() => { load(); }, []);

  const handleSubmit = async () => {
    if (!repoUrl.trim() || !submittedBy.trim()) return;
    await fetch('/api/foundry', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ repoUrl: repoUrl.trim(), submittedBy: submittedBy.trim() }),
    });
    setRepoUrl('');
    setSubmittedBy('');
    load();
  };

  const handleReview = async (id: string, action: string) => {
    await fetch('/api/foundry', {
      method: 'PATCH',
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
      body: JSON.stringify({ submissionId: id, action }),
    });
    load();
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3 style={{ color: '#f5c518', marginBottom: 4 }}>Foundry</h3>
      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 16 }}>Review external engine submissions. Auto-scanned and governance-audited on submission.</p>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: '1fr 1fr auto', gap: 12, marginBottom: 20 }}>
        <input placeholder="Repo URL" value={repoUrl} onChange={e => setRepoUrl(e.target.value)}
          style={{ padding: '10px 14px', background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14 }} />
        <input placeholder="Submitted by" value={submittedBy} onChange={e => setSubmittedBy(e.target.value)}
          style={{ padding: '10px 14px', background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14 }} />
        <button onClick={handleSubmit} style={{ padding: '10px 20px', background: '#f5c518', color: '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: 8, fontWeight: 600, cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 14 }}>
          Submit
        </button>
      </div>

      {loading ? <div style={{ color: '#888' }}>Loading...</div> : submissions.length === 0 ? (
        <div style={{ color: '#888' }}>No submissions yet.</div>
      ) : (
        <div style={{ display: 'grid', gap: 8 }}>
          {submissions.map((s: any) => (
            <div key={s.id} style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 14, display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'space-between', alignItems: 'center' }}>
              <div>
                <div style={{ color: '#fff', fontWeight: 500, fontSize: 14 }}>{s.repo_url}</div>
                <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 12 }}>by {s.submitted_by} · score: {s.governance_score ?? '—'} · {s.status}</div>
              </div>
              {s.status === 'pending-review' && (
                <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 8 }}>
                  <button onClick={() => handleReview(s.id, 'approve')} style={{ padding: '4px 12px', background: '#1a3a1a', color: '#4ade80', border: '1px solid #2a5a2a', borderRadius: 6, cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 12 }}>Approve</button>
                  <button onClick={() => handleReview(s.id, 'reject')} style={{ padding: '4px 12px', background: '#3a1a1a', color: '#ff4444', border: '1px solid #5a2a2a', borderRadius: 6, cursor: 'pointer', fontSize: 12 }}>Reject</button>
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// === Learner Tab ===
function LearnerTab() {
  const [report, setReport] = useState<any>(null);
  const [hints, setHints] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);

  useEffect(() => {
    (async () => {
      try {
        const [repRes, hintRes] = await Promise.all([
          fetch('/api/learner?type=report'),
          fetch('/api/learner?type=hints'),
        ]);
        if (repRes.ok) setReport(await repRes.json());
        if (hintRes.ok) {
          const h = await hintRes.json();
          setHints(h.hints || []);
        }
      } catch {}
      setLoading(false);
    })();
  }, []);

  return (
    <div>
      <h3 style={{ color: '#f5c518', marginBottom: 4 }}>Deploy Learner</h3>
      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 16 }}>Insights from deploy history. HEB learns from successes and failures to improve future builds.</p>

      {loading ? <div style={{ color: '#888' }}>Analyzing deploy history...</div> : (
        <>
          {report && (
            <div style={{ display: 'grid', gridTemplateColumns: 'repeat(3, 1fr)', gap: 12, marginBottom: 20 }}>
              <div style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 14 }}>
                <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 11, textTransform: 'uppercase', marginBottom: 4 }}>Total Deploys</div>
                <div style={{ color: '#fff', fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 700 }}>{report.totalDeploys || 0}</div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 14 }}>
                <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 11, textTransform: 'uppercase', marginBottom: 4 }}>Success Rate</div>
                <div style={{ color: '#4ade80', fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 700 }}>{report.successRate || '—'}%</div>
              </div>
              <div style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 14 }}>
                <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 11, textTransform: 'uppercase', marginBottom: 4 }}>Avg Duration</div>
                <div style={{ color: '#fff', fontSize: 24, fontWeight: 700 }}>{report.avgDuration ? `${(report.avgDuration / 1000).toFixed(1)}s` : '—'}</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          )}

          {hints.length > 0 && (
            <div style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 16 }}>
              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 11, textTransform: 'uppercase', marginBottom: 8 }}>Active Prompt Hints</div>
              {hints.map((h, i) => (
                <div key={i} style={{ color: h.startsWith('AVOID') ? '#ff8888' : '#88ff88', fontSize: 13, fontFamily: 'monospace', marginBottom: 4 }}>
                  {h}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}

          {report?.insights?.length > 0 && (
            <div style={{ marginTop: 16 }}>
              <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 11, textTransform: 'uppercase', marginBottom: 8 }}>Insights</div>
              {report.insights.map((ins: any, i: number) => (
                <div key={i} style={{ background: '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 8, padding: 12, marginBottom: 8 }}>
                  <div style={{ color: '#fff', fontSize: 14, fontWeight: 500 }}>{ins.pattern}</div>
                  <div style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 12 }}>{ins.recommendation} (confidence: {(ins.confidence * 100).toFixed(0)}%)</div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}
        </>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// === Settings Tab ===
function SettingsTab() {
  const [batchOp, setBatchOp] = useState('governance-audit');
  const { logs, isRunning, execute } = useSSE();
  const [engines, setEngines] = useState<Engine[]>([]);
  const [selected, setSelected] = useState<string[]>([]);

  useEffect(() => {
    (async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/list-engines');
        if (res.ok) setEngines(await res.json());
      } catch {}
    })();
  }, []);

  const toggleEngine = (slug: string) => {
    setSelected(prev => prev.includes(slug) ? prev.filter(s => s !== slug) : [...prev, slug]);
  };

  const handleBatch = () => {
    if (isRunning || selected.length === 0) return;
    execute('/api/batch', { operation: batchOp, engineSlugs: selected });
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <h3 style={{ color: '#f5c518', marginBottom: 4 }}>Batch Operations & Settings</h3>
      <p style={{ color: '#888', fontSize: 13, marginBottom: 16 }}>Run operations across multiple engines at once.</p>

      <div style={{ display: 'flex', gap: 12, marginBottom: 16 }}>
        <select value={batchOp} onChange={e => setBatchOp(e.target.value)}
          style={{ flex: 1, padding: '10px 14px', background: '#1a1a1a', border: '1px solid #333', borderRadius: 8, color: '#fff', fontSize: 14 }}>
          <option value="governance-audit">Governance Audit</option>
          <option value="add-ribbon">Add Multilingual Ribbon</option>
          <option value="add-first-visit-card">Add FirstVisitCard</option>
          <option value="add-auto-demo">Add AutoDemo</option>
          <option value="security-headers">Add Security Headers</option>
        </select>
        <button onClick={handleBatch} disabled={isRunning || selected.length === 0}
          style={{ padding: '10px 24px', background: isRunning ? '#555' : '#f5c518', color: '#000', border: 'none', borderRadius: 8, fontWeight: 600, cursor: isRunning ? 'default' : 'pointer', fontSize: 14 }}>
          {isRunning ? '⟳ Running...' : `Run on ${selected.length} engine(s)`}
        </button>
      </div>

      <div style={{ display: 'grid', gap: 6, marginBottom: 16 }}>
        {engines.map(eng => (
          <label key={eng.slug} style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10, padding: '8px 12px', background: selected.includes(eng.slug) ? '#1a2a1a' : '#111', border: '1px solid #222', borderRadius: 6, cursor: 'pointer' }}>
            <input type="checkbox" checked={selected.includes(eng.slug)} onChange={() => toggleEngine(eng.slug)} />
            <span style={{ color: '#fff', fontSize: 14 }}>{eng.name}</span>
            <span style={{ color: '#555', fontSize: 12, marginLeft: 'auto' }}>{eng.slug}</span>
          </label>
        ))}
      </div>

      {logs.length > 0 && <LogPanel logs={logs} title="Batch Log" />}
    </div>
  );
}

// === Main Page ===
export default function BuildPage() {
  const [authed, setAuthed] = useState(false);
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<Tab>('fleet');

  useEffect(() => {
    // Check if already authed via cookie
    if (document.cookie.includes('heb_creator=')) setAuthed(true);
  }, []);

  if (!authed) return <AuthGate onAuth={() => setAuthed(true)} />;

  const tabs: { key: Tab; label: string; icon: string }[] = [
    { key: 'build', label: 'Build', icon: '🔨' },
    { key: 'fleet', label: 'Fleet', icon: '🏠' },
    { key: 'adopt', label: 'Adopt', icon: '📥' },
    { key: 'update', label: 'Update', icon: '✏️' },
    { key: 'foundry', label: 'Foundry', icon: '🔧' },
    { key: 'learner', label: 'Learner', icon: '🧠' },
    { key: 'settings', label: 'Settings', icon: '⚙️' },
  ];

  return (
    <div style={{ minHeight: '100vh', background: '#0a0a0a', color: '#fff' }}>
      {/* Header */}
      <header style={{ borderBottom: '1px solid #222', padding: '16px 32px', display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', justifyContent: 'space-between' }}>
        <div style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center', gap: 10 }}>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 24 }}>🐝</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 18, fontWeight: 700, color: '#f5c518' }}>HEB 3.0</span>
          <span style={{ fontSize: 13, color: '#666', marginLeft: 8 }}>Engine Building Engine</span>
        </div>
        <div style={{ fontSize: 12, color: '#555' }}>Creator Console</div>
      </header>

      {/* Tabs */}
      <nav style={{ borderBottom: '1px solid #222', padding: '0 32px', display: 'flex', gap: 0 }}>
        {tabs.map(tab => (
          <button
            key={tab.key}
            onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab.key)}
            style={{
              padding: '12px 20px',
              background: 'transparent',
              border: 'none',
              borderBottom: activeTab === tab.key ? '2px solid #f5c518' : '2px solid transparent',
              color: activeTab === tab.key ? '#f5c518' : '#666',
              cursor: 'pointer',
              fontSize: 14,
              fontWeight: activeTab === tab.key ? 600 : 400,
              display: 'flex',
              alignItems: 'center',
              gap: 6,
            }}
          >
            <span>{tab.icon}</span>
            {tab.label}
          </button>
        ))}
      </nav>

      {/* Content */}
      <main style={{ padding: '32px', maxWidth: 960, margin: '0 auto' }}>
        {activeTab === 'build' && <BuildTab />}
        {activeTab === 'fleet' && <FleetTab />}
        {activeTab === 'adopt' && <AdoptTab />}
        {activeTab === 'update' && <UpdateTab />}
        {activeTab === 'foundry' && <FoundryTab />}
        {activeTab === 'learner' && <LearnerTab />}
        {activeTab === 'settings' && <SettingsTab />}
      </main>
    </div>
  );
}
