## File: `components/MemoryPanel.tsx`

```tsx
// =============================================================================
// HEB 3.0 — ENGINE MEMORY PANEL
// Per-engine conversation history, design decisions, search, annotations
// Designed to be embedded in the Fleet tab or as a slide-out panel
// =============================================================================

'use client';

import { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';

interface MemoryEntry {
  id: string;
  engine_slug: string;
  entry_type: string;
  role: string;
  content: string;
  metadata: Record<string, any>;
  created_at: string;
}

interface MemoryStats {
  total_entries: number;
  by_type: Record<string, number>;
  first_entry: string | null;
  last_entry: string | null;
  has_rolling_summary: boolean;
  estimated_tokens: number;
}

const TYPE_ICONS: Record<string, string> = {
  design_prompt: '💡',
  design_plan: '📐',
  design_decision: '⚖️',
  generated_code: '💻',
  governance_result: '🛡️',
  update_request: '✏️',
  update_plan: '📋',
  update_diff: '🔀',
  deploy_result: '🚀',
  chat_message: '💬',
  adoption_note: '📥',
  rollback_note: '⏪',
  batch_operation: '⚡',
  annotation: '📝',
};

const TYPE_COLORS: Record<string, string> = {
  design_prompt: 'text-amber-400',
  design_plan: 'text-blue-400',
  design_decision: 'text-purple-400',
  generated_code: 'text-green-400',
  governance_result: 'text-cyan-400',
  update_request: 'text-yellow-400',
  update_plan: 'text-blue-300',
  update_diff: 'text-orange-400',
  deploy_result: 'text-emerald-400',
  chat_message: 'text-gray-400',
  adoption_note: 'text-indigo-400',
  rollback_note: 'text-red-400',
  batch_operation: 'text-violet-400',
  annotation: 'text-gray-300',
};

const TYPE_LABELS: Record<string, string> = {
  design_prompt: 'Design Prompt',
  design_plan: 'Architecture Plan',
  design_decision: 'Design Decision',
  generated_code: 'Code Generated',
  governance_result: 'Governance Audit',
  update_request: 'Update Request',
  update_plan: 'Update Plan',
  update_diff: 'Update Applied',
  deploy_result: 'Deploy Result',
  chat_message: 'Chat',
  adoption_note: 'Adoption',
  rollback_note: 'Rollback',
  batch_operation: 'Batch Op',
  annotation: 'Note',
};

interface MemoryPanelProps {
  engineSlug: string;
  engineName: string;
  creatorSecret: string;
  onClose?: () => void;
  isOpen?: boolean;
}

export default function MemoryPanel({
  engineSlug,
  engineName,
  creatorSecret,
  onClose,
  isOpen = true,
}: MemoryPanelProps) {
  const [entries, setEntries] = useState<MemoryEntry[]>([]);
  const [stats, setStats] = useState<MemoryStats | null>(null);
  const [loading, setLoading] = useState(true);
  const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [searchQuery, setSearchQuery] = useState('');
  const [searchResults, setSearchResults] = useState<MemoryEntry[] | null>(null);
  const [filterType, setFilterType] = useState<string>('all');
  const [annotationText, setAnnotationText] = useState('');
  const [addingNote, setAddingNote] = useState(false);
  const [view, setView] = useState<'timeline' | 'decisions' | 'search'>('timeline');
  const scrollRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  const headers = {
    'x-creator-secret': creatorSecret,
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  };

  // Load entries and stats
  const loadMemory = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    setError(null);
    try {
      const typeParam = filterType !== 'all' ? `&types=${filterType}` : '';
      const [entriesRes, statsRes] = await Promise.all([
        fetch(`/api/engine-memory?slug=${engineSlug}&limit=200${typeParam}`, { headers }),
        fetch(`/api/engine-memory?slug=${engineSlug}&action=stats`, { headers }),
      ]);

      if (!entriesRes.ok || !statsRes.ok) {
        throw new Error('Failed to load memory');
      }

      const entriesData = await entriesRes.json();
      const statsData = await statsRes.json();

      setEntries(entriesData.entries || []);
      setStats(statsData);
    } catch (err: any) {
      setError(err.message);
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, [engineSlug, filterType, creatorSecret]);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (isOpen && engineSlug) {
      loadMemory();
    }
  }, [isOpen, engineSlug, loadMemory]);

  // Search
  const handleSearch = async () => {
    if (!searchQuery.trim()) {
      setSearchResults(null);
      return;
    }
    try {
      const res = await fetch(
        `/api/engine-memory?slug=${engineSlug}&action=search&q=${encodeURIComponent(searchQuery)}`,
        { headers }
      );
      const data = await res.json();
      setSearchResults(data.entries || []);
      setView('search');
    } catch (err: any) {
      setError(err.message);
    }
  };

  // Add annotation
  const handleAddAnnotation = async () => {
    if (!annotationText.trim()) return;
    setAddingNote(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/engine-memory', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers,
        body: JSON.stringify({
          slug: engineSlug,
          type: 'annotation',
          content: annotationText.trim(),
        }),
      });
      if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to add note');
      setAnnotationText('');
      await loadMemory();
    } catch (err: any) {
      setError(err.message);
    } finally {
      setAddingNote(false);
    }
  };

  // Format timestamp
  const formatTime = (ts: string) => {
    try {
      const d = new Date(ts);
      const now = new Date();
      const diffMs = now.getTime() - d.getTime();
      const diffMins = Math.floor(diffMs / 60000);
      const diffHours = Math.floor(diffMs / 3600000);
      const diffDays = Math.floor(diffMs / 86400000);

      if (diffMins < 1) return 'just now';
      if (diffMins < 60) return `${diffMins}m ago`;
      if (diffHours < 24) return `${diffHours}h ago`;
      if (diffDays < 7) return `${diffDays}d ago`;
      return d.toLocaleDateString('en-US', { month: 'short', day: 'numeric', year: d.getFullYear() !== now.getFullYear() ? 'numeric' : undefined });
    } catch {
      return ts;
    }
  };

  // Get unique types for filter
  const uniqueTypes = Array.from(new Set(entries.map(e => e.entry_type)));

  if (!isOpen) return null;

  const displayEntries = view === 'search' && searchResults ? searchResults :
    view === 'decisions' ? entries.filter(e => e.entry_type === 'design_decision') :
    entries;

  return (
    <div className="flex flex-col h-full bg-gray-950 border-l border-gray-800">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 border-b border-gray-800 bg-gray-900/50">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className="text-lg">🧠</span>
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-sm font-semibold text-white">Engine Memory</h3>
            <p className="text-xs text-gray-400">{engineName}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {stats && (
            <span className="text-xs text-gray-500">
              {stats.total_entries} entries · ~{(stats.estimated_tokens / 1000).toFixed(1)}k tokens
            </span>
          )}
          {onClose && (
            <button onClick={onClose} className="text-gray-400 hover:text-white text-lg px-1">×</button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* View tabs */}
      <div className="flex border-b border-gray-800 bg-gray-900/30">
        {(['timeline', 'decisions', 'search'] as const).map(v => (
          <button
            key={v}
            onClick={() => { setView(v); if (v !== 'search') setSearchResults(null); }}
            className={`px-4 py-2 text-xs font-medium transition-colors ${
              view === v
                ? 'text-amber-400 border-b-2 border-amber-400'
                : 'text-gray-500 hover:text-gray-300'
            }`}
          >
            {v === 'timeline' ? '📜 Timeline' : v === 'decisions' ? '⚖️ Decisions' : '🔍 Search'}
          </button>
        ))}

        {/* Type filter (timeline view only) */}
        {view === 'timeline' && (
          <select
            value={filterType}
            onChange={e => setFilterType(e.target.value)}
            className="ml-auto mr-2 bg-gray-800 text-gray-300 text-xs rounded px-2 py-1 border border-gray-700"
          >
            <option value="all">All types</option>
            {uniqueTypes.map(t => (
              <option key={t} value={t}>{TYPE_LABELS[t] || t}</option>
            ))}
          </select>
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Search bar (search view) */}
      {view === 'search' && (
        <div className="flex gap-2 p-3 border-b border-gray-800">
          <input
            type="text"
            value={searchQuery}
            onChange={e => setSearchQuery(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleSearch()}
            placeholder="Search engine memory..."
            className="flex-1 bg-gray-800 text-white text-sm rounded px-3 py-2 border border-gray-700 focus:border-amber-500 focus:outline-none"
          />
          <button
            onClick={handleSearch}
            className="bg-amber-600 hover:bg-amber-500 text-black text-sm font-medium px-4 py-2 rounded"
          >
            Search
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Stats bar */}
      {stats && stats.total_entries > 0 && view === 'timeline' && (
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 px-3 py-2 border-b border-gray-800 bg-gray-900/20">
          {Object.entries(stats.by_type).map(([type, count]) => (
            <button
              key={type}
              onClick={() => setFilterType(filterType === type ? 'all' : type)}
              className={`flex items-center gap-1 px-2 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs transition-colors ${
                filterType === type
                  ? 'bg-amber-900/50 text-amber-300 border border-amber-700'
                  : 'bg-gray-800 text-gray-400 border border-gray-700 hover:border-gray-600'
              }`}
            >
              <span>{TYPE_ICONS[type] || '📄'}</span>
              <span>{count}</span>
            </button>
          ))}
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Error */}
      {error && (
        <div className="mx-3 mt-2 p-2 bg-red-900/30 border border-red-800 rounded text-red-300 text-xs">
          {error}
          <button onClick={() => setError(null)} className="ml-2 text-red-400 hover:text-red-200">×</button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Entries */}
      <div ref={scrollRef} className="flex-1 overflow-y-auto px-3 py-2 space-y-1">
        {loading ? (
          <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
            <div className="text-gray-500 text-sm">Loading memory...</div>
          </div>
        ) : displayEntries.length === 0 ? (
          <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center py-12 text-center">
            <span className="text-3xl mb-2">🧠</span>
            <p className="text-gray-400 text-sm">
              {view === 'search' ? 'No results found' : 'No memory entries yet'}
            </p>
            <p className="text-gray-600 text-xs mt-1">
              {view === 'search'
                ? 'Try different search terms'
                : 'Memory is recorded automatically during builds and updates'}
            </p>
          </div>
        ) : (
          displayEntries.map((entry, idx) => (
            <div
              key={entry.id}
              className={`group relative pl-6 py-2 border-l-2 ${
                entry.entry_type === 'design_decision'
                  ? 'border-purple-800 bg-purple-900/10'
                  : entry.entry_type === 'deploy_result' && entry.content.includes('SUCCESS')
                  ? 'border-emerald-800'
                  : entry.entry_type === 'deploy_result' && entry.content.includes('FAILED')
                  ? 'border-red-800 bg-red-900/10'
                  : 'border-gray-800'
              } hover:bg-gray-900/50 rounded-r transition-colors`}
            >
              {/* Timeline dot */}
              <div className="absolute left-[-5px] top-3 w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-gray-700 group-hover:bg-amber-500 transition-colors" />

              {/* Header */}
              <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-1">
                <span className="text-sm">{TYPE_ICONS[entry.entry_type] || '📄'}</span>
                <span className={`text-xs font-medium ${TYPE_COLORS[entry.entry_type] || 'text-gray-400'}`}>
                  {TYPE_LABELS[entry.entry_type] || entry.entry_type}
                </span>
                <span className="text-xs text-gray-600">
                  {entry.role === 'creator' ? '👤' : entry.role === 'claude' ? '🤖' : '⚙️'}
                </span>
                <span className="text-xs text-gray-600 ml-auto">{formatTime(entry.created_at)}</span>
              </div>

              {/* Content */}
              <div className="text-sm text-gray-300 whitespace-pre-wrap break-words leading-relaxed">
                {entry.content.length > 500
                  ? entry.content.substring(0, 500) + '...'
                  : entry.content}
              </div>

              {/* Metadata badges */}
              {entry.metadata && Object.keys(entry.metadata).filter(k => !k.startsWith('_') && k !== 'event' && k !== 'timestamp' && k !== 'is_rolling_summary').length > 0 && (
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-1 mt-1">
                  {Object.entries(entry.metadata)
                    .filter(([k]) => !k.startsWith('_') && k !== 'event' && k !== 'timestamp' && k !== 'is_rolling_summary' && k !== 'seeded')
                    .slice(0, 5)
                    .map(([k, v]) => (
                      <span key={k} className="text-[10px] px-1.5 py-0.5 bg-gray-800 text-gray-500 rounded">
                        {k}: {typeof v === 'string' ? v : JSON.stringify(v)}
                      </span>
                    ))}
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          ))
        )}
      </div>

      {/* Add annotation */}
      <div className="border-t border-gray-800 p-3 bg-gray-900/30">
        <div className="flex gap-2">
          <input
            type="text"
            value={annotationText}
            onChange={e => setAnnotationText(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey && handleAddAnnotation()}
            placeholder="Add a design note or annotation..."
            className="flex-1 bg-gray-800 text-white text-sm rounded px-3 py-2 border border-gray-700 focus:border-amber-500 focus:outline-none"
            disabled={addingNote}
          />
          <button
            onClick={handleAddAnnotation}
            disabled={addingNote || !annotationText.trim()}
            className="bg-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-600 disabled:opacity-40 text-white text-sm px-3 py-2 rounded transition-colors"
          >
            {addingNote ? '...' : '📝 Add'}
          </button>
        </div>
        <p className="text-[10px] text-gray-600 mt-1">
          Notes are stored permanently and injected into Claude&apos;s context during future updates
        </p>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

## File: `lib/adopt.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Engine Adoption
// Registers existing hand-built engines into HEB management
// Scans → audits → registers → enables fleet management
// ============================================================

import { scanRepo } from './repo-scanner';
import { runGovernanceAudit } from './governance-audit';
import { createEngine, updateEngine, getEngine } from './db';
import type { AdoptRequest, EngineRecord, RepoScanResult, GovernanceAuditResult, StreamEvent } from './types-v3';

export interface AdoptResult {
  engine: EngineRecord;
  scan: RepoScanResult;
  audit: GovernanceAuditResult;
}

export async function adoptEngine(
  request: AdoptRequest,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<AdoptResult> {
  const emit = (phase: string, status: StreamEvent['status'], message: string, data?: any) => {
    onEvent?.({ phase, status, message, data });
  };

  // Check if already adopted
  const existing = await getEngine(request.slug);
  if (existing) {
    throw new Error(`Engine "${request.slug}" is already registered in HEB. Use update-engine instead.`);
  }

  // Step 1: Scan the repo
  emit('scan', 'running', `Scanning repo: ${request.repoUrl}`);
  let scan: RepoScanResult;
  try {
    scan = await scanRepo(request.repoUrl);
    emit('scan', 'done', `Scan complete: ${scan.fileCount} files, framework: ${scan.framework}`, {
      fileCount: scan.fileCount,
      framework: scan.framework,
      routes: scan.routes,
      apiRoutes: scan.apiRoutes,
      governanceScore: scan.governanceScore,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    emit('scan', 'error', `Scan failed: ${err.message}`);
    throw err;
  }

  // Step 2: Run governance audit
  emit('audit', 'running', 'Running QB governance audit...');
  let audit: GovernanceAuditResult;
  try {
    audit = await runGovernanceAudit(request.slug, scan);
    emit('audit', 'done', `Governance score: ${audit.score}/${audit.maxScore} (Grade: ${audit.grade})`, {
      score: audit.score,
      grade: audit.grade,
      passed: audit.passed.length,
      failed: audit.failed.length,
      warnings: audit.warnings.length,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    emit('audit', 'error', `Audit failed: ${err.message}`);
    throw err;
  }

  // Step 3: Detect Vercel project
  emit('register', 'running', 'Detecting Vercel project...');
  let vercelUrl = '';
  if (request.vercelProjectId) {
    vercelUrl = `https://vercel.com/project/${request.vercelProjectId}`;
  } else {
    // Try to infer from domain
    vercelUrl = `https://${request.domain}`;
  }

  // Step 4: Register in database
  emit('register', 'running', `Registering ${request.engineName} in HEB fleet...`);
  const engine: Partial<EngineRecord> = {
    slug: request.slug,
    name: request.engineName,
    description: `Adopted engine: ${request.engineName}. Framework: ${scan.framework}. Routes: ${scan.routes.join(', ')}`,
    repo_url: request.repoUrl,
    vercel_url: vercelUrl,
    domain: request.domain,
    status: 'live',
    adopted: true,
    template_id: null,
    dependencies: [],
    governance_score: audit.score,
    build_log: [
      { timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), phase: 'adopt', status: 'done', message: `Adopted from ${request.repoUrl}` },
      { timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), phase: 'scan', status: 'done', message: `${scan.fileCount} files, ${scan.framework}` },
      { timestamp: new Date().toISOString(), phase: 'audit', status: 'done', message: `Score: ${audit.score}/${audit.maxScore} (${audit.grade})` },
    ],
  };

  try {
    await createEngine(engine);
    emit('register', 'done', `${request.engineName} registered successfully`, {
      slug: request.slug,
      domain: request.domain,
      governanceScore: audit.score,
      grade: audit.grade,
    });
  } catch (err: any) {
    emit('register', 'error', `Registration failed: ${err.message}`);
    throw err;
  }

  // Step 5: Summary with recommendations
  if (audit.failed.length > 0 || audit.warnings.length > 0) {
    emit('recommendations', 'done',
      `Governance gaps found: ${audit.failed.length} critical, ${audit.warnings.length} warnings. ` +
      `Run "audit-engine" for details or use batch operations to fix.`,
      { recommendations: audit.recommendations }
    );
  }

  const fullEngine = await getEngine(request.slug);
  return { engine: fullEngine!, scan, audit };
}

// === Bulk Adopt ===
// Adopt multiple engines at once (e.g., all existing Hive engines)
export async function bulkAdopt(
  requests: AdoptRequest[],
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<AdoptResult[]> {
  const results: AdoptResult[] = [];

  for (const req of requests) {
    try {
      onEvent?.({ phase: 'bulk-adopt', status: 'running', message: `Adopting ${req.engineName}...` });
      const result = await adoptEngine(req, onEvent);
      results.push(result);
      onEvent?.({ phase: 'bulk-adopt', status: 'done', message: `${req.engineName} adopted (${result.audit.grade})` });
    } catch (err: any) {
      onEvent?.({ phase: 'bulk-adopt', status: 'error', message: `Failed to adopt ${req.engineName}: ${err.message}` });
    }
  }

  return results;
}

// === Pre-built adoption configs for existing Hive engines ===
export const HIVE_ENGINES: AdoptRequest[] = [
  {
    slug: 'hive-clarity',
    engineName: 'HiveClarity',
    repoUrl: 'https://github.com/saggarsonny-boop/hive-clarity',
    domain: 'hiveclarity.hive.baby',
  },
  {
    slug: 'hive-clock',
```

## File: `lib/auth.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Creator-Only Auth Gate
// All HEB routes and pages are gated behind HEB_CREATOR_SECRET
// Unauthenticated requests get 404 (not 401/403 — no info leak)
// ============================================================

import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';

const NOT_FOUND = NextResponse.json({ error: 'Not Found' }, { status: 404 });

/**
 * Validates creator auth from request.
 * Checks: Authorization header, x-heb-secret header, or ?secret= query param.
 * Returns null if valid, or a 404 response if invalid.
 */
export function requireCreator(req: NextRequest): NextResponse | null {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) {
    // If no secret is configured, deny all access
    console.error('[HEB Auth] HEB_CREATOR_SECRET not set — denying access');
    return NOT_FOUND;
  }

  // Check Authorization: Bearer <secret>
  const authHeader = req.headers.get('authorization');
  if (authHeader) {
    const token = authHeader.replace(/^Bearer\s+/i, '');
    if (token === secret) return null;
  }

  // Check x-heb-secret header
  const headerSecret = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret');
  if (headerSecret === secret) return null;

  // Check query param ?secret=
  const url = new URL(req.url);
  const querySecret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
  if (querySecret === secret) return null;

  // Check cookie (for UI pages)
  const cookieSecret = req.cookies.get('heb_creator')?.value;
  if (cookieSecret === secret) return null;

  return NOT_FOUND;
}

/**
 * Client-side: check if the creator secret cookie is set.
 * Used by UI pages to gate rendering.
 */
export function isCreatorAuthenticated(): boolean {
  if (typeof document === 'undefined') return false;
  return document.cookie.includes('heb_creator=');
}

/**
 * Client-side: set the creator cookie.
 */
export function setCreatorCookie(secret: string): void {
  document.cookie = `heb_creator=${secret}; path=/; max-age=86400; SameSite=Strict; Secure`;
}

/**
 * Middleware-style auth check for page routes.
 * Returns the secret if valid, null otherwise.
 */
export function getCreatorSecret(req: NextRequest): string | null {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return null;

  const cookieSecret = req.cookies.get('heb_creator')?.value;
  if (cookieSecret === secret) return secret;

  const url = new URL(req.url);
  const querySecret = url.searchParams.get('secret');
  if (querySecret === secret) return secret;

  return null;
}

```

## File: `lib/db.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Database Layer (Neon PostgreSQL)
// All tables, migrations, and query helpers
// ============================================================

import { neon } from '@neondatabase/serverless';
import type {
  EngineRecord, DeployOutcome, GovernanceAuditResult,
  EngineTemplate, FoundrySubmission, MonetizationConfig,
  ScalingConfig, StagingDeploy, BuildLogEntry,
} from './types-v3';

function getDb() {
  const url = process.env.DATABASE_URL;
  if (!url) throw new Error('DATABASE_URL not set');
  return neon(url);
}

// === Schema Initialization ===
export async function initSchema(): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_engines (
      slug TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      name TEXT NOT NULL,
      description TEXT DEFAULT '',
      repo_url TEXT DEFAULT '',
      vercel_url TEXT DEFAULT '',
      domain TEXT DEFAULT '',
      status TEXT DEFAULT 'building',
      adopted BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
      template_id TEXT,
      dependencies JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      governance_score INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      monetization_model TEXT,
      scaling_config JSONB,
      build_log JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_deploy_outcomes (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      engine_slug TEXT NOT NULL,
      timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      success BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
      build_duration INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      error_type TEXT,
      error_message TEXT,
      files_changed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      generation_prompt TEXT DEFAULT '',
      code_patterns JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      framework TEXT DEFAULT 'nextjs',
      node_version TEXT
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_governance_audits (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      engine_slug TEXT NOT NULL,
      score INTEGER NOT NULL,
      max_score INTEGER DEFAULT 100,
      grade TEXT DEFAULT 'F',
      passed JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      failed JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      warnings JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      recommendations JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_templates (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      name TEXT NOT NULL,
      description TEXT DEFAULT '',
      source_slug TEXT DEFAULT '',
      category TEXT DEFAULT 'utility',
      files JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      variables JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      governance_preset JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_staging (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      engine_slug TEXT NOT NULL,
      branch TEXT DEFAULT 'dev',
      staging_domain TEXT DEFAULT '',
      vercel_deploy_id TEXT DEFAULT '',
      status TEXT DEFAULT 'deploying',
      url TEXT DEFAULT '',
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      expires_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT (NOW() + INTERVAL '24 hours')
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_foundry_submissions (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      developer_name TEXT DEFAULT '',
      developer_email TEXT NOT NULL,
      engine_name TEXT NOT NULL,
      slug TEXT NOT NULL,
      repo_url TEXT NOT NULL,
      description TEXT DEFAULT '',
      category TEXT DEFAULT 'utility',
      status TEXT DEFAULT 'pending',
      governance_audit JSONB,
      submitted_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      reviewed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      deployed_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
      review_notes TEXT
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_monetization (
      engine_slug TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      model TEXT NOT NULL,
      stripe_product_id TEXT,
      stripe_price_ids JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
      support_tiers JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      webhook_secret TEXT,
      trial_days INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_scaling (
      engine_slug TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      max_concurrent INTEGER DEFAULT 10,
      function_timeout INTEGER DEFAULT 30,
      regions JSONB DEFAULT '["iad1"]',
      edge_runtime BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
      cron_jobs JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
      updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS heb_dependencies (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
      from_slug TEXT NOT NULL,
      to_slug TEXT NOT NULL,
      dep_type TEXT DEFAULT 'api',
      env_var TEXT DEFAULT '',
      description TEXT DEFAULT '',
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      UNIQUE(from_slug, to_slug)
    )
  `;
}

// === Engine CRUD ===
export async function createEngine(engine: Partial<EngineRecord>): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initSchema();
  await sql`
    INSERT INTO heb_engines (slug, name, description, repo_url, vercel_url, domain, status, adopted, template_id, dependencies, governance_score, monetization_model, scaling_config, build_log)
    VALUES (
      ${engine.slug!}, ${engine.name || ''}, ${engine.description || ''},
      ${engine.repo_url || ''}, ${engine.vercel_url || ''}, ${engine.domain || ''},
      ${engine.status || 'building'}, ${engine.adopted || false},
      ${engine.template_id || null}, ${JSON.stringify(engine.dependencies || [])},
      ${engine.governance_score || 0}, ${engine.monetization_model || null},
      ${engine.scaling_config ? JSON.stringify(engine.scaling_config) : null},
      ${JSON.stringify(engine.build_log || [])}
    )
    ON CONFLICT (slug) DO UPDATE SET
      name = EXCLUDED.name,
      description = EXCLUDED.description,
      repo_url = EXCLUDED.repo_url,
      vercel_url = EXCLUDED.vercel_url,
      domain = EXCLUDED.domain,
      status = EXCLUDED.status,
      adopted = EXCLUDED.adopted,
      governance_score = EXCLUDED.governance_score,
      updated_at = NOW()
  `;
}

export async function getEngine(slug: string): Promise<EngineRecord | null> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initSchema();
  const rows = await sql`SELECT * FROM heb_engines WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  if (rows.length === 0) return null;
  return rowToEngine(rows[0]);
}

export async function getAllEngines(): Promise<EngineRecord[]> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initSchema();
  const rows = await sql`SELECT * FROM heb_engines ORDER BY created_at DESC`;
  return rows.map(rowToEngine);
}

export async function updateEngine(slug: string, updates: Partial<EngineRecord>): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const sets: string[] = [];
  if (updates.status !== undefined) {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_engines SET status = ${updates.status}, updated_at = NOW() WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  }
  if (updates.governance_score !== undefined) {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_engines SET governance_score = ${updates.governance_score}, updated_at = NOW() WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  }
  if (updates.repo_url !== undefined) {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_engines SET repo_url = ${updates.repo_url}, updated_at = NOW() WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  }
  if (updates.vercel_url !== undefined) {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_engines SET vercel_url = ${updates.vercel_url}, updated_at = NOW() WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  }
  if (updates.domain !== undefined) {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_engines SET domain = ${updates.domain}, updated_at = NOW() WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  }
  if (updates.monetization_model !== undefined) {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_engines SET monetization_model = ${updates.monetization_model}, updated_at = NOW() WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  }
  if (updates.build_log !== undefined) {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_engines SET build_log = ${JSON.stringify(updates.build_log)}, updated_at = NOW() WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  }
}

export async function appendBuildLog(slug: string, entry: BuildLogEntry): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await sql`
    UPDATE heb_engines
    SET build_log = COALESCE(build_log, '[]'::jsonb) || ${JSON.stringify(entry)}::jsonb,
        updated_at = NOW()
    WHERE slug = ${slug}
  `;
}

export async function deleteEngine(slug: string): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await sql`DELETE FROM heb_engines WHERE slug = ${slug}`;
  await sql`DELETE FROM heb_deploy_outcomes WHERE engine_slug = ${slug}`;
  await sql`DELETE FROM heb_governance_audits WHERE engine_slug = ${slug}`;
  await sql`DELETE FROM heb_staging WHERE engine_slug = ${slug}`;
  await sql`DELETE FROM heb_dependencies WHERE from_slug = ${slug} OR to_slug = ${slug}`;
  await sql`DELETE FROM heb_monetization WHERE engine_slug = ${slug}`;
  await sql`DELETE FROM heb_scaling WHERE engine_slug = ${slug}`;
}

// === Deploy Outcomes ===
export async function recordDeployOutcome(outcome: DeployOutcome): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await sql`
    INSERT INTO heb_deploy_outcomes (id, engine_slug, success, build_duration, error_type, error_message, files_changed, generation_prompt, code_patterns, framework, node_version)
    VALUES (${outcome.id}, ${outcome.engineSlug}, ${outcome.success}, ${outcome.buildDuration},
      ${outcome.errorType}, ${outcome.errorMessage}, ${outcome.filesChanged},
      ${outcome.generationPrompt}, ${JSON.stringify(outcome.codePatterns)},
      ${outcome.framework}, ${outcome.nodeVersion})
  `;
}

export async function getDeployOutcomes(slug?: string, limit = 100): Promise<DeployOutcome[]> {
  const sql = getDb();
  if (slug) {
    const rows = await sql`SELECT * FROM heb_deploy_outcomes WHERE engine_slug = ${slug} ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT ${limit}`;
    return rows.map(rowToOutcome);
  }
  const rows = await sql`SELECT * FROM heb_deploy_outcomes ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT ${limit}`;
  return rows.map(rowToOutcome);
}

// === Governance Audits ===
export async function recordAudit(audit: GovernanceAuditResult): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const id = `audit-${audit.engineSlug}-${Date.now()}`;
  await sql`
    INSERT INTO heb_governance_audits (id, engine_slug, score, max_score, grade, passed, failed, warnings, recommendations)
    VALUES (${id}, ${audit.engineSlug}, ${audit.score}, ${audit.maxScore}, ${audit.grade},
      ${JSON.stringify(audit.passed)}, ${JSON.stringify(audit.failed)},
      ${JSON.stringify(audit.warnings)}, ${JSON.stringify(audit.recommendations)})
  `;
}

export async function getLatestAudit(slug: string): Promise<GovernanceAuditResult | null> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const rows = await sql`SELECT * FROM heb_governance_audits WHERE engine_slug = ${slug} ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT 1`;
  if (rows.length === 0) return null;
  return rowToAudit(rows[0]);
}

export async function getAuditHistory(slug: string, limit = 20): Promise<GovernanceAuditResult[]> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const rows = await sql`SELECT * FROM heb_governance_audits WHERE engine_slug = ${slug} ORDER BY timestamp DESC LIMIT ${limit}`;
  return rows.map(rowToAudit);
}

// === Templates ===

    VALUES (${template.id}, ${template.name}, ${template.description}, ${template.sourceSlug},
      ${template.category}, ${JSON.stringify(template.files)}, ${JSON.stringify(template.variables)},
      ${JSON.stringify(template.governancePreset)})
    ON CONFLICT (id) DO UPDATE SET
      name = EXCLUDED.name, description = EXCLUDED.description,
      files = EXCLUDED.files, variables = EXCLUDED.variables
  `;
}

}

  const sql = getDb();
  await sql`
    INSERT INTO heb_staging (id, engine_slug, branch, staging_domain, vercel_deploy_id, status, url, expires_at)
    VALUES (${staging.id}, ${staging.engineSlug}, ${staging.branch}, ${staging.stagingDomain},

  `;
}

export async function updateStagingStatus(id: string, status: string, deployId?: string): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  if (deployId) {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_staging SET status = ${status}, vercel_deploy_id = ${deployId} WHERE id = ${id}`;
  } else {
    await sql`UPDATE heb_staging SET status = ${status} WHERE id = ${id}`;
  }
}

export async function getActiveStaging(slug: string): Promise<StagingDeploy | null> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const rows = await sql`
    SELECT * FROM heb_staging
    WHERE engine_slug = ${slug} AND status IN ('deploying', 'ready') AND expires_at > NOW()
    ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 1
  `;
  if (rows.length === 0) return null;
  return rowToStaging(rows[0]);
}

// === Dependencies ===
export async function addDependency(from: string, to: string, type: string, envVar: string, desc: string): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const id = `dep-${from}-${to}`;
  await sql`
    INSERT INTO heb_dependencies (id, from_slug, to_slug, dep_type, env_var, description)
    VALUES (${id}, ${from}, ${to}, ${type}, ${envVar}, ${desc})
    ON CONFLICT (from_slug, to_slug) DO UPDATE SET
      dep_type = EXCLUDED.dep_type, env_var = EXCLUDED.env_var, description = EXCLUDED.description
  `;
}

export async function removeDependency(from: string, to: string): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await sql`DELETE FROM heb_dependencies WHERE from_slug = ${from} AND to_slug = ${to}`;
}

export async function getDependencies(slug: string): Promise<any[]> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const rows = await sql`SELECT * FROM heb_dependencies WHERE from_slug = ${slug} OR to_slug = ${slug}`;
  return rows;
}

export async function getAllDependencies(): Promise<any[]> {
  const sql = getDb();
  return await sql`SELECT * FROM heb_dependencies ORDER BY from_slug`;
}

// === Row Mappers ===
function rowToEngine(r: any): EngineRecord {
  return {
    slug: r.slug,
    name: r.name,
    description: r.description || '',
    repo_url: r.repo_url || '',
    vercel_url: r.vercel_url || '',
    domain: r.domain || '',
    status: r.status || 'building',
    adopted: r.adopted || false,
    template_id: r.template_id || null,
    dependencies: typeof r.dependencies === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.dependencies) : (r.dependencies || []),
    governance_score: r.governance_score || 0,
    monetization_model: r.monetization_model || null,
    scaling_config: r.scaling_config ? (typeof r.scaling_config === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.scaling_config) : r.scaling_config) : null,
    build_log: typeof r.build_log === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.build_log) : (r.build_log || []),
    created_at: r.created_at?.toISOString?.() || r.created_at || '',
    updated_at: r.updated_at?.toISOString?.() || r.updated_at || '',
  };
}

function rowToOutcome(r: any): DeployOutcome {
  return {
    id: r.id,
    engineSlug: r.engine_slug,
    timestamp: r.timestamp?.toISOString?.() || r.timestamp || '',
    success: r.success,
    buildDuration: r.build_duration || 0,
    errorType: r.error_type || null,
    errorMessage: r.error_message || null,
    filesChanged: r.files_changed || 0,
    generationPrompt: r.generation_prompt || '',
    codePatterns: typeof r.code_patterns === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.code_patterns) : (r.code_patterns || []),
    framework: r.framework || 'nextjs',
    nodeVersion: r.node_version || null,
  };
}

function rowToAudit(r: any): GovernanceAuditResult {
  return {
    engineSlug: r.engine_slug,
    score: r.score,
    maxScore: r.max_score || 100,
    grade: r.grade || 'F',
    passed: typeof r.passed === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.passed) : (r.passed || []),
    failed: typeof r.failed === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.failed) : (r.failed || []),
    warnings: typeof r.warnings === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.warnings) : (r.warnings || []),
    recommendations: typeof r.recommendations === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.recommendations) : (r.recommendations || []),
    timestamp: r.timestamp?.toISOString?.() || r.timestamp || '',
  };
}

function rowToTemplate(r: any): EngineTemplate {
  return {
    id: r.id,
    name: r.name,
    description: r.description || '',
    sourceSlug: r.source_slug || '',
    category: r.category || 'utility',
    files: typeof r.files === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.files) : (r.files || []),
    variables: typeof r.variables === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.variables) : (r.variables || []),
    governancePreset: typeof r.governance_preset === 'string' ? JSON.parse(r.governance_preset) : (r.governance_preset || {}),
    created_at: r.created_at?.toISOString?.() || r.created_at || '',
  };
}

    submittedAt: r.submitted_at?.toISOString?.() || r.submitted_at || '',

  };
```

## File: `lib/deploy-learner.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Deploy Learner (Self-Improving Factory)
// Analyzes deploy outcomes to identify success/failure patterns
// and improve code generation prompts over time
// ============================================================

import { getDeployOutcomes, recordDeployOutcome } from './db';
import type { DeployOutcome, DeployInsight, LearnerReport, StreamEvent } from './types-v3';
import { v4 as uuid } from 'uuid';

// === Record a deploy outcome ===
export async function recordOutcome(
  engineSlug: string,
  success: boolean,
  buildDuration: number,
  filesChanged: number,
  generationPrompt: string,
  errorType?: string,
  errorMessage?: string,
): Promise<DeployOutcome> {
  const patterns = extractCodePatterns(generationPrompt, errorMessage);

  const outcome: DeployOutcome = {
    id: `do-${uuid().slice(0, 8)}`,
    engineSlug,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    success,
    buildDuration,
    errorType: errorType || null,
    errorMessage: errorMessage || null,
    filesChanged,
    generationPrompt,
    codePatterns: patterns,
    framework: 'nextjs',
    nodeVersion: process.version || null,
  };

  await recordDeployOutcome(outcome);
  return outcome;
}

// === Extract code patterns from prompts and errors ===
function extractCodePatterns(prompt: string, error?: string): string[] {
  const patterns: string[] = [];
  const lower = prompt.toLowerCase();

  // Feature patterns
  if (lower.includes('api route') || lower.includes('api/')) patterns.push('api-route');
  if (lower.includes('database') || lower.includes('neon') || lower.includes('postgres')) patterns.push('database');
  if (lower.includes('stripe') || lower.includes('payment')) patterns.push('stripe');
  if (lower.includes('auth') || lower.includes('login')) patterns.push('auth');
  if (lower.includes('claude') || lower.includes('anthropic') || lower.includes('ai')) patterns.push('ai-integration');
  if (lower.includes('tailwind') || lower.includes('css') || lower.includes('style')) patterns.push('styling');
  if (lower.includes('component') || lower.includes('react')) patterns.push('component');
  if (lower.includes('form') || lower.includes('input')) patterns.push('form');
  if (lower.includes('chart') || lower.includes('graph') || lower.includes('visual')) patterns.push('visualization');
  if (lower.includes('email') || lower.includes('resend')) patterns.push('email');
  if (lower.includes('cron') || lower.includes('schedule')) patterns.push('scheduled');
  if (lower.includes('webhook')) patterns.push('webhook');
  if (lower.includes('multilingual') || lower.includes('i18n') || lower.includes('language')) patterns.push('i18n');

  // Error patterns
  if (error) {
    const errLower = error.toLowerCase();
    if (errLower.includes('module not found') || errLower.includes('cannot find module')) patterns.push('err:module-not-found');
    if (errLower.includes('type error') || errLower.includes('typescript')) patterns.push('err:typescript');
    if (errLower.includes('syntax error')) patterns.push('err:syntax');
    if (errLower.includes('build failed')) patterns.push('err:build-failed');
    if (errLower.includes('timeout')) patterns.push('err:timeout');
    if (errLower.includes('memory') || errLower.includes('heap')) patterns.push('err:memory');
    if (errLower.includes('env') || errLower.includes('environment')) patterns.push('err:env-var');
    if (errLower.includes('import')) patterns.push('err:import');
    if (errLower.includes('eslint') || errLower.includes('lint')) patterns.push('err:lint');
  }

  return patterns;
}

// === Analyze patterns and generate insights ===
export async function generateInsights(minSampleSize = 3): Promise<DeployInsight[]> {
  const outcomes = await getDeployOutcomes(undefined, 500);
  if (outcomes.length < minSampleSize) return [];

  // Group by pattern
  const patternStats = new Map<string, { successes: number; failures: number; totalDuration: number; count: number }>();

  for (const outcome of outcomes) {
    for (const pattern of outcome.codePatterns) {
      const existing = patternStats.get(pattern) || { successes: 0, failures: 0, totalDuration: 0, count: 0 };
      existing.count++;
      existing.totalDuration += outcome.buildDuration;
      if (outcome.success) existing.successes++;
      else existing.failures++;
      patternStats.set(pattern, existing);
    }
  }

  const insights: DeployInsight[] = [];

  for (const [pattern, stats] of patternStats) {
    if (stats.count < minSampleSize) continue;

    const successRate = stats.successes / stats.count;
    const avgDuration = stats.totalDuration / stats.count;

    let category: DeployInsight['category'];
    let recommendation: string;

    if (pattern.startsWith('err:')) {
      category = 'failure-pattern';
      recommendation = getErrorRecommendation(pattern, successRate);
    } else if (successRate >= 0.8) {
      category = 'success-pattern';
      recommendation = `Pattern "${pattern}" has ${Math.round(successRate * 100)}% success rate. Keep using this approach.`;
    } else if (successRate < 0.5) {
      category = 'failure-pattern';
      recommendation = `Pattern "${pattern}" has only ${Math.round(successRate * 100)}% success rate. Consider alternative approaches.`;
    } else {
      category = 'optimization';
      recommendation = `Pattern "${pattern}" at ${Math.round(successRate * 100)}% — review generation prompts for consistency.`;
    }

    insights.push({
      pattern,
      category,
      successRate: Math.round(successRate * 100) / 100,
      avgBuildDuration: Math.round(avgDuration),
      recommendation,
      sampleSize: stats.count,
      confidence: Math.min(1, stats.count / 20), // Confidence grows with sample size, max at 20
    });
  }

  // Sort by impact (failure patterns first, then by sample size)
  insights.sort((a, b) => {
    if (a.category === 'failure-pattern' && b.category !== 'failure-pattern') return -1;
    if (a.category !== 'failure-pattern' && b.category === 'failure-pattern') return 1;
    return b.sampleSize - a.sampleSize;
  });

  return insights;
}

function getErrorRecommendation(pattern: string, successRate: number): string {
  const recommendations: Record<string, string> = {
    'err:module-not-found': 'Ensure all imports reference files that exist in the generated codebase. Add import validation to the generation step.',
    'err:typescript': 'TypeScript errors are common in generated code. Add explicit type annotations and avoid using "any". Consider generating .d.ts files.',
    'err:syntax': 'Syntax errors suggest malformed generated code. Add JSON validation for multi-file outputs and ensure Claude returns complete files.',
    'err:build-failed': 'Build failures may indicate missing dependencies or config issues. Ensure package.json includes all required deps.',
    'err:timeout': 'Build timeouts suggest heavy computation or infinite loops. Set explicit timeouts in API routes and avoid synchronous operations.',
    'err:memory': 'Memory issues often come from large imports or unbounded data structures. Use dynamic imports and pagination.',
    'err:env-var': 'Missing environment variables cause runtime crashes. Generate .env.example files and validate env vars at startup.',
    'err:import': 'Import errors suggest wrong paths or missing exports. Use relative imports and ensure all exports are named.',
    'err:lint': 'ESLint errors can block builds. Either fix lint issues in generation or configure next.config to ignore ESLint during builds.',
  };

  return recommendations[pattern] || `Error pattern "${pattern}" detected in ${Math.round((1 - successRate) * 100)}% of deploys.`;
}

// === Generate full learner report ===
export async function generateLearnerReport(): Promise<LearnerReport> {
  const outcomes = await getDeployOutcomes(undefined, 500);
  const insights = await generateInsights();

  const totalDeploys = outcomes.length;
  const successCount = outcomes.filter(o => o.success).length;
  const successRate = totalDeploys > 0 ? successCount / totalDeploys : 0;
  const avgDuration = totalDeploys > 0
    ? outcomes.reduce((sum, o) => sum + o.buildDuration, 0) / totalDeploys
    : 0;

  return {
    totalDeploys,
    successRate: Math.round(successRate * 100) / 100,
    avgBuildDuration: Math.round(avgDuration),
    topFailurePatterns: insights.filter(i => i.category === 'failure-pattern').slice(0, 5),
    topSuccessPatterns: insights.filter(i => i.category === 'success-pattern').slice(0, 5),
    optimizations: insights.filter(i => i.category === 'optimization').slice(0, 5),
    generatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
  };
}

// === Generate improved system prompt based on learnings ===
export async function generateImprovedPromptHints(): Promise<string[]> {
  const insights = await generateInsights(5);
  const hints: string[] = [];

  for (const insight of insights) {
    if (insight.category === 'failure-pattern' && insight.confidence > 0.5) {
      hints.push(`AVOID: ${insight.recommendation}`);
    }
    if (insight.category === 'success-pattern' && insight.confidence > 0.5) {
      hints.push(`PREFER: ${insight.recommendation}`);
    }
  }

  // Add general learnings
  const outcomes = await getDeployOutcomes(undefined, 100);
  const recentFailures = outcomes.filter(o => !o.success).slice(0, 10);

  if (recentFailures.length > 0) {
    const commonErrors = new Map<string, number>();
    for (const f of recentFailures) {
      if (f.errorType) {
        commonErrors.set(f.errorType, (commonErrors.get(f.errorType) || 0) + 1);
      }
    }
    for (const [error, count] of commonErrors) {
      if (count >= 3) {
        hints.push(`RECENT ISSUE (${count}x): ${error} — address this in generated code`);
      }
    }
  }

  return hints;
}
```

## File: `lib/diff-engine.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Diff Engine
// Generates targeted code patches via Claude for existing engines
// Instead of regenerating everything, produces surgical updates
// ============================================================

import Anthropic from '@anthropic-ai/sdk';
import { fetchRepoFiles, scanRepo } from './repo-scanner';
import { runGovernanceAudit } from './governance-audit';
import { getEngine } from './db';
import type { DiffPatch, UpdatePlan, UpdateRequest, StreamEvent, RepoScanResult } from './types-v3';

function getAnthropic(): Anthropic {
  const key = process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY;
  if (!key) throw new Error('ANTHROPIC_API_KEY not set');
  return new Anthropic({ apiKey: key });
}

// === Generate Update Plan ===
export async function generateUpdatePlan(
  request: UpdateRequest,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<UpdatePlan> {
  const emit = (phase: string, status: StreamEvent['status'], message: string, data?: any) => {
    onEvent?.({ phase, status, message, data });
  };

  // Get engine record
  const engine = await getEngine(request.slug);
  if (!engine) throw new Error(`Engine "${request.slug}" not found. Adopt it first.`);

  // Scan current repo state
  emit('scan', 'running', `Scanning current state of ${engine.name}...`);
  const scan = await scanRepo(engine.repo_url);
  emit('scan', 'done', `Found ${scan.fileCount} files, ${scan.routes.length} routes`);

  // Fetch relevant source files for context
  emit('analyze', 'running', 'Fetching source files for analysis...');
  const relevantPaths = identifyRelevantFiles(scan, request.instruction);
  const sourceFiles = await fetchRepoFiles(engine.repo_url, relevantPaths);
  emit('analyze', 'done', `Loaded ${sourceFiles.size} files for context`);

  // Generate patches via Claude
  emit('generate', 'running', 'Generating targeted patches via Claude...');
  const patches = await generatePatches(engine.name, request.instruction, scan, sourceFiles);
  emit('generate', 'done', `Generated ${patches.length} patches`);

  // Run governance check on proposed changes
  emit('governance', 'running', 'Checking governance compliance of proposed changes...');
  const audit = await runGovernanceAudit(request.slug, scan);
  emit('governance', 'done', `Governance: ${audit.grade} (${audit.score}/${audit.maxScore})`);

  // Assess risk
  const risk = assessRisk(patches, scan);

  const plan: UpdatePlan = {
    engineSlug: request.slug,
    description: request.instruction,
    patches,
    governanceCheck: audit,
    estimatedRisk: risk,
    affectedRoutes: findAffectedRoutes(patches, scan),
    requiresStagingVerification: risk !== 'low' || patches.some(p => p.path.includes('api/')),
  };

  emit('plan', 'done', `Update plan ready: ${patches.length} patches, risk: ${risk}`, {
    patchCount: patches.length,
    risk,
    affectedRoutes: plan.affectedRoutes,
    requiresStaging: plan.requiresStagingVerification,
  });

  return plan;
}

// === Identify files relevant to the update request ===
function identifyRelevantFiles(scan: RepoScanResult, instruction: string): string[] {
  const files: Set<string> = new Set();
  const lower = instruction.toLowerCase();

  // Always include config files
  files.add('package.json');
  files.add('next.config.js');
  files.add('next.config.mjs');
  files.add('next.config.ts');
  files.add('tailwind.config.ts');
  files.add('tailwind.config.js');

  // Include layout and main page
  for (const f of scan.fileTree) {
    if (f.path.match(/^app\/layout\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/)) files.add(f.path);
    if (f.path.match(/^app\/page\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/)) files.add(f.path);
    if (f.path.match(/^app\/globals\.css$/)) files.add(f.path);
  }

  // Keyword-based relevance
  const keywords: Record<string, string[]> = {
    'api': ['app/api/'],
    'route': ['app/api/'],
    'style': ['globals.css', 'tailwind'],
    'css': ['globals.css', 'tailwind'],
    'dark': ['globals.css', 'tailwind', 'layout'],
    'theme': ['globals.css', 'tailwind', 'layout'],
    'ribbon': ['LanguageSelector', 'i18n'],
    'language': ['LanguageSelector', 'i18n'],
    'multilingual': ['LanguageSelector', 'i18n'],
    'auth': ['auth', 'middleware'],
    'login': ['auth', 'login'],
    'database': ['lib/db', 'lib/store', 'prisma'],
    'stripe': ['stripe', 'payment', 'pricing'],
    'component': ['components/'],
    'header': ['Header', 'Nav', 'layout'],
    'footer': ['Footer', 'layout'],
    'first visit': ['FirstVisit'],
    'demo': ['AutoDemo'],
    'onboarding': ['FirstVisit', 'AutoDemo'],
  };

  for (const [keyword, patterns] of Object.entries(keywords)) {
    if (lower.includes(keyword)) {
      for (const f of scan.fileTree) {
        for (const pattern of patterns) {
          if (f.path.toLowerCase().includes(pattern.toLowerCase())) {
            files.add(f.path);
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }

  // If nothing specific matched, include all components and API routes
  if (files.size <= 5) {
    for (const comp of scan.components) files.add(comp);
    for (const f of scan.fileTree) {
      if (f.path.match(/^app\/api\/.*\/route\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/)) files.add(f.path);
    }
  }

  // Cap at 30 files to stay within context limits
  return Array.from(files).slice(0, 30);
}

// === Generate patches via Claude ===
async function generatePatches(
  engineName: string,
  instruction: string,
  scan: RepoScanResult,
  sourceFiles: Map<string, string>
): Promise<DiffPatch[]> {
  const client = getAnthropic();

  const fileContext = Array.from(sourceFiles.entries())
    .map(([path, content]) => `=== ${path} ===\n${content}`)
    .join('\n\n');

  const prompt = `You are HEB 3.0's diff engine. You generate surgical code patches for existing Hive engines.

ENGINE: ${engineName}
FRAMEWORK: ${scan.framework} ${scan.frameworkVersion || ''}
ROUTES: ${scan.routes.join(', ')}
API ROUTES: ${scan.apiRoutes.join(', ')}
COMPONENTS: ${scan.components.join(', ')}

CURRENT SOURCE FILES:
${fileContext}

REQUESTED CHANGE:
${instruction}

Generate a JSON array of patches. Each patch has:
- "path": file path (relative to repo root)
- "action": "create" | "modify" | "delete"
- "content": full file content for create/modify (COMPLETE file, not a diff)
- "reason": why this change is needed

Rules:
1. For "modify": provide the COMPLETE new file content, not a diff
2. Preserve existing functionality unless explicitly asked to change it
3. Follow Next.js App Router conventions
4. Use TypeScript, Tailwind CSS
5. Maintain QB governance: zero-friction, invisible AI tone, no login walls
6. Every free-text input must have rotating placeholder examples
7. Include GrapplerHook metadata if creating ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md
8. Ensure all imports are correct and all referenced files exist
9. Minimize changes — only touch files that need changing
10. NEVER remove existing features unless explicitly asked

Return ONLY valid JSON array. No markdown, no explanation.`;

  const response = await client.messages.create({
    model: 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',
    max_tokens: 8000,
    messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }],
  });

  const text = response.content
    .filter((b): b is Anthropic.TextBlock => b.type === 'text')
    .map(b => b.text)
    .join('');

  try {
    // Extract JSON from response (handle potential markdown wrapping)
    const jsonMatch = text.match(/\[[\s\S]*\]/);
    if (!jsonMatch) throw new Error('No JSON array found in response');
    const patches: DiffPatch[] = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]);

    // Validate patches
    for (const patch of patches) {
      if (!patch.path || !patch.action || !patch.reason) {
        throw new Error(`Invalid patch: missing required fields`);
      }
      if ((patch.action === 'create' || patch.action === 'modify') && !patch.content) {
        throw new Error(`Patch for ${patch.path} (${patch.action}) missing content`);
      }
    }

    return patches;
  } catch (err: any) {
    throw new Error(`Failed to parse Claude's patch response: ${err.message}`);
  }
}

// === Assess risk of patches ===
function assessRisk(patches: DiffPatch[], scan: RepoScanResult): 'low' | 'medium' | 'high' {
  let risk = 0;

  for (const patch of patches) {
    // API route changes are medium risk
    if (patch.path.includes('api/')) risk += 2;

    // Layout changes affect everything
    if (patch.path.includes('layout.')) risk += 2;

    // Config changes are high risk
    if (patch.path.includes('next.config') || patch.path === 'package.json') risk += 3;

    // Auth changes are high risk
    if (patch.path.includes('auth') || patch.path.includes('middleware')) risk += 3;

    // Database changes are high risk
    if (patch.path.includes('db') || patch.path.includes('prisma') || patch.path.includes('migration')) risk += 3;

    // Deleting files is risky
    if (patch.action === 'delete') risk += 2;

    // New files are low risk
    if (patch.action === 'create') risk += 0.5;

    // Component modifications are medium risk
    if (patch.action === 'modify' && patch.path.includes('components/')) risk += 1;
  }

  if (risk >= 8) return 'high';
  if (risk >= 4) return 'medium';
  return 'low';
}

// === Find routes affected by patches ===
function findAffectedRoutes(patches: DiffPatch[], scan: RepoScanResult): string[] {
  const affected = new Set<string>();

  for (const patch of patches) {
    // Check if patch path corresponds to a route
    const routeMatch = patch.path.match(/^app\/(.+?)\/(page|route)\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/);
    if (routeMatch) {
      affected.add('/' + routeMatch[1]);
    }

    // Layout changes affect all routes
    if (patch.path.includes('layout.')) {
      for (const route of scan.routes) affected.add(route);
    }

    // Global CSS changes affect all routes
    if (patch.path.includes('globals.css')) {
      affected.add('/ (global styles)');
    }
  }

  return Array.from(affected);
}

// === Apply patches to a repo via GitHub API ===
export async function applyPatches(
  repoUrl: string,
  patches: DiffPatch[],
  branch: string,
  commitMessage: string,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<string> {
  const emit = (phase: string, status: StreamEvent['status'], message: string, data?: any) => {
    onEvent?.({ phase, status, message, data });
  };

  // Import GitHub utilities (these exist in the 2.0 codebase)
  const { createBlob, createTree, createCommit, updateRef, getRef } = await import('./github-ops');

  const { owner, repo } = parseRepoUrl(repoUrl);

  emit('apply', 'running', `Applying ${patches.length} patches to ${branch}...`);

  // Get current HEAD
  const headSha = await getRef(owner, repo, branch);

  // Create blobs for all new/modified files
  const treeItems: any[] = [];
  for (const patch of patches) {
    if (patch.action === 'delete') {
      treeItems.push({ path: patch.path, mode: '100644', type: 'blob', sha: null });
    } else {
      const blobSha = await createBlob(owner, repo, patch.content!);
      treeItems.push({ path: patch.path, mode: '100644', type: 'blob', sha: blobSha });
    }
  }

  // Create tree
  const treeSha = await createTree(owner, repo, treeItems, headSha);

  // Create commit
  const commitSha = await createCommit(owner, repo, commitMessage, treeSha, headSha);

  // Update branch ref
  await updateRef(owner, repo, branch, commitSha);

  emit('apply', 'done', `Applied ${patches.length} patches. Commit: ${commitSha.slice(0, 8)}`, { commitSha });

  return commitSha;
}

// Helper to parse repo URL (duplicated here for independence)
function parseRepoUrl(url: string): { owner: string; repo: string } {
  const cleaned = url.replace(/\.git$/, '').replace(/\/$/, '');
  const match = cleaned.match(/(?:github\.com\/)?([^\/]+)\/([^\/]+)$/);
  if (!match) throw new Error(`Cannot parse repo URL: ${url}`);
  return { owner: match[1], repo: match[2] };
}
```

## File: `lib/engine-deps.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Engine Dependency Graph
// Tracks inter-engine dependencies, computes deploy order,
// detects cycles, manages env var wiring between engines
// ============================================================

import { getAllEngines, getAllDependencies, addDependency, removeDependency } from './db';
import type { EngineDependency, DependencyGraph, StreamEvent } from './types-v3';

// === Build full dependency graph ===
export async function buildDependencyGraph(): Promise<DependencyGraph> {
  const engines = await getAllEngines();
  const depsRows = await getAllDependencies();

  const engineSlugs = engines.map(e => e.slug);
  const edges: EngineDependency[] = depsRows.map(r => ({
    from: r.from_slug,
    to: r.to_slug,
    type: r.dep_type || 'api',
    envVar: r.env_var || '',
    description: r.description || '',
  }));

  // Detect cycles
  const cycles = detectCycles(engineSlugs, edges);

  // Compute deploy order (topological sort)
  const deployOrder = topologicalSort(engineSlugs, edges);

  // Find isolated engines (no dependencies in or out)
  const connected = new Set<string>();
  for (const edge of edges) {
    connected.add(edge.from);
    connected.add(edge.to);
  }
  const isolated = engineSlugs.filter(s => !connected.has(s));

  return { engines: engineSlugs, edges, deployOrder, cycles, isolated };
}

// === Add a dependency ===
export async function addEngineDependency(
  from: string,
  to: string,
  type: EngineDependency['type'],
  envVar: string,
  description: string,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<void> {
  // Validate that both engines exist
  const engines = await getAllEngines();
  const slugs = engines.map(e => e.slug);
  if (!slugs.includes(from)) throw new Error(`Engine "${from}" not found`);
  if (!slugs.includes(to)) throw new Error(`Engine "${to}" not found`);
  if (from === to) throw new Error('Engine cannot depend on itself');

  // Check for cycles before adding
  const currentDeps = await getAllDependencies();
  const edges: EngineDependency[] = [
    ...currentDeps.map(r => ({ from: r.from_slug, to: r.to_slug, type: r.dep_type as any, envVar: r.env_var, description: r.description })),
    { from, to, type, envVar, description },
  ];
  const cycles = detectCycles(slugs, edges);
  if (cycles.length > 0) {
    throw new Error(`Adding this dependency would create a cycle: ${cycles[0].join(' → ')}`);
  }

  await addDependency(from, to, type, envVar, description);
  onEvent?.({ phase: 'deps', status: 'done', message: `Dependency added: ${from} → ${to} (${type})` });
}

// === Remove a dependency ===
export async function removeEngineDependency(from: string, to: string): Promise<void> {
  await removeDependency(from, to);
}

// === Get deploy order for a specific engine ===
export async function getDeployOrderFor(slug: string): Promise<string[]> {
  const graph = await buildDependencyGraph();

  // Find all transitive dependencies
  const deps = new Set<string>();
  const queue = [slug];
  while (queue.length > 0) {
    const current = queue.pop()!;
    for (const edge of graph.edges) {
      if (edge.from === current && !deps.has(edge.to)) {
        deps.add(edge.to);
        queue.push(edge.to);
      }
    }
  }

  // Return dependencies in topological order, then the engine itself
  const ordered = graph.deployOrder.filter(s => deps.has(s));
  ordered.push(slug);
  return ordered;
}

// === Topological Sort (Kahn's algorithm) ===
function topologicalSort(nodes: string[], edges: EngineDependency[]): string[] {
  const inDegree = new Map<string, number>();
  const adjList = new Map<string, string[]>();

  for (const node of nodes) {
    inDegree.set(node, 0);
    adjList.set(node, []);
  }

  for (const edge of edges) {
    // edge.from depends on edge.to → edge.to must deploy first
    adjList.get(edge.to)?.push(edge.from);
    inDegree.set(edge.from, (inDegree.get(edge.from) || 0) + 1);
  }

  const queue: string[] = [];
  for (const [node, degree] of inDegree) {
    if (degree === 0) queue.push(node);
  }

  const sorted: string[] = [];
  while (queue.length > 0) {
    const current = queue.shift()!;
    sorted.push(current);

    for (const neighbor of adjList.get(current) || []) {
      const newDegree = (inDegree.get(neighbor) || 1) - 1;
      inDegree.set(neighbor, newDegree);
      if (newDegree === 0) queue.push(neighbor);
    }
  }

  // If sorted doesn't contain all nodes, there's a cycle — return what we can
  if (sorted.length < nodes.length) {
    const remaining = nodes.filter(n => !sorted.includes(n));
    sorted.push(...remaining);
  }

  return sorted;
}

// === Cycle Detection (DFS) ===
function detectCycles(nodes: string[], edges: EngineDependency[]): string[][] {
  const adjList = new Map<string, string[]>();
  for (const node of nodes) adjList.set(node, []);
  for (const edge of edges) {
    adjList.get(edge.from)?.push(edge.to);
  }

  const cycles: string[][] = [];
  const visited = new Set<string>();
  const inStack = new Set<string>();
  const path: string[] = [];

  function dfs(node: string): void {
    visited.add(node);
    inStack.add(node);
    path.push(node);

    for (const neighbor of adjList.get(node) || []) {
      if (!visited.has(neighbor)) {
        dfs(neighbor);
      } else if (inStack.has(neighbor)) {
        // Found a cycle
        const cycleStart = path.indexOf(neighbor);
        if (cycleStart >= 0) {
          cycles.push([...path.slice(cycleStart), neighbor]);
        }
      }
    }

    path.pop();
    inStack.delete(node);
  }

  for (const node of nodes) {
    if (!visited.has(node)) dfs(node);
  }

  return cycles;
}

// === Check if all dependencies are deployed before deploying an engine ===
export async function checkDependenciesDeployed(slug: string): Promise<{ ready: boolean; missing: string[] }> {
  const engines = await getAllEngines();
  const depsRows = await getAllDependencies();

  const directDeps = depsRows
    .filter(r => r.from_slug === slug)
    .map(r => r.to_slug);

  const missing: string[] = [];
  for (const dep of directDeps) {
    const engine = engines.find(e => e.slug === dep);
    if (!engine || engine.status !== 'live') {
      missing.push(dep);
    }
  }

  return { ready: missing.length === 0, missing };
}

// === Get env vars that need to be set for an engine based on its dependencies ===
export async function getDependencyEnvVars(slug: string): Promise<Array<{ key: string; value: string; description: string }>> {
  const engines = await getAllEngines();
  const depsRows = await getAllDependencies();

  const deps = depsRows.filter(r => r.from_slug === slug);
  const envVars: Array<{ key: string; value: string; description: string }> = [];

  for (const dep of deps) {
    if (dep.env_var) {
      const targetEngine = engines.find(e => e.slug === dep.to_slug);
      const domain = targetEngine?.domain || `${dep.to_slug}.hive.baby`;
      envVars.push({
        key: dep.env_var,
        value: `https://${domain}`,
        description: `${dep.description || dep.dep_type} dependency on ${dep.to_slug}`,
      });
    }
  }

  return envVars;
}
```
