## File: `lib/engine-memory.ts`

```typescript
// =============================================================================
// HEB 3.0 — ENGINE MEMORY LAYER
// Per-engine persistent conversation history, design decisions, and context
// =============================================================================

import { neon } from '@neondatabase/serverless';

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Types
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export type MemoryEntryType =
  | 'design_prompt'      // Initial build request from creator
  | 'design_plan'        // Claude's architectural plan
  | 'design_decision'    // Explicit design choice (e.g., "use tabbed layout")
  | 'generated_code'     // Summary of what was generated (not full code — too large)
  | 'governance_result'  // QB audit results
  | 'update_request'     // Creator's update instruction
  | 'update_plan'        // Claude's plan for the update
  | 'update_diff'        // Summary of what changed
  | 'deploy_result'      // Deploy outcome (success/fail, URL, errors)
  | 'chat_message'       // Advisory discussion about this engine
  | 'adoption_note'      // When engine was adopted into HEB
  | 'rollback_note'      // When engine was rolled back
  | 'batch_operation'    // When engine was modified via batch op
  | 'annotation';        // Manual note from creator

export interface MemoryEntry {
  id: string;
  engine_slug: string;
  entry_type: MemoryEntryType;
  role: 'creator' | 'system' | 'claude';
  content: string;
  metadata: Record<string, any>;
  created_at: string;
}

export interface MemoryContext {
  engine_slug: string;
  engine_name: string;
  total_entries: number;
  summary: string | null;
  entries: MemoryEntry[];
  token_estimate: number;
}

export interface MemorySearchResult {
  entries: MemoryEntry[];
  query: string;
  total_matches: number;
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Database initialization
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

function getDb() {
  const url = process.env.DATABASE_URL;
  if (!url) throw new Error('DATABASE_URL not set');
  return neon(url);
}

export async function initMemoryTable(): Promise<void> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await sql`
    CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS engine_memory (
      id TEXT PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid()::text,
      engine_slug TEXT NOT NULL,
      entry_type TEXT NOT NULL,
      role TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'system',
      content TEXT NOT NULL,
      metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}'::jsonb,
      created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
      is_summarized BOOLEAN DEFAULT FALSE,
      summary_group_id TEXT DEFAULT NULL
    )
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_engine_memory_slug
    ON engine_memory(engine_slug, created_at DESC)
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_engine_memory_type
    ON engine_memory(engine_slug, entry_type)
  `;
  await sql`
    CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_engine_memory_search
    ON engine_memory USING gin(to_tsvector('english', content))
  `;
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Core CRUD
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export async function addMemory(
  engine_slug: string,
  entry_type: MemoryEntryType,
  role: 'creator' | 'system' | 'claude',
  content: string,
  metadata: Record<string, any> = {}
): Promise<string> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initMemoryTable();

  const rows = await sql`
    INSERT INTO engine_memory (engine_slug, entry_type, role, content, metadata)
    VALUES (${engine_slug}, ${entry_type}, ${role}, ${content}, ${JSON.stringify(metadata)}::jsonb)
    RETURNING id
  `;
  return rows[0].id;
}

export async function getMemory(
  engine_slug: string,
  options: {
    types?: MemoryEntryType[];
    limit?: number;
    offset?: number;
    since?: string;
    include_summarized?: boolean;
  } = {}
): Promise<MemoryEntry[]> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initMemoryTable();

  const {
    types,
    limit = 200,
    offset = 0,
    since,
    include_summarized = false
  } = options;

  // Build query conditionally
  if (types && types.length > 0 && since && !include_summarized) {
    const rows = await sql`
      SELECT id, engine_slug, entry_type, role, content, metadata, created_at::text
      FROM engine_memory
      WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug}
        AND entry_type = ANY(${types})
        AND created_at >= ${since}::timestamptz
        AND is_summarized = FALSE
      ORDER BY created_at ASC
      LIMIT ${limit} OFFSET ${offset}
    `;
    return rows as MemoryEntry[];
  }

  if (types && types.length > 0) {
    const rows = await sql`
      SELECT id, engine_slug, entry_type, role, content, metadata, created_at::text
      FROM engine_memory
      WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug}
        AND entry_type = ANY(${types})
        AND (is_summarized = FALSE OR ${include_summarized})
      ORDER BY created_at ASC
      LIMIT ${limit} OFFSET ${offset}
    `;
    return rows as MemoryEntry[];
  }

  const rows = await sql`
    SELECT id, engine_slug, entry_type, role, content, metadata, created_at::text
    FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug}
      AND (is_summarized = FALSE OR ${include_summarized})
    ORDER BY created_at ASC
    LIMIT ${limit} OFFSET ${offset}
  `;
  return rows as MemoryEntry[];
}

export async function searchMemory(
  engine_slug: string,
  query: string,
  limit: number = 20
): Promise<MemorySearchResult> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initMemoryTable();

  const rows = await sql`
    SELECT id, engine_slug, entry_type, role, content, metadata, created_at::text,
           ts_rank(to_tsvector('english', content), plainto_tsquery('english', ${query})) as rank
    FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug}
      AND to_tsvector('english', content) @@ plainto_tsquery('english', ${query})
    ORDER BY rank DESC, created_at DESC
    LIMIT ${limit}
  `;

  return {
    entries: rows as MemoryEntry[],
    query,
    total_matches: rows.length
  };
}

export async function searchMemoryAcrossEngines(
  query: string,
  limit: number = 20
): Promise<MemorySearchResult> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initMemoryTable();

  const rows = await sql`
    SELECT id, engine_slug, entry_type, role, content, metadata, created_at::text,
           ts_rank(to_tsvector('english', content), plainto_tsquery('english', ${query})) as rank
    FROM engine_memory
    WHERE to_tsvector('english', content) @@ plainto_tsquery('english', ${query})
    ORDER BY rank DESC, created_at DESC
    LIMIT ${limit}
  `;

  return {
    entries: rows as MemoryEntry[],
    query,
    total_matches: rows.length
  };
}

export async function deleteMemory(id: string): Promise<boolean> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const rows = await sql`
    DELETE FROM engine_memory WHERE id = ${id} RETURNING id
  `;
  return rows.length > 0;
}

export async function deleteEngineMemory(engine_slug: string): Promise<number> {
  const sql = getDb();
  const rows = await sql`
    DELETE FROM engine_memory WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug} RETURNING id
  `;
  return rows.length;
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Context assembly — builds the prompt context for Claude
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

const APPROX_CHARS_PER_TOKEN = 4;
const MAX_CONTEXT_TOKENS = 30000; // Reserve ~30k tokens for memory context

export async function assembleContext(
  engine_slug: string,
  engine_name: string,
  max_tokens: number = MAX_CONTEXT_TOKENS
): Promise<MemoryContext> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initMemoryTable();

  // Get total count
  const countRows = await sql`
    SELECT COUNT(*)::int as total FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug} AND is_summarized = FALSE
  `;
  const total = countRows[0].total;

  // Get rolling summary if one exists
  const summaryRows = await sql`
    SELECT content FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug}
      AND entry_type = 'annotation'
      AND metadata->>'is_rolling_summary' = 'true'
    ORDER BY created_at DESC
    LIMIT 1
  `;
  const summary = summaryRows.length > 0 ? summaryRows[0].content : null;

  // Priority loading: design decisions and recent entries first
  // 1. All design decisions (these are the most important — explicit choices)
  const decisions = await getMemory(engine_slug, {
    types: ['design_decision', 'design_prompt', 'design_plan'],
    limit: 50
  });

  // 2. All governance results (compliance history)
  const governance = await getMemory(engine_slug, {
    types: ['governance_result'],
    limit: 10
  });

  // 3. Recent everything (last 50 entries of any type)
  const recent = await getMemory(engine_slug, { limit: 50 });

  // Deduplicate by id
  const seen = new Set<string>();
  const allEntries: MemoryEntry[] = [];

  for (const entry of [...decisions, ...governance, ...recent]) {
    if (!seen.has(entry.id)) {
      seen.add(entry.id);
      allEntries.push(entry);
    }
  }

  // Sort chronologically
  allEntries.sort((a, b) =>
    new Date(a.created_at).getTime() - new Date(b.created_at).getTime()
  );

  // Trim to token budget
  const maxChars = max_tokens * APPROX_CHARS_PER_TOKEN;
  let charCount = summary ? summary.length : 0;
  const fittingEntries: MemoryEntry[] = [];

  for (const entry of allEntries) {
    const entryChars = entry.content.length + (entry.entry_type.length + 20);
    if (charCount + entryChars > maxChars) break;
    fittingEntries.push(entry);
    charCount += entryChars;
  }

  return {
    engine_slug,
    engine_name,
    total_entries: total,
    summary,
    entries: fittingEntries,
    token_estimate: Math.ceil(charCount / APPROX_CHARS_PER_TOKEN)
  };
}

export function formatContextForPrompt(ctx: MemoryContext): string {
  const lines: string[] = [
    `\n=== ENGINE MEMORY: ${ctx.engine_name} (${ctx.engine_slug}) ===`,
    `Total memory entries: ${ctx.total_entries}`,
    `Showing: ${ctx.entries.length} entries (~${ctx.token_estimate} tokens)`,
  ];

  if (ctx.summary) {
    lines.push(`\n--- ROLLING SUMMARY ---`);
    lines.push(ctx.summary);
  }

  lines.push(`\n--- MEMORY LOG ---`);

  for (const entry of ctx.entries) {
    const ts = entry.created_at.substring(0, 16).replace('T', ' ');
    const label = entry.entry_type.replace(/_/g, ' ').toUpperCase();
    lines.push(`\n[${ts}] ${label} (${entry.role})`);
    lines.push(entry.content);

    // Include key metadata inline
    if (entry.metadata && Object.keys(entry.metadata).length > 0) {
      const metaStr = Object.entries(entry.metadata)
        .filter(([k]) => !k.startsWith('_') && k !== 'is_rolling_summary')
        .map(([k, v]) => `${k}: ${typeof v === 'string' ? v : JSON.stringify(v)}`)
        .join(', ');
      if (metaStr) {
        lines.push(`  [meta: ${metaStr}]`);
      }
    }
  }

  lines.push(`\n=== END ENGINE MEMORY ===\n`);
  return lines.join('\n');
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Rolling summary — compresses old entries to save tokens
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export async function compressOldMemory(
  engine_slug: string,
  keepRecentCount: number = 30,
  generateSummary: (entries: MemoryEntry[]) => Promise<string>
): Promise<{ compressed: number; summary_id: string } | null> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initMemoryTable();

  // Count unsummarized entries
  const countRows = await sql`
    SELECT COUNT(*)::int as total FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug} AND is_summarized = FALSE
  `;
  const total = countRows[0].total;

  // Only compress if we have significantly more than the keep count
  if (total <= keepRecentCount * 1.5) return null;

  // Get entries to compress (oldest ones beyond the keep count)
  const toCompress = await sql`
    SELECT id, engine_slug, entry_type, role, content, metadata, created_at::text
    FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug} AND is_summarized = FALSE
    ORDER BY created_at ASC
    LIMIT ${total - keepRecentCount}
  `;

  if (toCompress.length === 0) return null;

  // Generate summary via Claude
  const summaryText = await generateSummary(toCompress as MemoryEntry[]);

  // Mark old entries as summarized
  const group_id = `summary_${Date.now()}`;
  const ids = toCompress.map(r => r.id);

  await sql`
    UPDATE engine_memory
    SET is_summarized = TRUE, summary_group_id = ${group_id}
    WHERE id = ANY(${ids})
  `;

  // Store the rolling summary
  const summary_id = await addMemory(
    engine_slug,
    'annotation',
    'system',
    summaryText,
    { is_rolling_summary: true, compressed_count: toCompress.length, group_id }
  );

  return { compressed: toCompress.length, summary_id };
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Memory stats
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export async function getMemoryStats(engine_slug: string): Promise<{
  total_entries: number;
  by_type: Record<string, number>;
  first_entry: string | null;
  last_entry: string | null;
  has_rolling_summary: boolean;
  estimated_tokens: number;
}> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initMemoryTable();

  const statsRows = await sql`
    SELECT
      COUNT(*)::int as total,
      MIN(created_at)::text as first_entry,
      MAX(created_at)::text as last_entry,
      SUM(LENGTH(content))::int as total_chars
    FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug} AND is_summarized = FALSE
  `;

  const typeRows = await sql`
    SELECT entry_type, COUNT(*)::int as count
    FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug} AND is_summarized = FALSE
    GROUP BY entry_type
  `;

  const summaryRows = await sql`
    SELECT COUNT(*)::int as count FROM engine_memory
    WHERE engine_slug = ${engine_slug}
      AND entry_type = 'annotation'
      AND metadata->>'is_rolling_summary' = 'true'
  `;

  const by_type: Record<string, number> = {};
  for (const row of typeRows) {
    by_type[row.entry_type] = row.count;
  }

  return {
    total_entries: statsRows[0].total,
    by_type,
    first_entry: statsRows[0].first_entry,
    last_entry: statsRows[0].last_entry,
    has_rolling_summary: summaryRows[0].count > 0,
    estimated_tokens: Math.ceil((statsRows[0].total_chars || 0) / APPROX_CHARS_PER_TOKEN)
  };
}

export async function getAllEngineMemoryStats(): Promise<Array<{
  engine_slug: string;
  total_entries: number;
  last_entry: string | null;
  estimated_tokens: number;
}>> {
  const sql = getDb();
  await initMemoryTable();

  const rows = await sql`
    SELECT
      engine_slug,
      COUNT(*)::int as total_entries,
      MAX(created_at)::text as last_entry,
      SUM(LENGTH(content))::int as total_chars
    FROM engine_memory
    WHERE is_summarized = FALSE
    GROUP BY engine_slug
    ORDER BY MAX(created_at) DESC
  `;

  return rows.map(r => ({
    engine_slug: r.engine_slug,
    total_entries: r.total_entries,
    last_entry: r.last_entry,
    estimated_tokens: Math.ceil((r.total_chars || 0) / APPROX_CHARS_PER_TOKEN)
  }));
}
```

## File: `lib/fleet.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Fleet Operations
// Health monitoring, batch operations, rollback for all engines
// ============================================================

import { getAllEngines, getEngine, updateEngine } from './db';
import { scanRepo } from './repo-scanner';
import { runGovernanceAudit } from './governance-audit';
import { generateUpdatePlan, applyPatches } from './diff-engine';
import { parseRepoUrl, getLatestCommit } from './github-ops';
import type {
  FleetHealth, FleetEngineStatus, BatchOperation, BatchResult,
  BatchItemResult, RollbackResult, RollbackRequest, StreamEvent, QuotaStatus,
} from './types-v3';

// === Daily Quota Tracking (in-memory, resets at midnight) ===
let quotaState = { apiCalls: 0, deploys: 0, repos: 0, resetAt: midnightToday() };

function midnightToday(): string {
  const d = new Date();
  d.setHours(24, 0, 0, 0);
  return d.toISOString();
}

function checkQuotaReset() {
  if (new Date().toISOString() >= quotaState.resetAt) {
    quotaState = { apiCalls: 0, deploys: 0, repos: 0, resetAt: midnightToday() };
  }
}

export function getQuotaStatus(): QuotaStatus {
  checkQuotaReset();
  return {
    apiCalls: { used: quotaState.apiCalls, limit: 500 },
    deploys: { used: quotaState.deploys, limit: 20 },
    repos: { used: quotaState.repos, limit: 10 },
    resetAt: quotaState.resetAt,
  };
}

export function incrementQuota(type: 'apiCalls' | 'deploys' | 'repos') {
  checkQuotaReset();
  quotaState[type]++;
}

// === Fleet Health Check ===
export async function getFleetHealth(
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<FleetHealth> {
  const emit = (msg: string) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'fleet-health', status: 'running', message: msg });

  emit('Loading all engines from database...');
  const engines = await getAllEngines();

  const statuses: FleetEngineStatus[] = [];
  let healthy = 0, degraded = 0, down = 0, unknown = 0;
  let totalGov = 0;

  // Check each engine in parallel (batches of 5)
  for (let i = 0; i < engines.length; i += 5) {
    const batch = engines.slice(i, i + 5);
    const results = await Promise.all(batch.map(async (engine) => {
      emit(`Checking ${engine.name}...`);
      const status = await checkEngineHealth(engine.domain, engine.repo_url);

      // Get latest commit info
      let lastCommit: string | null = null;
      let lastDeploy: string | null = null;
      try {
        const { owner, repo } = parseRepoUrl(engine.repo_url);
        const commit = await getLatestCommit(owner, repo);
        if (commit) {
          lastCommit = commit.date;
          lastDeploy = commit.date; // Approximation — deploy ≈ last commit for auto-deploy
        }
      } catch {}

      return {
        slug: engine.slug,
        name: engine.name,
        domain: engine.domain,
        repoUrl: engine.repo_url,
        vercelUrl: engine.vercel_url,
        status: status.health,
        lastDeploy,
        lastCommit,
        sslValid: status.sslValid,
        sslExpiry: status.sslExpiry,
        dnsResolved: status.dnsResolved,
        governanceScore: engine.governance_score,
        adopted: engine.adopted,
        dependencies: engine.dependencies,
        monetizationModel: engine.monetization_model,
        endpointLatency: status.latency,
      } as FleetEngineStatus;
    }));

    for (const s of results) {
      statuses.push(s);
      totalGov += s.governanceScore;
      switch (s.status) {
        case 'healthy': healthy++; break;
        case 'degraded': degraded++; break;
        case 'down': down++; break;
        default: unknown++; break;
      }
    }
  }

  const health: FleetHealth = {
    total: engines.length,
    healthy,
    degraded,
    down,
    unknown,
    averageGovernanceScore: engines.length > 0 ? Math.round(totalGov / engines.length) : 0,
    engines: statuses,
    lastSweep: new Date().toISOString(),
    quotaStatus: getQuotaStatus(),
  };

  onEvent?.({ phase: 'fleet-health', status: 'done', message: `Fleet: ${healthy} healthy, ${degraded} degraded, ${down} down`, data: health });
  return health;
}

// === Check individual engine health ===
async function checkEngineHealth(domain: string, repoUrl: string): Promise<{
  health: 'healthy' | 'degraded' | 'down' | 'unknown';
  sslValid: boolean;
  sslExpiry: string | null;
  dnsResolved: boolean;
  latency: number | null;
}> {
  if (!domain) return { health: 'unknown', sslValid: false, sslExpiry: null, dnsResolved: false, latency: null };

  try {
    const start = Date.now();
    const controller = new AbortController();
    const timeout = setTimeout(() => controller.abort(), 10000);

    const res = await fetch(`https://${domain}`, {
      method: 'HEAD',
      signal: controller.signal,
      redirect: 'follow',
    });
    clearTimeout(timeout);

    const latency = Date.now() - start;
    const sslValid = true; // If HTTPS succeeded, SSL is valid
    const dnsResolved = true;

    if (res.ok || res.status === 304) {
      return { health: latency > 5000 ? 'degraded' : 'healthy', sslValid, sslExpiry: null, dnsResolved, latency };
    } else if (res.status >= 500) {
      return { health: 'degraded', sslValid, sslExpiry: null, dnsResolved, latency };
    } else {
      return { health: 'healthy', sslValid, sslExpiry: null, dnsResolved, latency };
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    if (err.name === 'AbortError') {
      return { health: 'down', sslValid: false, sslExpiry: null, dnsResolved: false, latency: null };
    }
    // DNS resolution failure
    if (err.cause?.code === 'ENOTFOUND') {
      return { health: 'down', sslValid: false, sslExpiry: null, dnsResolved: false, latency: null };
    }
    // SSL error
    if (err.message?.includes('SSL') || err.message?.includes('certificate')) {
      return { health: 'degraded', sslValid: false, sslExpiry: null, dnsResolved: true, latency: null };
    }
    return { health: 'unknown', sslValid: false, sslExpiry: null, dnsResolved: false, latency: null };
  }
}

// === Batch Operations ===
export async function executeBatchOperation(
  operation: BatchOperation,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<BatchResult> {
  const emit = (msg: string, data?: any) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'batch', status: 'running', message: msg, data });
  const startedAt = new Date().toISOString();

  // Resolve target engines
  const allEngines = await getAllEngines();
  const targets = operation.targetSlugs === 'all'
    ? allEngines
    : allEngines.filter(e => (operation.targetSlugs as string[]).includes(e.slug));

  emit(`Batch ${operation.operation} targeting ${targets.length} engines`);

  const results: BatchItemResult[] = [];

  for (const engine of targets) {
    try {
      emit(`Processing ${engine.name}...`);

      switch (operation.operation) {
        case 'governance-audit': {
          const scan = await scanRepo(engine.repo_url);
          const audit = await runGovernanceAudit(engine.slug, scan);
          await updateEngine(engine.slug, { governance_score: audit.score });
          results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: `Score: ${audit.score} (${audit.grade})` });
          break;
        }

        case 'add-ribbon': {
          const plan = await generateUpdatePlan({
            slug: engine.slug,
            instruction: 'Add the multilingual LanguageSelector ribbon component with 9 languages (EN, AR, FR, ES, DE, ZH, JA, PT, HI), localStorage persistence under key hive_lang, fixed bottom-right position. Wire it to all API calls using withLang(input, getLang()) pattern. Include i18n.ts with getLang() and withLang() helpers.',
          });
          if (!plan.patches.length) {
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: 'Already has ribbon or no changes needed' });
          } else {
            const commitSha = await applyPatches(engine.repo_url, plan.patches, 'dev', `feat: add multilingual ribbon to ${engine.name}`);
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: `Ribbon added`, commitSha });
            incrementQuota('deploys');
          }
          break;
        }

        case 'add-first-visit-card': {
          const plan = await generateUpdatePlan({
            slug: engine.slug,
            instruction: 'Add a FirstVisitCard component that shows on first visit (localStorage check), explains what the engine does in one sentence, shows a CTA button, and auto-dismisses after interaction. Follow QB zero-friction onboarding rules.',
          });
          if (plan.patches.length > 0) {
            const commitSha = await applyPatches(engine.repo_url, plan.patches, 'dev', `feat: add FirstVisitCard to ${engine.name}`);
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: 'FirstVisitCard added', commitSha });
          } else {
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: 'Already has FirstVisitCard' });
          }
          break;
        }

        case 'add-auto-demo': {
          const plan = await generateUpdatePlan({
            slug: engine.slug,
            instruction: 'Add an AutoDemo component that immediately demonstrates the engine value on first load with pre-filled example content. User should see what the engine produces before doing anything.',
          });
          if (plan.patches.length > 0) {
            const commitSha = await applyPatches(engine.repo_url, plan.patches, 'dev', `feat: add AutoDemo to ${engine.name}`);
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: 'AutoDemo added', commitSha });
          } else {
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: 'Already has AutoDemo' });
          }
          break;
        }

        case 'security-headers': {
          const plan = await generateUpdatePlan({
            slug: engine.slug,
            instruction: 'Add security headers to next.config: Strict-Transport-Security (max-age=31536000, includeSubDomains), X-Content-Type-Options: nosniff, X-Frame-Options: DENY, X-XSS-Protection: 1; mode=block, Referrer-Policy: strict-origin-when-cross-origin',
          });
          if (plan.patches.length > 0) {
            const commitSha = await applyPatches(engine.repo_url, plan.patches, 'dev', `sec: add security headers to ${engine.name}`);
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: 'Security headers added', commitSha });
          } else {
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: 'Headers already present' });
          }
          break;
        }

        case 'update-dependency': {
          const pkg = operation.payload?.package;
          const version = operation.payload?.version;
          if (!pkg) throw new Error('payload.package required');
          const plan = await generateUpdatePlan({
            slug: engine.slug,
            instruction: `Update the npm dependency "${pkg}" to version "${version || 'latest'}" in package.json`,
          });
          if (plan.patches.length > 0) {
            const commitSha = await applyPatches(engine.repo_url, plan.patches, 'dev', `deps: update ${pkg} in ${engine.name}`);
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: `${pkg} updated`, commitSha });
          } else {
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: `${pkg} already at target version` });
          }
          break;
        }

        case 'custom-patch': {
          const instruction = operation.payload?.instruction;
          if (!instruction) throw new Error('payload.instruction required for custom-patch');
          const plan = await generateUpdatePlan({ slug: engine.slug, instruction });
          if (plan.patches.length > 0) {
            const commitSha = await applyPatches(engine.repo_url, plan.patches, 'dev', `custom: ${instruction.slice(0, 50)}`);
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: `${plan.patches.length} patches applied`, commitSha });
          } else {
            results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: true, message: 'No changes needed' });
          }
          break;
        }

        default:
          results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: false, message: `Unknown operation: ${operation.operation}` });
      }

      incrementQuota('apiCalls');
    } catch (err: any) {
      results.push({ slug: engine.slug, success: false, message: err.message });
    }
  }

  return {
    operation: operation.operation,
    startedAt,
    completedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    results,
  };
}

// === Rollback ===
export async function rollbackEngine(
  request: RollbackRequest,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<RollbackResult> {
  const emit = (msg: string) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'rollback', status: 'running', message: msg });

  const engine = await getEngine(request.slug);
  if (!engine) throw new Error(`Engine "${request.slug}" not found`);

  emit(`Rolling back ${engine.name}...`);

  const vercelToken = process.env.VERCEL_TOKEN;
  if (!vercelToken) throw new Error('VERCEL_TOKEN required for rollback');

  // Get deployments list
  const deploymentsRes = await fetch(
    `https://api.vercel.com/v6/deployments?projectId=${engine.slug}&limit=5&state=READY`,
    { headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${vercelToken}` } }
  );

  if (!deploymentsRes.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to list deployments: ${deploymentsRes.status}`);
  const deploymentsData = await deploymentsRes.json();
  const deployments = deploymentsData.deployments || [];

  if (deployments.length < 2) {
    throw new Error('Not enough deployments to rollback — need at least 2');
  }

  const currentDeploy = deployments[0];
  const targetDeploy = request.targetDeployId
    ? deployments.find((d: any) => d.uid === request.targetDeployId)
    : deployments[1]; // Previous deployment

  if (!targetDeploy) throw new Error('Target deployment not found');

  emit(`Rolling back from ${currentDeploy.uid.slice(0, 8)} to ${targetDeploy.uid.slice(0, 8)}...`);

  // Promote the target deployment
  // Vercel doesn't have a direct "rollback" API — we promote the old deployment
  // by aliasing the domain to it
  const aliasRes = await fetch(`https://api.vercel.com/v2/deployments/${targetDeploy.uid}/aliases`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      Authorization: `Bearer ${vercelToken}`,
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({ alias: engine.domain }),
  });

  if (!aliasRes.ok) {
    const body = await aliasRes.text();
    throw new Error(`Rollback alias failed: ${aliasRes.status} ${body}`);
  }

  emit(`Rollback complete: ${engine.name} now serving deployment ${targetDeploy.uid.slice(0, 8)}`);
  incrementQuota('deploys');

  return {
    slug: request.slug,
    previousDeployId: currentDeploy.uid,
    newDeployId: targetDeploy.uid,
    success: true,
    message: `Rolled back ${engine.name} to deployment ${targetDeploy.uid.slice(0, 8)}. Reason: ${request.reason}`,
  };
}

// === Deploy Freeze ===
let deployFrozen = false;

export function isDeployFrozen(): boolean {
  // Check env var first, then in-memory state
  return process.env.DEPLOY_FROZEN === 'true' || deployFrozen;
}

export function setDeployFreeze(frozen: boolean): void {
  deployFrozen = frozen;
}
```

## File: `lib/foundry.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Foundry (External Developer Platform)
// Accept, scan, audit, review, and deploy third-party engines
// All engines must pass QB governance before going live
// ============================================================

import { scanRepo } from './repo-scanner';
import { runGovernanceAudit } from './governance-audit';
import { adoptEngine } from './adopt';
import { createSubmission, getSubmission, getAllSubmissions, updateSubmissionStatus } from './db';
import type { FoundrySubmission, FoundryReviewAction, GovernanceAuditResult, StreamEvent } from './types-v3';
import { v4 as uuid } from 'uuid';

const MIN_GOVERNANCE_SCORE = 60; // Minimum score to be eligible for approval

// === Submit an engine to the Foundry ===
export async function submitToFoundry(
  developerName: string,
  developerEmail: string,
  engineName: string,
  repoUrl: string,
  description: string,
  category: string,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<FoundrySubmission> {
  const emit = (msg: string, data?: any) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'foundry', status: 'running', message: msg, data });

  const slug = engineName.toLowerCase().replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '-').replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
  const id = `fnd-${uuid().slice(0, 8)}`;

  emit(`Received submission: ${engineName} from ${developerName}`);

  // Auto-scan the repo
  emit('Scanning submitted repository...');
  let governanceAudit: GovernanceAuditResult | null = null;
  try {
    const scan = await scanRepo(repoUrl);
    emit(`Scan complete: ${scan.fileCount} files, ${scan.framework}`);

    // Run governance audit
    emit('Running QB governance audit...');
    governanceAudit = await runGovernanceAudit(slug, scan);
    emit(`Governance score: ${governanceAudit.score} (${governanceAudit.grade})`);
  } catch (err: any) {
    emit(`Scan failed: ${err.message} — submission recorded for manual review`);
  }

  const submission: FoundrySubmission = {
    id,
    developerName,
    developerEmail,
    engineName,
    slug,
    repoUrl,
    description,
    category,
    status: governanceAudit ? 'scanning' : 'pending',
    governanceAudit,
    submittedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    reviewedAt: null,
    deployedAt: null,
    reviewNotes: null,
  };

  // Auto-reject if governance score is too low
  if (governanceAudit && governanceAudit.score < MIN_GOVERNANCE_SCORE / 2) {
    submission.status = 'rejected';
    submission.reviewNotes = `Auto-rejected: Governance score ${governanceAudit.score} is below minimum threshold. Required fixes: ${governanceAudit.recommendations.slice(0, 3).join('; ')}`;
    emit(`Auto-rejected: governance score too low (${governanceAudit.score})`);
  } else if (governanceAudit) {
    submission.status = 'reviewing';
    emit('Submission ready for creator review');
  }

  await createSubmission(submission);

  onEvent?.({ phase: 'foundry', status: 'done', message: `Submission ${id} recorded`, data: submission });
  return submission;
}

// === Review a submission ===
export async function reviewSubmission(
  action: FoundryReviewAction,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<FoundrySubmission> {
  const emit = (msg: string) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'foundry-review', status: 'running', message: msg });

  const submission = await getSubmission(action.submissionId);
  if (!submission) throw new Error(`Submission "${action.submissionId}" not found`);

  emit(`Reviewing ${submission.engineName}: ${action.action}`);

  switch (action.action) {
    case 'approve':
      await updateSubmissionStatus(action.submissionId, 'approved', action.notes);
      submission.status = 'approved';
      submission.reviewNotes = action.notes;
      emit(`Approved: ${submission.engineName}`);
      break;

    case 'reject':
      await updateSubmissionStatus(action.submissionId, 'rejected', action.notes);
      submission.status = 'rejected';
      submission.reviewNotes = action.notes;
      emit(`Rejected: ${submission.engineName} — ${action.notes}`);
      break;

    case 'request-changes':
      const notes = action.requiredFixes
        ? `Changes requested: ${action.requiredFixes.join('; ')}. ${action.notes}`
        : action.notes;
      await updateSubmissionStatus(action.submissionId, 'pending', notes);
      submission.status = 'pending';
      submission.reviewNotes = notes;
      emit(`Changes requested for ${submission.engineName}`);
      break;
  }

  onEvent?.({ phase: 'foundry-review', status: 'done', message: `Review complete: ${action.action}`, data: submission });
  return submission;
}

// === Deploy an approved Foundry submission ===
export async function deployFoundrySubmission(
  submissionId: string,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<void> {
  const emit = (msg: string) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'foundry-deploy', status: 'running', message: msg });

  const submission = await getSubmission(submissionId);
  if (!submission) throw new Error(`Submission "${submissionId}" not found`);
  if (submission.status !== 'approved') throw new Error(`Submission must be approved before deployment. Current status: ${submission.status}`);

  emit(`Deploying Foundry engine: ${submission.engineName}`);

  // Use the adopt pipeline to register the engine
  await adoptEngine({
    slug: submission.slug,
    engineName: submission.engineName,
    repoUrl: submission.repoUrl,
    domain: `${submission.slug.replace(/^hive-/, '')}.hive.baby`,
  }, (event) => onEvent?.(event));

  await updateSubmissionStatus(submissionId, 'deployed');
  emit(`Foundry engine deployed: ${submission.engineName}`);

  onEvent?.({ phase: 'foundry-deploy', status: 'done', message: `${submission.engineName} is live` });
}

// === List submissions with optional filter ===
export async function listSubmissions(status?: string): Promise<FoundrySubmission[]> {
  return getAllSubmissions(status);
}

// === Get submission details ===
export async function getSubmissionDetails(id: string): Promise<FoundrySubmission | null> {
  return getSubmission(id);
}
```

## File: `lib/github-ops.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — GitHub Operations
// Low-level Git Data API helpers for commits, trees, blobs
// Used by diff-engine, fleet, and staging modules
// ============================================================

const GITHUB_API = 'https://api.github.com';

function getHeaders(): Record<string, string> {
  const token = process.env.GITHUB_TOKEN;
  if (!token) throw new Error('GITHUB_TOKEN not set');
  return {
    Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
    Accept: 'application/vnd.github.v3+json',
    'User-Agent': 'HEB-3.0',
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
  };
}

export function parseRepoUrl(url: string): { owner: string; repo: string } {
  const cleaned = url.replace(/\.git$/, '').replace(/\/$/, '');
  const match = cleaned.match(/(?:github\.com\/)?([^\/]+)\/([^\/]+)$/);
  if (!match) throw new Error(`Cannot parse repo URL: ${url}`);
  return { owner: match[1], repo: match[2] };
}

// === Ref Operations ===
export async function getRef(owner: string, repo: string, branch: string): Promise<string> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/git/ref/heads/${branch}`, {
    headers: getHeaders(),
  });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to get ref ${branch}: ${res.status}`);
  const data = await res.json();
  return data.object.sha;
}

export async function updateRef(owner: string, repo: string, branch: string, sha: string): Promise<void> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/git/refs/heads/${branch}`, {
    method: 'PATCH',
    headers: getHeaders(),
    body: JSON.stringify({ sha, force: false }),
  });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to update ref ${branch}: ${res.status}`);
}

export async function createBranch(owner: string, repo: string, branch: string, fromSha: string): Promise<void> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/git/refs`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: getHeaders(),
    body: JSON.stringify({ ref: `refs/heads/${branch}`, sha: fromSha }),
  });
  if (!res.ok) {
    const body = await res.text();
    if (body.includes('Reference already exists')) return; // Branch already exists
    throw new Error(`Failed to create branch ${branch}: ${res.status} ${body}`);
  }
}

// === Blob Operations ===
export async function createBlob(owner: string, repo: string, content: string): Promise<string> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/git/blobs`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: getHeaders(),
    body: JSON.stringify({ content, encoding: 'utf-8' }),
  });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to create blob: ${res.status}`);
  const data = await res.json();
  return data.sha;
}

// === Tree Operations ===
export async function createTree(
  owner: string,
  repo: string,
  items: Array<{ path: string; mode: string; type: string; sha: string | null }>,
  baseSha: string
): Promise<string> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/git/trees`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: getHeaders(),
    body: JSON.stringify({ base_tree: baseSha, tree: items }),
  });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to create tree: ${res.status}`);
  const data = await res.json();
  return data.sha;
}

// === Commit Operations ===
export async function createCommit(
  owner: string,
  repo: string,
  message: string,
  treeSha: string,
  parentSha: string
): Promise<string> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/git/commits`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: getHeaders(),
    body: JSON.stringify({ message, tree: treeSha, parents: [parentSha] }),
  });
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to create commit: ${res.status}`);
  const data = await res.json();
  return data.sha;
}

// === Repo Operations ===
export async function createRepo(name: string, isPrivate = false): Promise<{ fullName: string; cloneUrl: string }> {
  const owner = process.env.GITHUB_OWNER || 'saggarsonny-boop';
  // Try org repo first, then user repo
  let res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/orgs/${owner}/repos`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: getHeaders(),
    body: JSON.stringify({ name, private: isPrivate, auto_init: true }),
  });
  if (!res.ok) {
    res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/user/repos`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: getHeaders(),
      body: JSON.stringify({ name, private: isPrivate, auto_init: true }),
    });
  }
  if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Failed to create repo ${name}: ${res.status}`);
  const data = await res.json();
  return { fullName: data.full_name, cloneUrl: data.clone_url };
}

export async function deleteRepo(owner: string, repo: string): Promise<void> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}`, {
    method: 'DELETE',
    headers: getHeaders(),
  });
  if (!res.ok && res.status !== 404) throw new Error(`Failed to delete repo: ${res.status}`);
}

// === Get latest commit info ===
export async function getLatestCommit(owner: string, repo: string, branch = 'main'): Promise<{ sha: string; message: string; date: string } | null> {
  try {
    const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/commits/${branch}`, {
      headers: getHeaders(),
    });
    if (!res.ok) return null;
    const data = await res.json();
    return {
      sha: data.sha,
      message: data.commit?.message || '',
      date: data.commit?.committer?.date || '',
    };
  } catch {
    return null;
  }
}

// === List branches ===
export async function listBranches(owner: string, repo: string): Promise<string[]> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/branches`, {
    headers: getHeaders(),
  });
  if (!res.ok) return [];
  const data = await res.json();
  return data.map((b: any) => b.name);
}

// === Merge branches ===
export async function mergeBranches(
  owner: string,
  repo: string,
  base: string,
  head: string,
  message: string
): Promise<string | null> {
  const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/merges`, {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: getHeaders(),
    body: JSON.stringify({ base, head, commit_message: message }),
  });
  if (!res.ok) return null;
  const data = await res.json();
  return data.sha;
}

// === Push multiple files in a single commit ===
export async function pushFiles(
  owner: string,
  repo: string,
  branch: string,
  files: Array<{ path: string; content: string }>,
  message: string
): Promise<string> {
  const headSha = await getRef(owner, repo, branch);

  // Create blobs in parallel (batches of 5)
  const treeItems: Array<{ path: string; mode: string; type: string; sha: string }> = [];
  for (let i = 0; i < files.length; i += 5) {
    const batch = files.slice(i, i + 5);
    const results = await Promise.all(
      batch.map(async (f) => {
        const blobSha = await createBlob(owner, repo, f.content);
        return { path: f.path, mode: '100644' as const, type: 'blob' as const, sha: blobSha };
      })
    );
    treeItems.push(...results);
  }

  const treeSha = await createTree(owner, repo, treeItems, headSha);
  const commitSha = await createCommit(owner, repo, message, treeSha, headSha);
  await updateRef(owner, repo, branch, commitSha);

  return commitSha;
}
```

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Governance Audit Engine
// Full QB compliance scanning with 22-point checklist
// Produces scored, graded audit reports per engine
// ============================================================

import type { GovernanceAuditResult, GovernanceCheckItem, RepoScanResult, GovernanceFlags } from './types-v3';
import { recordAudit } from './db';

// === 22-Point QB Governance Checklist ===
interface GovernanceRule {
  key: keyof GovernanceFlags;
  rule: string;
  category: string;
  weight: number;
  check: (scan: RepoScanResult) => boolean;
  description: string;
}

const GOVERNANCE_RULES: GovernanceRule[] = [
  {
    key: 'engineGrammarPresent',
    rule: 'ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md present',
    category: 'Structure',
    weight: 5,
    check: (s) => s.hasEngineGrammar,
    description: 'Every engine must have ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md defining its purpose, schema, and metadata',
  },
  {
    key: 'grapplerHookPresent',
    rule: 'GrapplerHook → QueenBee.MasterGrappler',
    category: 'Structure',
    weight: 5,
    check: (s) => s.hasGrapplerHook,
    description: 'ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md must contain grappler_target: QueenBee.MasterGrappler',
  },
  {
    key: 'readmePresent',
    rule: 'README.md present',
    category: 'Structure',
    weight: 3,
    check: (s) => s.hasReadme,
    description: 'Every engine must have a README documenting purpose and usage',
  },
  {
    key: 'firstVisitCardPresent',
    rule: 'FirstVisitCard component',
    category: 'Onboarding',
    weight: 4,
    check: (s) => s.hasFirstVisitCard,
    description: 'Zero-friction onboarding card shown on first visit',
  },
  {
    key: 'autoDemoPresent',
    rule: 'AutoDemo component',
    category: 'Onboarding',
    weight: 3,
    check: (s) => s.hasAutoDemo,
    description: 'Instant value demonstration before user interaction',
  },
  {
    key: 'zeroFrictionOnboarding',
    rule: 'No login walls or paywalls before value',
    category: 'Onboarding',
    weight: 5,
    check: (s) => {
      // Check that main page doesn't require auth
      const mainRouteFiles = s.fileTree.filter(f =>
        f.path.match(/^app\/page\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/) ||
        f.path.match(/^app\/\(.*\)\/page\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/)
      );
      // No auth middleware blocking root
      const hasAuthMiddleware = s.fileTree.some(f => f.path === 'middleware.ts' || f.path === 'middleware.js');
      // If there's middleware, it might gate — flag as warning unless we can read it
      return mainRouteFiles.length > 0;
    },
    description: 'Users must see value before any login, signup, or payment wall',
  },
  {
    key: 'globalLanguageAgnosticism',
    rule: 'Multilingual ribbon (LanguageSelector)',
    category: 'Accessibility',
    weight: 4,
    check: (s) => s.hasMultilingualRibbon,
    description: 'LanguageSelector component with 9+ language support',
  },
  {
    key: 'invisibleAiTone',
    rule: 'No robotic UI copy',
    category: 'UX',
    weight: 3,
    check: (_s) => true, // Requires content analysis — default pass, Claude audit can override
    description: 'AI tone must be warm, competent, and non-robotic throughout',
  },
  {
    key: 'studioTemplating',
    rule: 'Consistent Hive visual identity',
    category: 'Design',
    weight: 3,
    check: (s) => {
      // Check for Tailwind and consistent theming
      const deps = { ...s.dependencies, ...s.devDependencies };
      return !!deps.tailwindcss || !!deps['tailwindcss'];
    },
    description: 'Engine uses Studio templates and consistent Hive design language',
  },
  {
    key: 'sunkCostArchitecture',
    rule: 'User investment accumulation',
    category: 'Retention',
    weight: 2,
    check: (_s) => true, // Architectural pattern — needs deeper analysis
    description: 'Every action increases user investment and reduces churn',
  },
  {
    key: 'universalPortability',
    rule: 'Data export capability',
    category: 'Trust',
    weight: 3,
    check: (s) => {
      return s.apiRoutes.some(r => r.includes('export')) ||
             s.fileTree.some(f => f.path.toLowerCase().includes('export'));
    },

    rule: 'Metadata and audit trail',

  },
  {
    key: 'universalUrgency',
    rule: 'Ethical urgency generation',
    category: 'Engagement',
    weight: 1,
    check: (_s) => true, // Feature-level
    description: 'Engine can generate urgency ethically when appropriate',
  },
];

// === Run Full Governance Audit ===
export async function runGovernanceAudit(
  slug: string,
  scan: RepoScanResult
): Promise<GovernanceAuditResult> {
  const passed: GovernanceCheckItem[] = [];
  const failed: GovernanceCheckItem[] = [];
  const warnings: GovernanceCheckItem[] = [];
  const recommendations: string[] = [];

  let earnedPoints = 0;
  let maxPoints = 0;

  for (const rule of GOVERNANCE_RULES) {
    maxPoints += rule.weight;

    const item: GovernanceCheckItem = {
      rule: rule.rule,
      category: rule.category,
      description: rule.description,
      weight: rule.weight,
    };

    try {
      const result = rule.check(scan);
      if (result) {
        passed.push(item);
        earnedPoints += rule.weight;
      } else {
        if (rule.weight >= 4) {
          failed.push(item);
        } else {
          warnings.push(item);
        }
      }
    } catch {
      warnings.push(item);
    }
  }

  // Add governance gap recommendations
  for (const gap of scan.governanceGaps) {
    if (gap.severity === 'critical') {
      recommendations.push(`CRITICAL: ${gap.description} — ${gap.fix}`);
    } else if (gap.severity === 'warning') {
      recommendations.push(`WARNING: ${gap.description} — ${gap.fix}`);
    } else {
      recommendations.push(`INFO: ${gap.description} — ${gap.fix}`);
    }
  }

  // Generate fix recommendations for failed items
  for (const item of failed) {
    const rule = GOVERNANCE_RULES.find(r => r.rule === item.rule);
    if (rule) {
      recommendations.push(`Fix required: ${item.rule} — ${item.description}`);
    }
  }

  const score = Math.round((earnedPoints / maxPoints) * 100);
  const grade = scoreToGrade(score);

  const audit: GovernanceAuditResult = {
    engineSlug: slug,
    score,
    maxScore: 100,
    grade,
    passed,
    failed,
    warnings,
    recommendations,
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
  };

  // Record in database
  try {
    await recordAudit(audit);
  } catch (err) {
    // Don't fail audit if DB write fails
    console.error('Failed to record audit:', err);
  }

  return audit;
}

function scoreToGrade(score: number): 'A' | 'B' | 'C' | 'D' | 'F' {
  if (score >= 90) return 'A';
  if (score >= 80) return 'B';
  if (score >= 70) return 'C';
  if (score >= 60) return 'D';
  return 'F';
}

// === Quick Governance Check (lighter, no DB write) ===
export function quickGovernanceCheck(scan: RepoScanResult): GovernanceFlags {
  const flags: Partial<GovernanceFlags> = {};
  for (const rule of GOVERNANCE_RULES) {
    try {
      flags[rule.key] = rule.check(scan);
    } catch {
      flags[rule.key] = false;
    }
  }
  return flags as GovernanceFlags;
}

// === Generate Governance Fix Patches ===
// Returns the diff patches needed to bring an engine to full compliance
export function generateGovernanceFixList(audit: GovernanceAuditResult): string[] {
  const fixes: string[] = [];

  for (const item of audit.failed) {
    switch (item.rule) {
      case 'ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md present':
        fixes.push('Create ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md with GrapplerHook metadata block');
        break;
      case 'GrapplerHook → QueenBee.MasterGrappler':
        fixes.push('Add grappler_target: QueenBee.MasterGrappler to ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md');
        break;
      case 'README.md present':
        fixes.push('Create README.md documenting engine purpose, usage, and architecture');
        break;
      case 'FirstVisitCard component':
        fixes.push('Add components/FirstVisitCard.tsx for zero-friction onboarding');
        break;
      case 'AutoDemo component':
        fixes.push('Add components/AutoDemo.tsx for instant value demonstration');
        break;
      case 'Multilingual ribbon (LanguageSelector)':
        fixes.push('Add components/LanguageSelector.tsx with 9-language support + i18n wiring');
        break;
      case 'No login walls or paywalls before value':
        fixes.push('Remove authentication gates from main page route');
        break;
      case 'Data export capability':
        fixes.push('Add /api/export route for data portability');
        break;
      default:
        fixes.push(`Fix: ${item.rule} — ${item.description}`);
    }
  }

  return fixes;
}

export { GOVERNANCE_RULES };
```

## File: `lib/monetization.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Monetization Engine
// Stripe product/pricing wiring per engine, support tiers,
// webhook configuration, aligned with Hive pricing rules
// ============================================================

import { getEngine, updateEngine, saveMonetization, getMonetization } from './db';
import type { MonetizationConfig, SupportTier, StreamEvent } from './types-v3';

const STRIPE_API = 'https://api.stripe.com/v1';

function getStripeHeaders(): Record<string, string> {
  const key = process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY;
  if (!key) throw new Error('STRIPE_SECRET_KEY not set');
  return { Authorization: `Bearer ${key}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/x-www-form-urlencoded' };
}

// === Hive Pricing Rules ===
// Free or $1/year → optional support ($20/$40/$60 one-time dropdown)
// Monthly pricing → no optional support
// Enterprise → unlimited usage per department, no seat limits

const SUPPORT_TIERS: SupportTier[] = [
  { amount: 20, label: 'Basic Support ($20 one-time)', stripePriceId: null },
  { amount: 40, label: 'Priority Support ($40 one-time)', stripePriceId: null },
  { amount: 60, label: 'Premium Support ($60 one-time)', stripePriceId: null },
];

// === Configure monetization for an engine ===
export async function configureMonetization(
  slug: string,
  model: MonetizationConfig['model'],
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<MonetizationConfig> {
  const emit = (msg: string, data?: any) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'monetize', status: 'running', message: msg, data });

  const engine = await getEngine(slug);
  if (!engine) throw new Error(`Engine "${slug}" not found`);

  emit(`Configuring ${model} monetization for ${engine.name}...`);

  let stripeProductId: string | null = null;
  const stripePriceIds: Record<string, string> = {};
  let supportTiers: SupportTier[] = [];
  let webhookSecret: string | null = null;
  let trialDays = 0;

  const stripeKey = process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY;

  if (stripeKey && model !== 'free') {
    // Create Stripe product
    emit('Creating Stripe product...');
    try {
      const productRes = await fetch(`${STRIPE_API}/products`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: getStripeHeaders(),
        body: new URLSearchParams({
          name: engine.name,
          description: engine.description || `${engine.name} — Hive Engine`,
          metadata: JSON.stringify({ engine_slug: slug, hive_engine: 'true' }),
        }),
      });
      if (productRes.ok) {
        const product = await productRes.json();
        stripeProductId = product.id;
        emit(`Stripe product created: ${product.id}`);
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      emit(`Stripe product creation failed: ${err.message}`);
    }

    // Create prices based on model
    if (stripeProductId) {
      switch (model) {
        case 'dollar-per-year':
          emit('Creating $1/year price...');
          const yearlyPrice = await createStripePrice(stripeProductId, 100, 'usd', 'year');
          if (yearlyPrice) stripePriceIds['yearly'] = yearlyPrice;
          break;

        case 'monthly':
          emit('Creating monthly price...');
          // Default monthly price — creator can adjust in Stripe dashboard
          const monthlyPrice = await createStripePrice(stripeProductId, 999, 'usd', 'month');
          if (monthlyPrice) stripePriceIds['monthly'] = monthlyPrice;
          break;

        case 'enterprise':
          emit('Creating enterprise price...');
          // Enterprise is custom pricing — create a placeholder
          const enterprisePrice = await createStripePrice(stripeProductId, 49900, 'usd', 'month');
          if (enterprisePrice) stripePriceIds['enterprise'] = enterprisePrice;
          trialDays = 14; // Trust-first philosophy
          break;

        case 'free-with-support':
          // No subscription price, just support tiers
          break;
      }

      // Create support tier prices (for free and $1/year models)
      if (model === 'free' || model === 'free-with-support' || model === 'dollar-per-year') {
        emit('Creating optional support tier prices...');
        supportTiers = await createSupportTierPrices(stripeProductId);
      }
    }

    // Create webhook endpoint
    emit('Configuring webhook...');
    try {
      const webhookRes = await fetch(`${STRIPE_API}/webhook_endpoints`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: getStripeHeaders(),
        body: new URLSearchParams({
          url: `https://${engine.domain}/api/stripe-webhook`,
          'enabled_events[]': 'checkout.session.completed',
          description: `${engine.name} webhook`,
        }),
      });
      if (webhookRes.ok) {
        const webhook = await webhookRes.json();
        webhookSecret = webhook.secret;
        emit('Webhook configured');
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      emit(`Webhook creation failed: ${err.message} — can be configured manually`);
    }
  } else if (model === 'free') {
    emit('Free model — no Stripe configuration needed');
  } else {
    emit('STRIPE_SECRET_KEY not set — monetization config saved but Stripe not wired');
  }

  const config: MonetizationConfig = {
    engineSlug: slug,
    model,
    stripeProductId,
    stripePriceIds,
    supportTiers,
    webhookSecret,
    trialDays,
    created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
  };

  await saveMonetization(config);
  await updateEngine(slug, { monetization_model: model });

  onEvent?.({ phase: 'monetize', status: 'done', message: `Monetization configured: ${model}`, data: config });
  return config;
}

// === Create a Stripe price ===
async function createStripePrice(
  productId: string,
  unitAmount: number,
  currency: string,
  interval: 'month' | 'year'
): Promise<string | null> {
  try {
    const res = await fetch(`${STRIPE_API}/prices`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: getStripeHeaders(),
      body: new URLSearchParams({
        product: productId,
        unit_amount: unitAmount.toString(),
        currency,
        'recurring[interval]': interval,
      }),
    });
    if (res.ok) {
      const price = await res.json();
      return price.id;
    }
  } catch {}
  return null;
}

// === Create support tier one-time prices ===
async function createSupportTierPrices(productId: string): Promise<SupportTier[]> {
  const tiers: SupportTier[] = [];

  for (const tier of SUPPORT_TIERS) {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${STRIPE_API}/prices`, {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: getStripeHeaders(),
        body: new URLSearchParams({
          product: productId,
          unit_amount: (tier.amount * 100).toString(),
          currency: 'usd',
        }),
      });
      if (res.ok) {
        const price = await res.json();
        tiers.push({ ...tier, stripePriceId: price.id });
      } else {
        tiers.push(tier);
      }
    } catch {
      tiers.push(tier);
    }
  }

  return tiers;
}

// === Get monetization config for an engine ===
export async function getMonetizationConfig(slug: string): Promise<MonetizationConfig | null> {
  return getMonetization(slug);
}

// === Generate Stripe webhook route code for an engine ===
export function generateWebhookRouteCode(config: MonetizationConfig): string {
  return `import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import Stripe from 'stripe';

const stripe = new Stripe(process.env.STRIPE_SECRET_KEY!, { apiVersion: '2024-12-18.acacia' });
const webhookSecret = process.env.STRIPE_WEBHOOK_SECRET!;

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const body = await req.text();
  const sig = req.headers.get('stripe-signature')!;

  let event: Stripe.Event;
  try {
    event = stripe.webhooks.constructEvent(body, sig, webhookSecret);
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Webhook signature verification failed' }, { status: 400 });
  }

  switch (event.type) {
    case 'checkout.session.completed':
      const session = event.data.object as Stripe.Checkout.Session;
      // Handle successful payment
      console.log('Payment completed:', session.id);
      break;
    default:
      console.log('Unhandled event type:', event.type);
  }

  return NextResponse.json({ received: true });
}
`;
}
```

## File: `lib/orchestrator-memory.ts`

```typescript
// =============================================================================
// HEB 3.0 — ORCHESTRATOR ↔ MEMORY INTEGRATION
// Hooks that wire memory recording into every orchestrator pipeline step.
// Import these in your existing orchestrator and call at each stage.
// =============================================================================

import {
  recordBuildStart,
  recordDesignPlan,
  recordDesignDecision,
  recordCodeGeneration,
  recordGovernanceResult,
  recordUpdateRequest,
  recordUpdateDiff,
  recordDeployResult,
  recordAdoption,
  recordAnnotation,
  addMemory,
  assembleContext,
  formatContextForPrompt,
  compressOldMemory,
  MemoryEntry
} from './engine-memory';

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Build pipeline memory hooks
// Called by the orchestrator at each stage of engine creation
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export const buildMemoryHooks = {
  /**
   * Stage 1: Creator submits a build request
   * Call this as soon as the build request is validated
   */
  async onBuildRequested(slug: string, prompt: string, features?: string[]) {
    await recordBuildStart(slug, prompt, {
      features: features || [],
      pipeline: 'build'
    });
  },

  /**
   * Stage 2: Claude generates the architecture plan
   * Call after Claude returns the engine plan (name, pages, routes, etc.)
   */
  async onPlanGenerated(slug: string, plan: any) {
    const planText = typeof plan === 'string' ? plan : JSON.stringify(plan, null, 2);
    await recordDesignPlan(slug, planText, {
      page_count: plan.pages?.length,
      api_route_count: plan.apiRoutes?.length,
      pricing_model: plan.pricing
    });

    // Record each significant design decision from the plan
    if (plan.pricing) {
      await recordDesignDecision(slug, `Pricing model: ${plan.pricing}`, 'Auto-selected by Claude during planning');
    }
    if (plan.pages?.length) {
      await recordDesignDecision(slug, `Page structure: ${plan.pages.map((p: any) => p.path || p).join(', ')}`, 'Determined by Claude from prompt analysis');
    }
    if (plan.features?.length) {
      await recordDesignDecision(slug, `Core features: ${plan.features.join(', ')}`, 'Extracted from creator prompt');
    }
  },

  /**
   * Stage 3: Claude generates code files
   * Call after each code generation batch completes
   */
  async onCodeGenerated(slug: string, files: Array<{ path: string; content: string }>, phase: string) {
    const filePaths = files.map(f => f.path);
    const summary = `Phase "${phase}" generated ${files.length} files totaling ${files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.content.length, 0)} bytes`;
    await recordCodeGeneration(slug, summary, filePaths, { phase });
  },

  /**
   * Stage 4: Governance check completed
   * Call after QB governance audit runs
   */
  async onGovernanceChecked(slug: string, result: { grade: string; passed: string[]; failed: string[] }) {
    await recordGovernanceResult(slug, result.grade, result.passed, result.failed);
  },

  /**
   * Stage 5: GitHub repo created
   */
  async onRepoCreated(slug: string, repoUrl: string, owner: string) {
    await addMemory(slug, 'annotation', 'system',
      `GitHub repo created: ${repoUrl} (owner: ${owner})`,
      { event: 'repo_created', repo_url: repoUrl, owner }
    );
  },

  /**
   * Stage 6: Code pushed to GitHub
   */
  async onCodePushed(slug: string, branch: string, fileCount: number) {
    await addMemory(slug, 'annotation', 'system',
      `Code pushed to branch "${branch}" — ${fileCount} files`,
      { event: 'code_pushed', branch, file_count: fileCount }
    );
  },

  /**
   * Stage 7: Vercel project created
   */
  async onVercelProjectCreated(slug: string, projectId: string, projectName: string) {
    await addMemory(slug, 'annotation', 'system',
      `Vercel project created: ${projectName} (ID: ${projectId})`,
      { event: 'vercel_project_created', project_id: projectId, project_name: projectName }
    );
  },

  /**
   * Stage 8: Domain configured
   */
  async onDomainConfigured(slug: string, domain: string, dnsProvider: string) {
    await addMemory(slug, 'annotation', 'system',
      `Domain configured: ${domain} via ${dnsProvider}`,
      { event: 'domain_configured', domain, dns_provider: dnsProvider }
    );
  },

  /**
   * Stage 9: Env vars set
   */
  async onEnvVarsSet(slug: string, varNames: string[]) {
    await addMemory(slug, 'annotation', 'system',
      `Environment variables configured: ${varNames.join(', ')}`,
      { event: 'env_vars_set', var_names: varNames, count: varNames.length }
    );
  },

  /**
   * Stage 10: Deploy completed
   */
  async onDeployCompleted(slug: string, success: boolean, url: string | null, error?: string) {
    await recordDeployResult(slug, success, url, error || null, { pipeline: 'build' });
  },

  /**
   * Final: Build pipeline finished (success or failure)
   */
  async onBuildFinished(slug: string, success: boolean, summary: string) {
    await addMemory(slug, 'annotation', 'system',
      `BUILD ${success ? 'COMPLETE' : 'FAILED'}: ${summary}`,
      { event: 'build_finished', success }
    );
  }
};

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Update pipeline memory hooks
// Called by the orchestrator during engine updates
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export const updateMemoryHooks = {
  /**
   * Creator requests an update to an existing engine
   */
  async onUpdateRequested(slug: string, instruction: string) {
    await recordUpdateRequest(slug, instruction);
  },

  /**
   * Claude analyzes existing code and plans the update
   */
  async onUpdatePlanGenerated(slug: string, plan: string) {
    await addMemory(slug, 'update_plan', 'claude', plan, {
      event: 'update_plan',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  },

  /**
   * Diff applied — files changed
   */
  async onDiffApplied(slug: string, summary: string, filesChanged: string[]) {
    await recordUpdateDiff(slug, summary, filesChanged);
  },

  /**
   * Update deployed successfully
   */
  async onUpdateDeployed(slug: string, success: boolean, url: string | null, error?: string) {
    await recordDeployResult(slug, success, url, error || null, { pipeline: 'update' });
  }
};

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Adopt pipeline memory hooks
// Called when existing engines are brought under HEB management
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export const adoptMemoryHooks = {
  /**
   * Engine adopted into HEB fleet
   */
  async onEngineAdopted(slug: string, repoUrl: string, domain: string, scanResult?: any) {
    await recordAdoption(slug, repoUrl, domain, {
      scan_result_summary: scanResult ? {
        file_count: scanResult.file_count,
        framework: scanResult.framework,
        has_api_routes: scanResult.has_api_routes,
        has_engine_grammar: scanResult.has_engine_grammar
      } : null
    });
  },

  /**
   * Governance audit run on adopted engine
   */
  async onAdoptedEngineAudited(slug: string, grade: string, passed: string[], failed: string[]) {
    await recordGovernanceResult(slug, grade, passed, failed);
  }
};

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Context injection — gets memory for Claude prompts
// Used by the code generator and update diff engine
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

/**
 * Get full engine context formatted for injection into a Claude system prompt.
 * Used when:
 * - Generating updates (Claude needs to know all prior design decisions)
 * - Chat about an engine (Claude needs conversation history)
 * - Governance audits (Claude needs to know what was intended)
 * 
 * @param slug Engine slug
 * @param name Engine display name
 * @param maxTokens Token budget for memory context (default 30k)
 * @returns Formatted string ready to append to system prompt
 */
export async function getMemoryContextForPrompt(
  slug: string,
  name: string,
  maxTokens: number = 30000
): Promise<string> {
  try {
    const ctx = await assembleContext(slug, name, maxTokens);
    if (ctx.entries.length === 0 && !ctx.summary) {
      return ''; // No memory yet — don't inject empty block
    }
    return formatContextForPrompt(ctx);
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(`Failed to load memory context for ${slug}:`, err);
    return ''; // Graceful degradation — proceed without memory
  }
}

/**
 * Compress old memory entries when they exceed the threshold.
 * Call this periodically (e.g., after each build/update completes)
 * to keep token usage manageable.
 * 
 * @param slug Engine slug
 * @param claudeCall Function that calls Claude to generate a summary
 */
export async function maybeCompressMemory(
  slug: string,
  claudeCall: (prompt: string) => Promise<string>
): Promise<void> {
  try {
    await compressOldMemory(slug, 30, async (entries: MemoryEntry[]) => {
      const entriesText = entries.map(e => {
        const ts = e.created_at.substring(0, 16);
        return `[${ts}] ${e.entry_type}: ${e.content}`;
      }).join('\n\n');

      const prompt = `You are summarizing the design and build history of an engine in the Hive ecosystem.
Below are ${entries.length} chronological memory entries for this engine. Create a concise but complete summary that preserves:
- All design decisions and the reasoning behind them
- Architecture choices (pages, API routes, features)
- Governance audit results and any fixes applied
- Update history (what was changed and why)
- Any creator preferences or constraints mentioned

Do NOT lose any design decisions or explicit choices. Those are the most important.

ENTRIES:
${entriesText}

SUMMARY:`;

      return await claudeCall(prompt);
    });
  } catch (err) {
    console.error(`Memory compression failed for ${slug}:`, err);
    // Non-fatal — old entries remain unsummarized
  }
}

// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------
// Seed memory for existing engines (used during bulk-adopt)
// Captures known design context from external sources
// -----------------------------------------------------------------------------

export async function seedEngineMemory(
  slug: string,
  context: {
    description: string;
    features?: string[];
    designNotes?: string;
    deployHistory?: string[];
    governanceGrade?: string;
  }
): Promise<number> {
  let count = 0;

  // Record the description as the original design intent
  await addMemory(slug, 'design_prompt', 'system',
    `[SEEDED FROM ADOPTION] Original engine description: ${context.description}`,
    { seeded: true, source: 'adoption' }
  );
  count++;

  // Record known features as design decisions
  if (context.features?.length) {
    for (const feature of context.features) {
      await recordDesignDecision(slug, feature, 'Identified during adoption scan', { seeded: true });
      count++;
    }
  }

  // Record design notes if provided
  if (context.designNotes) {
    await recordAnnotation(slug, `[SEEDED] Design notes: ${context.designNotes}`, { seeded: true });
    count++;
  }

  // Record deploy history
  if (context.deployHistory?.length) {
    for (const entry of context.deployHistory) {
      await addMemory(slug, 'deploy_result', 'system', `[SEEDED] ${entry}`, { seeded: true });
      count++;
    }
  }

  return count;
}
```
