## File: `lib/repo-scanner.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Repo Scanner
// Analyzes existing GitHub repos via API to map structure,
// framework, components, routes, and governance compliance
// ============================================================

import type { RepoScanResult, FileNode, GovernanceGap } from './types-v3';

const GITHUB_API = 'https://api.github.com';

interface GitHubTreeItem {
  path: string;
  mode: string;
  type: 'blob' | 'tree';
  sha: string;
  size?: number;
}

function getHeaders(): Record<string, string> {
  const token = process.env.GITHUB_TOKEN;
  if (!token) throw new Error('GITHUB_TOKEN not set');
  return {
    Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`,
    Accept: 'application/vnd.github.v3+json',
    'User-Agent': 'HEB-3.0-Scanner',
  };
}

function parseRepoUrl(url: string): { owner: string; repo: string } {
  // Handles: https://github.com/owner/repo, github.com/owner/repo, owner/repo
  const cleaned = url.replace(/\.git$/, '').replace(/\/$/, '');
  const match = cleaned.match(/(?:github\.com\/)?([^\/]+)\/([^\/]+)$/);
  if (!match) throw new Error(`Cannot parse repo URL: ${url}`);
  return { owner: match[1], repo: match[2] };
}

// Fetch entire repo tree recursively
async function fetchTree(owner: string, repo: string, branch = 'main'): Promise<GitHubTreeItem[]> {
  const headers = getHeaders();

  // Try main, then deploy, then master
  const branches = [branch, 'deploy', 'main', 'master'];
  for (const b of branches) {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/git/trees/${b}?recursive=1`, { headers });
      if (res.ok) {
        const data = await res.json();
        return data.tree || [];
      }
    } catch {}
  }
  throw new Error(`Cannot fetch tree for ${owner}/${repo}`);
}

// Fetch file content from repo
async function fetchFileContent(owner: string, repo: string, path: string, branch = 'main'): Promise<string | null> {
  const headers = getHeaders();
  const branches = [branch, 'deploy', 'main', 'master'];

  for (const b of branches) {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${GITHUB_API}/repos/${owner}/${repo}/contents/${path}?ref=${b}`, { headers });
      if (res.ok) {
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.content && data.encoding === 'base64') {
          return Buffer.from(data.content, 'base64').toString('utf-8');
        }
        return null;
      }
    } catch {}
  }
  return null;
}

// Detect framework from package.json
function detectFramework(pkgJson: any): { framework: RepoScanResult['framework']; version: string | null } {
  const deps = { ...(pkgJson.dependencies || {}), ...(pkgJson.devDependencies || {}) };
  if (deps.next) return { framework: 'nextjs', version: deps.next };
  if (deps.vite) return { framework: 'vite', version: deps.vite };
  if (deps.react) return { framework: 'react', version: deps.react };
  return { framework: 'unknown', version: null };
}

// Extract routes from file tree
function extractRoutes(tree: GitHubTreeItem[]): string[] {
  return tree
    .filter(f => f.type === 'blob' && /^(app|pages)\//.test(f.path) && /page\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/.test(f.path))
    .map(f => {
      // app/about/page.tsx → /about
      // app/api/chat/route.ts → /api/chat
      return '/' + f.path
        .replace(/^(app|pages)\//, '')
        .replace(/\/page\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/, '')
        .replace(/\/route\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/, '')
        .replace(/^page\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/, '')
        .replace(/^route\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/, '');
    })
    .map(r => r === '/' ? '/' : r.replace(/\/$/, ''));
}

// Extract API routes
function extractApiRoutes(tree: GitHubTreeItem[]): string[] {
  return tree
    .filter(f => f.type === 'blob' && /^app\/api\//.test(f.path) && /route\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/.test(f.path))
    .map(f => '/' + f.path.replace(/^app\//, '').replace(/\/route\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/, ''));
}

// Extract component files
function extractComponents(tree: GitHubTreeItem[]): string[] {
  return tree
    .filter(f =>
      f.type === 'blob' &&
      /\.(tsx?|jsx?)$/.test(f.path) &&
      /^(components|app\/components|src\/components)\//.test(f.path)
    )
    .map(f => f.path);
}

// Detect env vars from .env.example or .env.local.example
function extractEnvVarNames(content: string): string[] {
  return content
    .split('\n')
    .filter(line => line.includes('=') && !line.startsWith('#'))
    .map(line => line.split('=')[0].trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
}

// Check governance compliance
function checkGovernance(tree: GitHubTreeItem[], files: Map<string, string>): { score: number; gaps: GovernanceGap[] } {
  const gaps: GovernanceGap[] = [];
  const checks: Array<{ file: string; rule: string; severity: GovernanceGap['severity']; fix: string }> = [
    { file: 'ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md', rule: 'ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md present', severity: 'critical', fix: 'Add ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md with GrapplerHook metadata block' },
    { file: 'README.md', rule: 'README.md present', severity: 'warning', fix: 'Add a README documenting the engine purpose and usage' },
  ];

  const filePaths = tree.map(f => f.path);

  // File presence checks
  for (const check of checks) {
    if (!filePaths.includes(check.file)) {
      gaps.push({ rule: check.rule, severity: check.severity, description: `${check.file} not found`, fix: check.fix });
    }
  }

  // GrapplerHook check
  const grammarContent = files.get('ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md') || '';
  if (grammarContent && !grammarContent.includes('QueenBee.MasterGrappler')) {
    gaps.push({ rule: 'GrapplerHook targets QueenBee.MasterGrappler', severity: 'critical', description: 'GrapplerHook metadata block missing or not pointing to QueenBee.MasterGrappler', fix: 'Add grappler_target: QueenBee.MasterGrappler to ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md frontmatter' });
  }

  // FirstVisitCard check
  const hasFirstVisit = filePaths.some(f => /FirstVisit/i.test(f));
  if (!hasFirstVisit) {
    gaps.push({ rule: 'FirstVisitCard component present', severity: 'warning', description: 'No FirstVisitCard component found', fix: 'Add components/FirstVisitCard.tsx for zero-friction onboarding' });
  }

  // AutoDemo check
  const hasAutoDemo = filePaths.some(f => /AutoDemo/i.test(f));
  if (!hasAutoDemo) {
    gaps.push({ rule: 'AutoDemo component present', severity: 'warning', description: 'No AutoDemo component found', fix: 'Add components/AutoDemo.tsx for instant value demonstration' });
  }

  // Multilingual ribbon check
  const hasRibbon = filePaths.some(f => /LanguageSelector/i.test(f));
  if (!hasRibbon) {
    gaps.push({ rule: 'Multilingual ribbon (LanguageSelector) present', severity: 'info', description: 'No LanguageSelector component found', fix: 'Add components/LanguageSelector.tsx with 9-language support' });
  }

  // Security headers check (next.config)
  const nextConfig = files.get('next.config.js') || files.get('next.config.mjs') || files.get('next.config.ts') || '';
  if (!nextConfig.includes('Strict-Transport-Security')) {
    gaps.push({ rule: 'HSTS security header configured', severity: 'warning', description: 'Strict-Transport-Security header not found in next.config', fix: 'Add security headers in next.config.js' });
  }

  // Free-text input examples check
  const hasPlaceholders = Array.from(files.values()).some(content =>
    /placeholder.*["'].*\.\.\.["']/i.test(content) || /rotating.*example/i.test(content)
  );
  if (!hasPlaceholders) {
    gaps.push({ rule: 'Free-text input has rotating placeholder examples', severity: 'info', description: 'No rotating placeholder examples detected in free-text inputs', fix: 'Add faded rotating examples to all free-text input boxes' });
  }

  // Score calculation
  const maxPoints = 10;
  const criticalPenalty = gaps.filter(g => g.severity === 'critical').length * 3;
  const warningPenalty = gaps.filter(g => g.severity === 'warning').length * 1.5;
  const infoPenalty = gaps.filter(g => g.severity === 'info').length * 0.5;
  const score = Math.max(0, Math.round(((maxPoints - criticalPenalty - warningPenalty - infoPenalty) / maxPoints) * 100));

  return { score, gaps };
}

// === Main Scanner ===
export async function scanRepo(repoUrl: string): Promise<RepoScanResult> {
  const { owner, repo } = parseRepoUrl(repoUrl);
  const tree = await fetchTree(owner, repo);

  // Fetch key files in parallel
  const keyFiles = [
    'package.json',
    'ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md',
    'README.md',
    'next.config.js',
    'next.config.mjs',
    'next.config.ts',
    '.env.example',
    '.env.local.example',
    'tsconfig.json',
  ];

  const fileContents = new Map<string, string>();
  const fetchPromises = keyFiles.map(async (path) => {
    const content = await fetchFileContent(owner, repo, path);
    if (content) fileContents.set(path, content);
  });
  await Promise.all(fetchPromises);

  // Parse package.json
  let pkgJson: any = {};
  try {
    pkgJson = JSON.parse(fileContents.get('package.json') || '{}');
  } catch {}

  const { framework, version: frameworkVersion } = detectFramework(pkgJson);

  // Extract env vars
  const envContent = fileContents.get('.env.example') || fileContents.get('.env.local.example') || '';
  const envVars = envContent ? extractEnvVarNames(envContent) : [];

  // Governance check
  const { score, gaps } = checkGovernance(tree, fileContents);

  // Build file tree
  const fileTree: FileNode[] = tree
    .filter(f => f.type === 'blob')
    .map(f => ({ path: f.path, type: 'file' as const, size: f.size, sha: f.sha }));

  return {
    framework,
    frameworkVersion,
    hasEngineGrammar: fileContents.has('ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md'),
    hasGrapplerHook: (fileContents.get('ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md') || '').includes('QueenBee.MasterGrappler'),
    hasFirstVisitCard: tree.some(f => /FirstVisit/i.test(f.path)),
    hasAutoDemo: tree.some(f => /AutoDemo/i.test(f.path)),
    hasMultilingualRibbon: tree.some(f => /LanguageSelector/i.test(f.path)),
    hasReadme: fileContents.has('README.md'),
    routes: extractRoutes(tree),
    components: extractComponents(tree),
    apiRoutes: extractApiRoutes(tree),
    envVars,
    dependencies: pkgJson.dependencies || {},
    devDependencies: pkgJson.devDependencies || {},
    fileTree,
    fileCount: fileTree.length,
    totalSize: fileTree.reduce((sum, f) => sum + (f.size || 0), 0),
    governanceScore: score,
    governanceGaps: gaps,
  };
}

// === Fetch specific files for diff-engine analysis ===
export async function fetchRepoFiles(repoUrl: string, paths: string[]): Promise<Map<string, string>> {
  const { owner, repo } = parseRepoUrl(repoUrl);
  const contents = new Map<string, string>();
  const promises = paths.map(async (path) => {
    const content = await fetchFileContent(owner, repo, path);
    if (content) contents.set(path, content);
  });
  await Promise.all(promises);
  return contents;
}

// === Fetch all source files (for template extraction) ===
export async function fetchAllSourceFiles(repoUrl: string, extensions = ['.ts', '.tsx', '.js', '.jsx', '.css', '.json', '.md']): Promise<Map<string, string>> {
  const { owner, repo } = parseRepoUrl(repoUrl);
  const tree = await fetchTree(owner, repo);

  const sourceFiles = tree.filter(f =>
    f.type === 'blob' &&
    extensions.some(ext => f.path.endsWith(ext)) &&
    !f.path.includes('node_modules') &&
    !f.path.includes('.next') &&
    (f.size || 0) < 100_000 // Skip files over 100KB
  );

  const contents = new Map<string, string>();
  // Batch fetch in groups of 10 to avoid rate limiting
  for (let i = 0; i < sourceFiles.length; i += 10) {
    const batch = sourceFiles.slice(i, i + 10);
    const promises = batch.map(async (f) => {
      const content = await fetchFileContent(owner, repo, f.path);
      if (content) contents.set(f.path, content);
    });
    await Promise.all(promises);
  }

  return contents;
}

export { parseRepoUrl, fetchFileContent };

```

## File: `lib/scaling.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Scaling Configuration
// Per-engine Vercel scaling: regions, function timeout,
// max concurrent executions, edge runtime, cron jobs
// ============================================================

import { getEngine, updateEngine, saveScaling, getScaling } from './db';
import type { ScalingConfig, StreamEvent } from './types-v3';

const VERCEL_API = 'https://api.vercel.com';

function vercelHeaders(): Record<string, string> {
  const token = process.env.VERCEL_TOKEN;
  if (!token) throw new Error('VERCEL_TOKEN not set');
  return { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
}

// === Default scaling config ===
const DEFAULT_CONFIG: Omit<ScalingConfig, 'engineSlug'> = {
  regions: ['iad1'],              // US East (closest to St Louis)
  maxConcurrent: 10,
  functionTimeout: 30,            // seconds
  edgeRuntime: false,
  cronJobs: [],
  maxDuration: 60,
  memory: 1024,                   // MB
};

// === Configure scaling for an engine ===
export async function configureScaling(
  slug: string,
  overrides: Partial<ScalingConfig> = {},
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<ScalingConfig> {
  const emit = (msg: string) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'scaling', status: 'running', message: msg });

  const engine = await getEngine(slug);
  if (!engine) throw new Error(`Engine "${slug}" not found`);

  const config: ScalingConfig = {
    engineSlug: slug,
    ...DEFAULT_CONFIG,
    ...overrides,
  };

  emit(`Configuring scaling for ${engine.name}...`);

  // Apply to Vercel project if token exists
  const vercelToken = process.env.VERCEL_TOKEN;
  if (vercelToken && engine.vercel_project_id) {
    // Update project settings
    emit('Applying Vercel project settings...');
    try {
      const updateRes = await fetch(`${VERCEL_API}/v9/projects/${engine.vercel_project_id}`, {
        method: 'PATCH',
        headers: vercelHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({
          serverlessFunctionRegion: config.regions[0],
          ...(config.edgeRuntime ? { framework: 'nextjs' } : {}),
        }),
      });

      if (updateRes.ok) {
        emit(`Region set to ${config.regions[0]}`);
      } else {
        const err = await updateRes.json();
        emit(`Region config warning: ${err.error?.message || 'unknown error'}`);
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      emit(`Vercel update failed: ${err.message}`);
    }

    // Configure cron jobs via vercel.json (would need code push)
    if (config.cronJobs.length > 0) {
      emit(`${config.cronJobs.length} cron job(s) configured — will be applied on next deploy`);
    }

    // Configure env vars for scaling
    emit('Setting scaling env vars...');
    const envVars: Record<string, string> = {
      FUNCTION_MAX_DURATION: config.maxDuration.toString(),
      FUNCTION_MEMORY: config.memory.toString(),
    };

    for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(envVars)) {
      try {
        await fetch(`${VERCEL_API}/v10/projects/${engine.vercel_project_id}/env`, {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: vercelHeaders(),
          body: JSON.stringify({
            key,
            value,
            type: 'plain',
            target: ['production', 'preview'],
          }),
        });
      } catch {}
    }
    emit('Scaling env vars set');
  } else {
    emit('Scaling config saved locally — will apply when Vercel token is available');
  }

  await saveScaling(config);

  onEvent?.({ phase: 'scaling', status: 'done', message: `Scaling configured for ${engine.name}`, data: config });
  return config;
}

// === Get current scaling config ===
export async function getScalingConfig(slug: string): Promise<ScalingConfig | null> {
  return getScaling(slug);
}

// === Generate vercel.json with scaling + cron config ===
export function generateVercelJson(config: ScalingConfig): object {
  const vercelConfig: any = {
    framework: 'nextjs',
    regions: config.regions,
    functions: {
      'app/api/**/*.ts': {
        maxDuration: config.maxDuration,
        memory: config.memory,
      },
    },
  };

  if (config.cronJobs.length > 0) {
    vercelConfig.crons = config.cronJobs.map(cron => ({
      path: cron.path,
      schedule: cron.schedule,
    }));
  }

  return vercelConfig;
}

// === Preset scaling profiles ===
export const SCALING_PRESETS: Record<string, Partial<ScalingConfig>> = {
  'starter': {
    regions: ['iad1'],
    maxConcurrent: 5,
    functionTimeout: 15,
    maxDuration: 30,
    memory: 512,
    edgeRuntime: false,
  },
  'standard': {
    regions: ['iad1'],
    maxConcurrent: 10,
    functionTimeout: 30,
    maxDuration: 60,
    memory: 1024,
    edgeRuntime: false,
  },
  'performance': {
    regions: ['iad1', 'sfo1', 'lhr1'],
    maxConcurrent: 50,
    functionTimeout: 60,
    maxDuration: 300,
    memory: 3008,
    edgeRuntime: false,
  },
  'edge-global': {
    regions: ['iad1', 'sfo1', 'lhr1', 'hnd1', 'sin1', 'syd1'],
    maxConcurrent: 100,
    functionTimeout: 30,
    maxDuration: 30,
    memory: 128,
    edgeRuntime: true,
  },
};

// === Apply a preset ===
export async function applyScalingPreset(
  slug: string,
  preset: keyof typeof SCALING_PRESETS,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<ScalingConfig> {
  const presetConfig = SCALING_PRESETS[preset];
  if (!presetConfig) throw new Error(`Unknown preset: ${preset}. Available: ${Object.keys(SCALING_PRESETS).join(', ')}`);

  onEvent?.({ phase: 'scaling', status: 'running', message: `Applying "${preset}" scaling preset...` });
  return configureScaling(slug, presetConfig, onEvent);
}

## File: `lib/staging.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Staging & Preview Deploys
// Create dev.enginename.hive.baby preview deployments
// before promoting to production
// ============================================================

import { getEngine } from './db';
import { createStagingRecord, updateStagingStatus, getActiveStaging } from './db';
import { parseRepoUrl, createBranch, getRef, mergeBranches } from './github-ops';
import { isDeployFrozen, incrementQuota } from './fleet';
import type { StagingDeploy, StreamEvent } from './types-v3';
import { v4 as uuid } from 'uuid';

const VERCEL_API = 'https://api.vercel.com';

function getVercelHeaders(): Record<string, string> {
  const token = process.env.VERCEL_TOKEN;
  if (!token) throw new Error('VERCEL_TOKEN not set');
  return { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}`, 'Content-Type': 'application/json' };
}

// === Create Staging Deploy ===
export async function createStagingDeploy(
  slug: string,
  branch = 'dev',
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<StagingDeploy> {
  const emit = (msg: string, data?: any) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'staging', status: 'running', message: msg, data });

  if (isDeployFrozen()) throw new Error('Deploy freeze active — cannot create staging deploys');

  const engine = await getEngine(slug);
  if (!engine) throw new Error(`Engine "${slug}" not found`);

  // Check for existing active staging
  const existing = await getActiveStaging(slug);
  if (existing && existing.status === 'ready') {
    emit(`Active staging already exists: ${existing.url}`);
    return existing;
  }

  const stagingDomain = `dev-${slug.replace(/^hive-/, '')}.hive.baby`;
  const id = `stg-${uuid().slice(0, 8)}`;

  emit(`Creating staging deploy for ${engine.name} from branch ${branch}...`);

  // Ensure dev branch exists
  try {
    const { owner, repo } = parseRepoUrl(engine.repo_url);
    const mainSha = await getRef(owner, repo, 'main');
    await createBranch(owner, repo, 'dev', mainSha);
  } catch {}

  // Trigger Vercel deployment from the dev branch
  let vercelDeployId = '';
  try {
    const { owner, repo } = parseRepoUrl(engine.repo_url);
    const res = await fetch(`${VERCEL_API}/v13/deployments`, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: getVercelHeaders(),
      body: JSON.stringify({
        name: slug,
        gitSource: {
          type: 'github',
          org: owner,
          repo,
          ref: branch,
        },
        target: 'preview',
      }),
    });

    if (res.ok) {
      const data = await res.json();
      vercelDeployId = data.id || data.uid || '';
      emit(`Vercel preview deploy triggered: ${vercelDeployId}`);
    } else {
      const body = await res.text();
      emit(`Vercel deploy failed: ${res.status} — falling back to branch-only staging`);
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    emit(`Vercel API unavailable: ${err.message} — branch created, manual deploy needed`);
  }

  const expiresAt = new Date(Date.now() + 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString(); // 24h expiry

  const staging: StagingDeploy = {
    id,
    engineSlug: slug,
    branch,
    stagingDomain,
    vercelDeployId,
    status: vercelDeployId ? 'deploying' : 'ready',
    url: vercelDeployId ? `https://${vercelDeployId}.vercel.app` : `Branch ${branch} ready for manual preview`,
    createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    expiresAt,
  };

  await createStagingRecord(staging);
  incrementQuota('deploys');

  // Poll for deployment completion if we have a deploy ID
  if (vercelDeployId) {
    emit('Waiting for staging deploy to complete...');
    const finalStatus = await pollDeployment(vercelDeployId, 120); // 2 min timeout for staging
    staging.status = finalStatus ? 'ready' : 'failed';
    await updateStagingStatus(id, staging.status);
    if (finalStatus) {
      emit(`Staging ready: ${staging.url}`);
    } else {
      emit('Staging deploy timed out or failed');
    }
  }

  onEvent?.({ phase: 'staging', status: 'done', message: `Staging: ${staging.url}`, data: staging });
  return staging;
}

// === Promote Staging to Production ===
export async function promoteStagingToProduction(
  slug: string,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<void> {
  const emit = (msg: string) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'promote', status: 'running', message: msg });

  if (isDeployFrozen()) throw new Error('Deploy freeze active');

  const engine = await getEngine(slug);
  if (!engine) throw new Error(`Engine "${slug}" not found`);

  const staging = await getActiveStaging(slug);
  if (!staging || staging.status !== 'ready') {
    throw new Error('No ready staging deploy to promote');
  }

  emit(`Promoting staging to production for ${engine.name}...`);

  // Merge dev → deploy (or dev → main depending on branch strategy)
  const { owner, repo } = parseRepoUrl(engine.repo_url);
  const mergeSha = await mergeBranches(owner, repo, 'deploy', 'dev', `promote: staging → production for ${engine.name}`);

  if (!mergeSha) {
    // Try main if deploy branch doesn't exist
    const mainMerge = await mergeBranches(owner, repo, 'main', 'dev', `promote: staging → production for ${engine.name}`);
    if (!mainMerge) throw new Error('Failed to merge dev into production branch');
  }

  await updateStagingStatus(staging.id, 'promoted');
  incrementQuota('deploys');

  emit(`Promoted: dev merged into production branch. Auto-deploy will pick it up.`);
  onEvent?.({ phase: 'promote', status: 'done', message: 'Staging promoted to production' });
}

// === Poll Vercel deployment status ===
async function pollDeployment(deployId: string, timeoutSeconds: number): Promise<boolean> {
  const start = Date.now();
  const deadline = start + timeoutSeconds * 1000;

  while (Date.now() < deadline) {
    try {
      const res = await fetch(`${VERCEL_API}/v13/deployments/${deployId}`, {
        headers: getVercelHeaders(),
      });
      if (res.ok) {
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.readyState === 'READY') return true;
        if (data.readyState === 'ERROR' || data.readyState === 'CANCELED') return false;
      }
    } catch {}

    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 5000)); // Poll every 5s
  }

  return false;
}

// === Get staging status ===
export async function getStagingStatus(slug: string): Promise<StagingDeploy | null> {
  return getActiveStaging(slug);
}

## File: `lib/template-library.ts`

```typescript
// ============================================================
// HEB 3.0 — Template Library
// Extract engine patterns as reusable templates, instantiate
// new engines from templates with variable substitution
// ============================================================

import { fetchAllSourceFiles, scanRepo } from './repo-scanner';
import { saveTemplate, getTemplate, getAllTemplates } from './db';
import { quickGovernanceCheck } from './governance-audit';
import type { EngineTemplate, TemplateFile, TemplateVariable, StreamEvent } from './types-v3';
import { v4 as uuid } from 'uuid';

// === Extract template from existing engine ===
export async function extractTemplate(
  sourceSlug: string,
  repoUrl: string,
  templateName: string,
  description: string,
  category: EngineTemplate['category'] = 'utility',
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<EngineTemplate> {
  const emit = (msg: string) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'template', status: 'running', message: msg });

  emit(`Scanning ${sourceSlug} for template extraction...`);
  const scan = await scanRepo(repoUrl);

  emit(`Fetching source files...`);
  const sourceFiles = await fetchAllSourceFiles(repoUrl);

  // Convert to template files with variable markers
  const templateFiles: TemplateFile[] = [];
  const engineNameRegex = new RegExp(sourceSlug.replace(/-/g, '[-\\s]?'), 'gi');

  for (const [path, content] of sourceFiles) {
    // Skip node_modules, .next, etc.
    if (path.includes('node_modules') || path.includes('.next') || path.includes('.git')) continue;

    // Replace engine-specific values with template variables
    let templated = content
      .replace(engineNameRegex, '{{ENGINE_SLUG}}')
      .replace(new RegExp(templateName.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&'), 'gi'), '{{ENGINE_NAME}}');

    const isTemplate = templated !== content;

    templateFiles.push({
      path,
      content: templated,
      isTemplate,
    });
  }

  // Detect variables from the codebase
  const variables: TemplateVariable[] = [
    { key: 'ENGINE_NAME', label: 'Engine Name', defaultValue: 'My Engine', required: true },
    { key: 'ENGINE_SLUG', label: 'Engine Slug', defaultValue: 'my-engine', required: true },
    { key: 'ENGINE_DESCRIPTION', label: 'Description', defaultValue: 'A Hive engine', required: true },
    { key: 'ENGINE_DOMAIN', label: 'Domain', defaultValue: 'myengine.hive.baby', required: true },
  ];

  // Check for API keys in env vars
  if (scan.envVars.includes('ANTHROPIC_API_KEY')) {
    variables.push({ key: 'ANTHROPIC_API_KEY', label: 'Anthropic API Key', defaultValue: '', required: false });
  }
  if (scan.envVars.some(v => v.includes('STRIPE'))) {
    variables.push({ key: 'STRIPE_SECRET_KEY', label: 'Stripe Secret Key', defaultValue: '', required: false });
  }
  if (scan.envVars.some(v => v.includes('DATABASE') || v.includes('NEON'))) {
    variables.push({ key: 'DATABASE_URL', label: 'Database URL', defaultValue: '', required: false });
  }

  // Get governance preset
  const governancePreset = quickGovernanceCheck(scan);

  const template: EngineTemplate = {
    id: `tpl-${uuid().slice(0, 8)}`,
    name: templateName,
    description,
    sourceSlug,
    category,
    files: templateFiles,
    variables,
    governancePreset,
    created_at: new Date().toISOString(),
  };

  await saveTemplate(template);
  emit(`Template "${templateName}" saved with ${templateFiles.length} files and ${variables.length} variables`);

  return template;
}

// === Instantiate engine from template ===
export async function instantiateTemplate(
  templateId: string,
  variableValues: Record<string, string>,
  onEvent?: (event: StreamEvent) => void
): Promise<Array<{ path: string; content: string }>> {
  const emit = (msg: string) => onEvent?.({ phase: 'template', status: 'running', message: msg });

  const template = await getTemplate(templateId);
  if (!template) throw new Error(`Template "${templateId}" not found`);

  emit(`Instantiating template "${template.name}" with ${template.files.length} files...`);

  const files: Array<{ path: string; content: string }> = [];

  for (const tf of template.files) {
    let content = tf.content;
    let path = tf.path;

    // Replace all template variables
    for (const variable of template.variables) {
      const value = variableValues[variable.key] || variable.defaultValue;
      const placeholder = `{{${variable.key}}}`;
      content = content.split(placeholder).join(value);
      path = path.split(placeholder).join(value);
    }

    files.push({ path, content });
  }

  emit(`Generated ${files.length} files from template`);
  return files;
}

// === List available templates ===
export async function listTemplates(): Promise<EngineTemplate[]> {
  return getAllTemplates();
}

// === Pre-built template definitions ===
// These can be loaded on first run to seed the template library
export const BUILT_IN_TEMPLATES: Array<{
  name: string;
  description: string;
  category: EngineTemplate['category'];
  files: Array<{ path: string; content: string; isTemplate: boolean }>;
  variables: TemplateVariable[];
}> = [
  {
    name: 'Clarity Engine',
    description: 'AI-powered clarity engine: free-text input, Claude analysis, structured output with viral sharing loop',
    category: 'clarity',
    variables: [
      { key: 'ENGINE_NAME', label: 'Engine Name', defaultValue: 'HiveClarity', required: true },
      { key: 'ENGINE_SLUG', label: 'Engine Slug', defaultValue: 'hive-clarity', required: true },

      { key: 'ENGINE_DOMAIN', label: 'Domain', defaultValue: 'hiveclarity.hive.baby', required: true },
      { key: 'SYSTEM_PROMPT', label: 'Claude System Prompt', defaultValue: 'You are a clarity engine. Analyze the input and produce structured, actionable clarity.', required: true },
    ],
    files: [], // Populated dynamically from HiveClarity scan
  },
  {
    name: 'Tracking Engine',
    description: 'Personal tracking engine: log entries, AI analysis, pattern detection, history view',
    category: 'tracking',
    variables: [
      { key: 'ENGINE_NAME', label: 'Engine Name', defaultValue: 'HiveTracker', required: true },
      { key: 'ENGINE_SLUG', label: 'Engine Slug', defaultValue: 'hive-tracker', required: true },
      { key: 'TRACK_WHAT', label: 'What are users tracking?', defaultValue: 'daily entries', required: true },
      { key: 'ENGINE_DOMAIN', label: 'Domain', defaultValue: 'hivetracker.hive.baby', required: true },

    ],
    files: [], // Populated dynamically from HiveField scan
  },
];

  status: 'pending' | 'scanning' | 'reviewing' | 'approved' | 'rejected' | 'deployed';
  governanceAudit: GovernanceAuditResult | null;
  submittedAt: string;
  reviewedAt: string | null;
  deployedAt: string | null;
  reviewNotes: string | null;
}

export interface FoundryReviewAction {
  submissionId: string;
  action: 'approve' | 'reject' | 'request-changes';
  notes: string;
  requiredFixes?: string[];
}

// === Monetization (3.0) ===
export interface MonetizationConfig {

}

## File: `app/api/workshop/batch/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 4.0 API — Batch Intent (Feature 7)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { planBatch, approveBatch, executeBatch, getBatchHistory, getBatch } from '../../../../lib/batch-intent';

function isAuthed(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return false;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret') || req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return header === secret;
}

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const { action, instruction, engines, batchId } = body;

    switch (action) {
      case 'plan': {
        if (!instruction || !engines) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'instruction and engines required' }, { status: 400 });
        const batch = await planBatch(instruction, engines);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, batch });
      }

      case 'approve': {
        if (!batchId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'batchId required' }, { status: 400 });
        const batch = await approveBatch(batchId);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, batch });
      }

      case 'execute': {
        if (!batchId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'batchId required' }, { status: 400 });
        const batch = await getBatch(batchId);
        if (!batch) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Batch not found' }, { status: 404 });
        
        // Execute with a placeholder engine executor
        // In production, this would wire into the diff engine + GitHub ops
        const result = await executeBatch(batch, async (slug, variation) => {
          // TODO: Wire into diff-engine + github-ops for real execution
          return { success: true };
        });
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, batch: result });
      }

      default:
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid action. Use: plan, approve, execute' }, { status: 400 });
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url);
    const batchId = searchParams.get('id');

    if (batchId) {
      const batch = await getBatch(batchId);
      if (!batch) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Batch not found' }, { status: 404 });
      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, batch });
    }

    const history = await getBatchHistory(20);
    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, batches: history });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

## File: `app/api/workshop/brainstorm/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 4.0 API — Brainstorm Mode (Feature 1)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { processBrainstorm, refineBlueprint } from '../../../../lib/brainstorm';
import { recordDecisions, getDecisions } from '../../../../lib/intent-memory';
import { getHintsForPrompt } from '../../../../lib/learner-v2';
import { v4 as uuid } from 'uuid';

function isAuthed(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return false;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret') || req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return header === secret;
}

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const { action, rawInput, blueprint, answers, additionalNotes, engineSlug } = body;

    if (action === 'refine' && blueprint && answers) {
      // Refine existing blueprint with answers
      const { updatedBlueprint, newDecisions } = await refineBlueprint(blueprint, answers, additionalNotes);
      
      // Record decisions
      const recorded = await recordDecisions(newDecisions);

      return NextResponse.json({
        success: true,
        blueprint: { ...updatedBlueprint, id: updatedBlueprint.id || uuid(), updatedAt: new Date().toISOString() },
        decisions: recorded,
      });
    }

    if (!rawInput) {
      return NextResponse.json({ error: 'rawInput required' }, { status: 400 });
    }

    // Get existing decisions if updating an existing engine
    const existingDecisions = engineSlug ? await getDecisions(engineSlug) : undefined;

    // Process brainstorm
    const { blueprint: newBlueprint, extractedDecisions } = await processBrainstorm(rawInput, existingDecisions);

    // Assign ID and timestamps
    const fullBlueprint = {
      ...newBlueprint,
      id: uuid(),
      createdAt: new Date().toISOString(),
      updatedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
    };

    // Record design decisions
    const recorded = await recordDecisions(extractedDecisions);

    // Get learner hints for context
    const hints = await getHintsForPrompt();

    return NextResponse.json({
      success: true,
      blueprint: fullBlueprint,
      decisions: recorded,
      learnerHints: hints || null,
    });

  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

## File: `app/api/workshop/break-mode/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 4.0 API — Break Mode (Feature 3)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { createFlagSession, addFlag, dismissFlag, classifyFlagType, processFixQueue, applyFixResults } from '../../../../lib/break-mode';
import { recordDecisions } from '../../../../lib/intent-memory';
import { recordFlagPattern } from '../../../../lib/learner-v2';

function isAuthed(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return false;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret') || req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return header === secret;
}

// In-memory sessions (persisted per-request cycle; in production use DB)
const sessions = new Map<string, ReturnType<typeof createFlagSession>>();

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const { action, engineSlug, sessionId, flag, flagId, repoFiles } = body;

    switch (action) {
      case 'create-session': {
        if (!engineSlug) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'engineSlug required' }, { status: 400 });
        const session = createFlagSession(engineSlug);
        sessions.set(session.id, session);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, session });
      }

      case 'add-flag': {
        if (!sessionId || !flag) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'sessionId and flag required' }, { status: 400 });
        let session = sessions.get(sessionId);
        if (!session) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Session not found' }, { status: 404 });

        // Auto-classify flag type if not provided
        if (!flag.type) flag.type = classifyFlagType(flag.note || '');

        session = addFlag(session, flag);
        sessions.set(sessionId, session);

        // Record pattern for Learner
        await recordFlagPattern(flag.type, flag.note || '', undefined);

        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, session });
      }

      case 'dismiss-flag': {
        if (!sessionId || !flagId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'sessionId and flagId required' }, { status: 400 });
        let session = sessions.get(sessionId);
        if (!session) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Session not found' }, { status: 404 });

        session = dismissFlag(session, flagId);
        sessions.set(sessionId, session);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, session });
      }

      case 'fix-all': {
        if (!sessionId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'sessionId required' }, { status: 400 });
        const session = sessions.get(sessionId);
        if (!session) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Session not found' }, { status: 404 });

        const openFlags = session.flags.filter(f => f.status === 'open');
        if (openFlags.length === 0) return NextResponse.json({ success: true, message: 'No open flags', session });

        // Process fixes via Claude
        const { fixes } = await processFixQueue(openFlags, repoFiles || []);

        // Apply results to session
        const { session: updatedSession, decisions } = applyFixResults(session, fixes);
        sessions.set(sessionId, updatedSession);

        // Record design decisions
        if (decisions.length > 0) await recordDecisions(decisions);

        return NextResponse.json({
          success: true,
          session: updatedSession,
          fixes,
          decisionsRecorded: decisions.length,
        });
      }

      case 'get-session': {
        if (!sessionId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'sessionId required' }, { status: 400 });
        const session = sessions.get(sessionId);
        if (!session) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Session not found' }, { status: 404 });
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, session });
      }

      default:
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid action. Use: create-session, add-flag, dismiss-flag, fix-all, get-session' }, { status: 400 });
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

## File: `app/api/workshop/decisions/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 4.0 API — Intent Memory / Design Decisions (Feature 4)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { getDecisions, getDecisionSummary, searchDecisions, deleteDecisions, recordDecision } from '../../../../lib/intent-memory';

function isAuthed(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return false;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret') || req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return header === secret;
}

export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url);
    const engineSlug = searchParams.get('engineSlug');
    const query = searchParams.get('q');
    const view = searchParams.get('view') || 'list';

    if (query) {
      const results = await searchDecisions(query, engineSlug || undefined);
      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, decisions: results });
    }

    if (!engineSlug) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'engineSlug required' }, { status: 400 });

    if (view === 'summary') {
      const summary = await getDecisionSummary(engineSlug);
      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, summary });
    }

    const phase = searchParams.get('phase') || undefined;
    const category = searchParams.get('category') || undefined;
    const limit = searchParams.get('limit') ? parseInt(searchParams.get('limit')!) : undefined;

    const decisions = await getDecisions(engineSlug, { phase, category, limit });
    return NextResponse.json({ success: true, decisions, count: decisions.length });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const { action, engineSlug, decision } = body;

    switch (action) {
      case 'add': {
        if (!decision) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'decision object required' }, { status: 400 });
        const recorded = await recordDecision(decision);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, decision: recorded });
      }
      case 'delete-all': {
        if (!engineSlug) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'engineSlug required' }, { status: 400 });
        const count = await deleteDecisions(engineSlug);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, deleted: count });
      }
      default:
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid action. Use: add, delete-all' }, { status: 400 });
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

```

// HEB 4.0 API — Factory Status (Feature 6)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { getFactoryRun, getLatestFactoryRun } from '../../../../lib/factory-pipeline';

function isAuthed(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return false;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret') || req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return header === secret;
}

export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url);
    const runId = searchParams.get('runId');
    const engineSlug = searchParams.get('engineSlug');

    if (runId) {
      const run = await getFactoryRun(runId);
      if (!run) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Run not found' }, { status: 404 });
      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, run });
    }

    if (engineSlug) {
      const run = await getLatestFactoryRun(engineSlug);
      if (!run) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'No factory runs for this engine' }, { status: 404 });
      return NextResponse.json({ success: true, run });
    }

    return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Provide runId or engineSlug' }, { status: 400 });
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

## File: `app/api/workshop/generate/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 4.0 — Workshop Code Generation (SSE streaming)
// Generates engine code from blueprint, streams progress to the Workshop UI
import { NextRequest } from 'next/server';
import { initV4Schema } from '@/lib/db-schema-v4';
import { neon } from '@neondatabase/serverless';

const db = neon(process.env.DATABASE_URL!);

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  const secret = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret');
  if (secret !== process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET) {
    return new Response('Not found', { status: 404 });
  }

  await initV4Schema();

  const body = await req.json();
  const { sessionId, blueprint } = body;

  if (!sessionId || !blueprint) {
    return new Response(JSON.stringify({ error: 'sessionId and blueprint required' }), {
      status: 400,
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
    });
  }

  // Load learner hints to improve generation
  let learnerHints = '';
  try {
    const hints = await db`
      SELECT type, pattern, suggestion, confidence
      FROM heb_learner_hints
      WHERE active = true
      ORDER BY confidence DESC
      LIMIT 20
    `;
    if (hints.length > 0) {
      learnerHints = '\n\nLEARNER HINTS (from prior deploy outcomes):\n' +
        hints.map((h: any) => `${h.type.toUpperCase()}: ${h.suggestion} (confidence: ${Math.round(h.confidence * 100)}%)`).join('\n');
    }
  } catch (_) {
    // Learner table may not exist yet — skip hints
  }

  // Load intent memory for this engine if it exists (for updates)
  let priorDecisions = '';
  try {
    const decisions = await db`
      SELECT creator_words, claude_interpretation, category
      FROM heb_design_decisions
      WHERE engine_slug = ${blueprint.slug}
      ORDER BY created_at ASC
    `;
    if (decisions.length > 0) {
      priorDecisions = '\n\nPRIOR DESIGN DECISIONS (from creator):\n' +
        decisions.map((d: any) => `[${d.category}] Creator: "${d.creator_words}" → Interpreted: ${d.claude_interpretation}`).join('\n');
    }
  } catch (_) {
    // No prior decisions — fresh build
  }

  const encoder = new TextEncoder();
  const stream = new ReadableStream({
    async start(controller) {
      const send = (event: string, data: any) => {
        controller.enqueue(encoder.encode(`event: ${event}\ndata: ${JSON.stringify(data)}\n\n`));
      };

      try {
        send('status', { phase: 'planning', message: 'Analyzing blueprint and planning architecture...' });

        // Phase 1: Generate the architecture plan
        const architecturePrompt = buildArchitecturePrompt(blueprint, learnerHints, priorDecisions);
        const archResponse = await callClaude(architecturePrompt, 4096);
        
        let architecture: any;
        try {
          architecture = JSON.parse(archResponse);
        } catch {
          architecture = { pages: [{ path: '/', name: 'Home' }], apiRoutes: ['/api/main'], components: [] };
        }

        send('architecture', { 
          pages: architecture.pages, 
          apiRoutes: architecture.apiRoutes,
          components: architecture.components || [],
          totalFiles: (architecture.pages?.length || 0) + (architecture.apiRoutes?.length || 0) + (architecture.components?.length || 0) + 5
        });

        // Phase 2: Generate files one by one
        const files: { path: string; content: string }[] = [];
        const totalFiles = (architecture.pages?.length || 0) + (architecture.apiRoutes?.length || 0) + (architecture.components?.length || 0) + 5;
        let fileIndex = 0;

        // Generate package.json
        send('status', { phase: 'generating', message: 'Generating package.json...', progress: fileIndex / totalFiles });
        const packageJson = generatePackageJson(blueprint);
        files.push({ path: 'package.json', content: packageJson });
        send('file', { path: 'package.json', size: packageJson.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });

        // Generate tailwind.config.ts
        send('status', { phase: 'generating', message: 'Generating tailwind config...', progress: fileIndex / totalFiles });
        const tailwindConfig = generateTailwindConfig(blueprint);
        files.push({ path: 'tailwind.config.ts', content: tailwindConfig });
        send('file', { path: 'tailwind.config.ts', size: tailwindConfig.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });

        // Generate next.config.js
        const nextConfig = `/** @type {import('next').NextConfig} */\nconst nextConfig = { reactStrictMode: true };\nmodule.exports = nextConfig;\n`;
        files.push({ path: 'next.config.js', content: nextConfig });
        send('file', { path: 'next.config.js', size: nextConfig.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });

        // Generate layout.tsx
        send('status', { phase: 'generating', message: 'Generating app layout...', progress: fileIndex / totalFiles });
        const layoutPrompt = buildLayoutPrompt(blueprint, architecture);
        const layoutContent = await callClaude(layoutPrompt, 4096);
        files.push({ path: 'app/layout.tsx', content: cleanCodeBlock(layoutContent) });
        send('file', { path: 'app/layout.tsx', size: layoutContent.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });

        // Generate globals.css
        const globalsCSS = generateGlobalsCss(blueprint);
        files.push({ path: 'app/globals.css', content: globalsCSS });
        send('file', { path: 'app/globals.css', size: globalsCSS.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });

        // Generate each page
        for (const page of architecture.pages || []) {
          send('status', { 
            phase: 'generating', 
            message: `Generating page: ${page.name || page.path}...`,
            progress: fileIndex / totalFiles 
          });

          const pagePrompt = buildPagePrompt(blueprint, architecture, page, learnerHints);
          const pageContent = await callClaude(pagePrompt, 8192);
          const pagePath = page.path === '/' ? 'app/page.tsx' : `app${page.path}/page.tsx`;
          files.push({ path: pagePath, content: cleanCodeBlock(pageContent) });
          send('file', { path: pagePath, size: pageContent.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });
        }

        // Generate each API route
        for (const route of architecture.apiRoutes || []) {
          send('status', { 
            phase: 'generating', 
            message: `Generating API: ${route}...`,
            progress: fileIndex / totalFiles 
          });

          const routePrompt = buildRoutePrompt(blueprint, architecture, route, learnerHints);
          const routeContent = await callClaude(routePrompt, 4096);
          files.push({ path: `app${route}/route.ts`, content: cleanCodeBlock(routeContent) });
          send('file', { path: `app${route}/route.ts`, size: routeContent.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });
        }

        // Generate each component
        for (const comp of architecture.components || []) {
          send('status', { 
            phase: 'generating', 
            message: `Generating component: ${comp.name || comp}...`,
            progress: fileIndex / totalFiles 
          });

          const compName = typeof comp === 'string' ? comp : comp.name;
          const compPrompt = buildComponentPrompt(blueprint, architecture, comp, learnerHints);
          const compContent = await callClaude(compPrompt, 4096);
          files.push({ path: `components/${compName}.tsx`, content: cleanCodeBlock(compContent) });
          send('file', { path: `components/${compName}.tsx`, size: compContent.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });
        }

        // Generate ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md
        const grammarContent = generateEngineGrammar(blueprint);
        files.push({ path: 'ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md', content: grammarContent });
        send('file', { path: 'ENGINE_GRAMMAR.md', size: grammarContent.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });

        // Generate README.md
        const readmeContent = generateReadme(blueprint, architecture);
        files.push({ path: 'README.md', content: readmeContent });
        send('file', { path: 'README.md', size: readmeContent.length, index: ++fileIndex, total: totalFiles });

        // Store session files in DB
        await db`
          UPDATE heb_workshop_sessions
          SET status = 'generated',
              generated_files = ${JSON.stringify(files.map(f => ({ path: f.path, size: f.content.length })))::"jsonb"},
              updated_at = NOW()
          WHERE id = ${sessionId}
        `;

        // Record design decision
        await db`
          INSERT INTO heb_design_decisions (engine_slug, category, creator_words, claude_interpretation)
          VALUES (${blueprint.slug}, 'architecture', 
                  ${`Generated from blueprint: ${blueprint.name}`},
                  ${`${files.length} files: ${architecture.pages?.length || 0} pages, ${architecture.apiRoutes?.length || 0} API routes, ${architecture.components?.length || 0} components`})
        `;

        send('complete', { 
          fileCount: files.length, 
          totalSize: files.reduce((sum, f) => sum + f.content.length, 0),
          files: files.map(f => ({ path: f.path, size: f.content.length }))
        });

        // Send all file contents as final payload
        send('payload', { files });

      } catch (error: any) {
        send('error', { message: error.message || 'Generation failed' });
      } finally {
        controller.close();
      }
    },
  });

  return new Response(stream, {
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'text/event-stream',
      'Cache-Control': 'no-cache',
      'Connection': 'keep-alive',
    },
  });
}

// === Claude API Call ===
async function callClaude(prompt: string, maxTokens: number): Promise<string> {
  const response = await fetch('https://api.anthropic.com/v1/messages', {
    method: 'POST',
    headers: {
      'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      'x-api-key': process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY!,
      'anthropic-version': '2023-06-01',
    },
    body: JSON.stringify({
      model: process.env.CLAUDE_MODEL || 'claude-sonnet-4-20250514',
      max_tokens: maxTokens,
      messages: [{ role: 'user', content: prompt }],
    }),
  });

  if (!response.ok) {
    const err = await response.text();
    throw new Error(`Claude API error: ${response.status} — ${err}`);
  }

  const data = await response.json();
  return data.content?.[0]?.text || '';
}

function generatePackageJson(blueprint: any): string {
  const deps: Record<string, string> = {
    'next': '^14.2.0',
    'react': '^18.3.0',
    'react-dom': '^18.3.0',
  };
  if (blueprint.usesAI) {
    deps['@anthropic-ai/sdk'] = '^0.30.0';
  }

  return JSON.stringify({
    name: blueprint.slug,
    version: '1.0.0',
    private: true,
    scripts: {
      dev: 'next dev',
      build: 'next build',
      start: 'next start',
      lint: 'next lint',
    },
    dependencies: deps,
    devDependencies: {
      '@types/node': '^20.0.0',
      '@types/react': '^18.3.0',
      '@types/react-dom': '^18.3.0',
      'autoprefixer': '^10.4.0',
      'postcss': '^8.4.0',
      'tailwindcss': '^3.4.0',
      'typescript': '^5.0.0',
    },
  }, null, 2);
}

function cleanCodeBlock(content: string): string {
  // Remove markdown code fences if Claude wraps the code in them
  return content
    .replace(/^```(?:tsx?|javascript|jsx?)?\n/gm, '')
    .replace(/\n```$/gm, '')
    .trim();
}

## File: `app/api/workshop/learner/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 4.0 API — Learner (Feature 8)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { getStats, getActiveHints, getHintsForPrompt, addManualHint, deactivateHint, getFrequentFlags } from '../../../../lib/learner-v2';

function isAuthed(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return false;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret') || req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return header === secret;
}

export async function GET(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const { searchParams } = new URL(req.url);
    const view = searchParams.get('view') || 'stats';

    switch (view) {
      case 'stats': {
        const stats = await getStats();
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, stats });
      }
      case 'hints': {
        const hints = await getActiveHints(0);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, hints });
      }
      case 'prompt': {
        const prompt = await getHintsForPrompt();
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, prompt });
      }
      case 'flags': {
        const flags = await getFrequentFlags(20);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, flags });
      }
      default:
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid view. Use: stats, hints, prompt, flags' }, { status: 400 });
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const { action, type, pattern, reason, hintId } = body;

    switch (action) {
      case 'add-hint': {
        if (!type || !pattern || !reason) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'type, pattern, reason required' }, { status: 400 });
        const hint = await addManualHint(type, pattern, reason);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, hint });
      }
      case 'deactivate': {
        if (!hintId) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'hintId required' }, { status: 400 });
        await deactivateHint(hintId);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true });
      }
      default:
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid action. Use: add-hint, deactivate' }, { status: 400 });
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

```

## File: `app/api/workshop/preview/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 4.0 API — Live Preview (Feature 2)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { createStagingDeploy, checkStagingHealth, getStagingEndpoints } from '../../../../lib/preview';

function isAuthed(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return false;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret') || req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return header === secret;
}

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const { action, engineSlug, repoOwner, repoName, stagingUrl, pages, apiRoutes } = body;

    switch (action) {
      case 'deploy': {
        if (!engineSlug || !repoOwner || !repoName) {
          return NextResponse.json({ error: 'engineSlug, repoOwner, repoName required' }, { status: 400 });
        }
        const result = await createStagingDeploy(engineSlug, repoOwner, repoName);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, ...result });
      }

      case 'health': {
        if (!stagingUrl) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'stagingUrl required' }, { status: 400 });
        const health = await checkStagingHealth(stagingUrl);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, ...health });
      }

      case 'verify': {
        if (!stagingUrl) return NextResponse.json({ error: 'stagingUrl required' }, { status: 400 });
        const endpoints = await getStagingEndpoints(stagingUrl, pages || [], apiRoutes || []);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, ...endpoints });
      }

      default:
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid action. Use: deploy, health, verify' }, { status: 400 });
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

```

## File: `app/api/workshop/ship-it/route.ts`

```typescript
// HEB 4.0 API — Ship It Gate (Feature 5)
import { NextRequest, NextResponse } from 'next/server';
import { runPreFlight, canShip } from '../../../../lib/ship-it';
import { createFactoryRun, executeFactory } from '../../../../lib/factory-pipeline';
import { recordDeployOutcome } from '../../../../lib/learner-v2';
import { recordDecisions } from '../../../../lib/intent-memory';

function isAuthed(req: NextRequest): boolean {
  const secret = process.env.HEB_CREATOR_SECRET;
  if (!secret) return false;
  const header = req.headers.get('x-heb-secret') || req.headers.get('authorization')?.replace('Bearer ', '');
  return header === secret;
}

export async function POST(req: NextRequest) {
  if (!isAuthed(req)) return new NextResponse(null, { status: 404 });

  try {
    const body = await req.json();
    const { action, blueprint, flagSession, stagingUrl, repoFiles, repoOwner, repoName, vercelProjectId } = body;

    switch (action) {
      case 'preflight': {
        if (!blueprint || !flagSession || !stagingUrl) {
          return NextResponse.json({ error: 'blueprint, flagSession, stagingUrl required' }, { status: 400 });
        }
        const preFlight = await runPreFlight(blueprint, flagSession, stagingUrl, repoFiles || []);
        const shipStatus = canShip(preFlight);
        return NextResponse.json({ success: true, preFlight, canShip: shipStatus });
      }

      case 'ship': {
        if (!blueprint || !flagSession || !stagingUrl) {
          return NextResponse.json({ error: 'blueprint, flagSession, stagingUrl required' }, { status: 400 });
        }

        // Run preflight one final time
        const preFlight = await runPreFlight(blueprint, flagSession, stagingUrl, repoFiles || []);
        const shipStatus = canShip(preFlight);

        if (!shipStatus.allowed) {
          return NextResponse.json({
            success: false,
            error: 'Ship It gate blocked',
            reason: shipStatus.reason,
            preFlight,
          }, { status: 422 });
        }

        // Record the Ship It decision
        await recordDecisions([{
          engineSlug: blueprint.engineSlug,
          phase: 'ship',
          decision: `Shipped to production. Grade: ${preFlight.grade}. ${preFlight.checks.filter(c => c.status === 'pass').length}/${preFlight.checks.length} checks passed.`,
          creatorWords: 'Ship It approved',
          claudeInterpretation: `Engine passed all blocking checks with grade ${preFlight.grade}`,
          category: 'governance',
        }]);

        // Create and start factory run
        const domain = `${blueprint.engineSlug}.hive.baby`;
        const run = createFactoryRun(blueprint.engineSlug, blueprint);

        // Execute factory in background (non-blocking response)
        const factoryPromise = executeFactory(run, blueprint, {
          repoOwner: repoOwner || process.env.GITHUB_OWNER || 'hive-baby',
          repoName: repoName || `hive-${blueprint.engineSlug}`,
          vercelProjectId: vercelProjectId || `hive-${blueprint.engineSlug}`,
          domain,
        }).then(async (completedRun) => {
          // Record outcome for Learner
          await recordDeployOutcome({
            engineSlug: blueprint.engineSlug,
            success: completedRun.status === 'completed',
            durationMs: completedRun.completedAt
              ? new Date(completedRun.completedAt).getTime() - new Date(completedRun.startedAt).getTime()
              : 0,
            fileCount: blueprint.pages.length + blueprint.apiRoutes.length,
            governanceGrade: preFlight.grade,
            errorMessage: completedRun.stopReason,
            errorCategory: completedRun.stopReason ? 'factory_stop' : undefined,
          });
        }).catch(console.error);

        // Don't await — return immediately
        return NextResponse.json({
          success: true,
          message: 'Engine entering factory — check Fleet tab for status',
          factoryRunId: run.id,
          domain,
          preFlight,
        });
      }

      default:
        return NextResponse.json({ error: 'Invalid action. Use: preflight, ship' }, { status: 400 });
    }
  } catch (err: any) {
    return NextResponse.json({ error: err.message }, { status: 500 });
  }
}

```
