## File: `app/workshop/page.tsx`

```tsx
'use client';

import { useState, useEffect, useRef, useCallback } from 'react';
import BlueprintCard from '@/components/BlueprintCard';
import PreviewFrame from '@/components/PreviewFrame';
import FlagQueue from '@/components/FlagQueue';
import ShipItGate from '@/components/ShipItGate';
import FactoryProgress from '@/components/FactoryProgress';

// === Types ===
type Phase = 'brainstorm' | 'blueprint' | 'generate' | 'preview' | 'break' | 'ship' | 'factory' | 'complete';
type Tab = 'workshop' | 'fleet' | 'batch' | 'learner';

interface Blueprint {
  name: string;
  slug: string;
  purpose: string;
  pages: { path: string; name: string; description: string }[];
  features: string[];
  pricing: string;
  pricingYear1: string;
  pricingYear2: string;
  viralLoop: string;
  theme: string;
  usesAI: boolean;
  governanceFlags: string[];
}

interface Flag {
  id: string;
  page: string;
  element: string;
  note: string;
  type: 'bug' | 'design' | 'feature' | 'content';
  status: 'open' | 'fixing' | 'fixed' | 'wontfix';
  screenshot?: string;
}

interface GeneratedFile {
  path: string;
  size: number;
}

interface FactoryStep {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  status: 'pending' | 'running' | 'passed' | 'failed' | 'skipped';
  detail?: string;
}

interface FleetEngine {
  slug: string;
  name: string;
  domain: string;
  status: string;
  governanceGrade: string;
  lastDeploy: string;
}

interface LearnerHint {
  type: string;
  pattern: string;
  suggestion: string;
  confidence: number;
}

// === Auth Helper ===
function getSecret(): string {
  if (typeof window === 'undefined') return '';
  return localStorage.getItem('heb_creator_secret') || '';
}

function apiHeaders(): Record<string, string> {
  return {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    'x-heb-secret': getSecret(),
  };
}

// === Main Component ===
export default function WorkshopPage() {
  // Auth
  const [authed, setAuthed] = useState(false);
  const [secretInput, setSecretInput] = useState('');

  // Navigation
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState<Tab>('workshop');

  // Workshop state
  const [phase, setPhase] = useState<Phase>('brainstorm');
  const [sessionId, setSessionId] = useState<string | null>(null);

  // Brainstorm
  const [brainstormInput, setBrainstormInput] = useState('');
  const [brainstormLoading, setBrainstormLoading] = useState(false);
  const [questions, setQuestions] = useState<{ id: string; question: string; options: string[] }[]>([]);
  const [answers, setAnswers] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});

  // Blueprint
  const [blueprint, setBlueprint] = useState<Blueprint | null>(null);

  // Generation
  const [genLog, setGenLog] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [genFiles, setGenFiles] = useState<GeneratedFile[]>([]);
  const [genProgress, setGenProgress] = useState(0);

  // Preview
  const [stagingUrl, setStagingUrl] = useState('');
  const [viewport, setViewport] = useState<'desktop' | 'mobile' | 'tablet'>('desktop');
  const [previewLang, setPreviewLang] = useState('en');

  // Break Mode
  const [flags, setFlags] = useState<Flag[]>([]);
  const [breakModeActive, setBreakModeActive] = useState(false);
  const [flagNote, setFlagNote] = useState('');
  const [fixingAll, setFixingAll] = useState(false);

  // Ship It
  const [preFlightResult, setPreFlightResult] = useState<any>(null);
  const [shipping, setShipping] = useState(false);

  // Factory
  const [factorySteps, setFactorySteps] = useState<FactoryStep[]>([]);
  const [factoryRunning, setFactoryRunning] = useState(false);
  const [finalUrl, setFinalUrl] = useState('');

  // Fleet
  const [fleet, setFleet] = useState<FleetEngine[]>([]);
  const [fleetLoading, setFleetLoading] = useState(false);

  // Batch
  const [batchInstruction, setBatchInstruction] = useState('');
  const [batchPlan, setBatchPlan] = useState<any>(null);
  const [batchRunning, setBatchRunning] = useState(false);

  // Learner
  const [hints, setHints] = useState<LearnerHint[]>([]);
  const [learnerStats, setLearnerStats] = useState<any>(null);

  // Log ref for auto-scroll
  const logRef = useRef<HTMLDivElement>(null);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (logRef.current) {
      logRef.current.scrollTop = logRef.current.scrollHeight;
    }
  }, [genLog]);

  // Auth check
  useEffect(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('heb_creator_secret');
    if (saved) setAuthed(true);
  }, []);

  const handleAuth = () => {
    localStorage.setItem('heb_creator_secret', secretInput);
    setAuthed(true);
  };

  // === API CALLS ===

  // 1. Brainstorm
  const submitBrainstorm = async () => {
    setBrainstormLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/brainstorm', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ input: brainstormInput }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
      setSessionId(data.sessionId);
      setBlueprint(data.blueprint);
      setQuestions(data.questions || []);
      if (data.questions?.length > 0) {
        setPhase('brainstorm'); // Stay for questions
      } else {
        setPhase('blueprint');
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `ERROR: ${err.message}`]);
    } finally {
      setBrainstormLoading(false);
    }
  };

  const submitAnswers = async () => {
    setBrainstormLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/brainstorm', {
        method: 'PUT',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ sessionId, answers }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
      setBlueprint(data.blueprint);
      setQuestions([]);
      setPhase('blueprint');
    } catch (err: any) {
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `ERROR: ${err.message}`]);
    } finally {
      setBrainstormLoading(false);
    }
  };

  // 2. Generate (SSE)
  const startGeneration = async () => {
    if (!blueprint || !sessionId) return;
    setPhase('generate');
    setGenLog([]);
    setGenFiles([]);
    setGenProgress(0);

    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/generate', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ sessionId, blueprint }),
      });

      if (!res.ok) throw new Error(`Generation failed: ${res.status}`);
      if (!res.body) throw new Error('No response body');

      const reader = res.body.getReader();
      const decoder = new TextDecoder();
      let buffer = '';

      while (true) {
        const { done, value } = await reader.read();
        if (done) break;

        buffer += decoder.decode(value, { stream: true });
        const lines = buffer.split('\n');
        buffer = lines.pop() || '';

        let currentEvent = '';
        for (const line of lines) {
          if (line.startsWith('event: ')) {
            currentEvent = line.slice(7);
          } else if (line.startsWith('data: ')) {
            try {
              const data = JSON.parse(line.slice(6));
              handleSSEEvent(currentEvent, data);
            } catch {}
          }
        }
      }
    } catch (err: any) {
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `FATAL: ${err.message}`]);
    }
  };

  const handleSSEEvent = (event: string, data: any) => {
    switch (event) {
      case 'status':
        setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `[${data.phase}] ${data.message}`]);
        if (data.progress !== undefined) setGenProgress(data.progress);
        break;
      case 'architecture':
        setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `Architecture: ${data.totalFiles} files planned`]);
        break;
      case 'file':
        setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `✓ ${data.path} (${(data.size / 1024).toFixed(1)}KB) [${data.index}/${data.total}]`]);
        setGenFiles(prev => [...prev, { path: data.path, size: data.size }]);
        setGenProgress(data.index / data.total);
        break;
      case 'complete':
        setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `\n✅ Generation complete — ${data.fileCount} files, ${(data.totalSize / 1024).toFixed(1)}KB total`]);
        setGenProgress(1);
        // Auto-advance to preview after a moment
        setTimeout(() => triggerPreview(), 1000);
        break;
      case 'error':
        setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `❌ ERROR: ${data.message}`]);
        break;
    }
  };

  // 3. Preview
  const triggerPreview = async () => {
    setPhase('preview');
    setGenLog(prev => [...prev, 'Deploying to staging...']);
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/preview', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ sessionId, engineSlug: blueprint?.slug }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
      setStagingUrl(data.stagingUrl || `https://dev.${blueprint?.slug}.hive.baby`);
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `✅ Staging live at ${data.stagingUrl}`]);
    } catch (err: any) {
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `Preview error: ${err.message}`]);
      // Use placeholder URL
      setStagingUrl(`https://dev.${blueprint?.slug || 'engine'}.hive.baby`);
    }
  };

  // 4. Break Mode - Add Flag
  const addFlag = () => {
    if (!flagNote.trim()) return;
    const newFlag: Flag = {
      id: crypto.randomUUID(),
      page: stagingUrl,
      element: 'user-flagged',
      note: flagNote,
      type: flagNote.toLowerCase().includes('bug') || flagNote.toLowerCase().includes('broken') || flagNote.toLowerCase().includes('error')
        ? 'bug'
        : flagNote.toLowerCase().includes('add') || flagNote.toLowerCase().includes('new')
        ? 'feature'
        : flagNote.toLowerCase().includes('color') || flagNote.toLowerCase().includes('font') || flagNote.toLowerCase().includes('size')
        ? 'design'
        : 'content',
      status: 'open',
    };
    setFlags(prev => [...prev, newFlag]);
    setFlagNote('');

    // Record flag via API
    fetch('/api/workshop/break-mode', {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: apiHeaders(),
      body: JSON.stringify({ 
        action: 'flag',
        sessionId,
        engineSlug: blueprint?.slug,
        flag: newFlag,
      }),
    }).catch(() => {});
  };

  // Fix All
  const fixAll = async () => {
    const openFlags = flags.filter(f => f.status === 'open');
    if (openFlags.length === 0) return;
    setFixingAll(true);

    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/break-mode', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({
          action: 'fix-all',
          sessionId,
          engineSlug: blueprint?.slug,
          flags: openFlags,
        }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);

      // Update flag statuses
      setFlags(prev => prev.map(f => {
        if (f.status !== 'open') return f;
        const result = data.results?.find((r: any) => r.flagId === f.id);
        return { ...f, status: result?.fixed ? 'fixed' : 'wontfix' };
      }));

      // Redeploy staging
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `Fixed ${data.fixedCount || openFlags.length} flags. Redeploying staging...`]);
      await triggerPreview();
    } catch (err: any) {
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `Fix error: ${err.message}`]);
    } finally {
      setFixingAll(false);
    }
  };

  // 5. Ship It
  const runPreFlight = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/ship-it', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'preflight', sessionId, engineSlug: blueprint?.slug }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      setPreFlightResult(data);
    } catch (err: any) {
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `Preflight error: ${err.message}`]);
    }
  };

  const shipIt = async () => {
    setShipping(true);
    setPhase('factory');
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/ship-it', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'ship', sessionId, engineSlug: blueprint?.slug }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      if (data.error) throw new Error(data.error);
      // Start factory monitoring
      pollFactory(data.factoryRunId || sessionId);
    } catch (err: any) {
      setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `Ship error: ${err.message}`]);
      setShipping(false);
    }
  };

  // 6. Factory
  const pollFactory = async (runId: string) => {
    setFactoryRunning(true);
    const defaultSteps: FactoryStep[] = [
      { id: 'f1', name: 'Governance Audit (final)', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f2', name: 'Merge staging → deploy', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f3', name: 'Vercel production build', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f4', name: 'Poll deployment ready', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f5', name: 'Cloudflare DNS', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f6', name: 'DNS propagation', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f7', name: 'SSL verification', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f8', name: 'Endpoint verification', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f9', name: 'Fleet registration', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f10', name: 'Monetization wiring', status: 'pending' },
      { id: 'f11', name: 'Learner log + memory', status: 'pending' },
    ];
    setFactorySteps(defaultSteps);

    const poll = async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/factory', {
          method: 'POST',
          headers: apiHeaders(),
          body: JSON.stringify({ runId }),
        });
        const data = await res.json();
        if (data.steps) setFactorySteps(data.steps);
        if (data.status === 'complete') {
          setFactoryRunning(false);
          setFinalUrl(data.url || `https://${blueprint?.slug}.hive.baby`);
          setPhase('complete');
          return;
        }
        if (data.status === 'failed') {
          setFactoryRunning(false);
          setGenLog(prev => [...prev, `Factory stopped: ${data.error}`]);
          return;
        }
        // Keep polling
        setTimeout(poll, 2000);
      } catch {
        setTimeout(poll, 3000);
      }
    };
    poll();
  };

  // Fleet
  const loadFleet = async () => {
    setFleetLoading(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/fleet-health', { headers: apiHeaders() });
      const data = await res.json();
      setFleet(data.engines || []);
    } catch {}
    setFleetLoading(false);
  };

  // Batch
  const planBatch = async () => {
    if (!batchInstruction.trim()) return;
    setBatchRunning(true);
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/batch', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'plan', instruction: batchInstruction }),
      });
      const data = await res.json();
      setBatchPlan(data.plan);
    } catch {}
    setBatchRunning(false);
  };

  const executeBatch = async () => {
    if (!batchPlan) return;
    setBatchRunning(true);
    try {
      await fetch('/api/workshop/batch', {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: apiHeaders(),
        body: JSON.stringify({ action: 'execute', plan: batchPlan }),
      });
      setBatchPlan(null);
      setBatchInstruction('');
    } catch {}
    setBatchRunning(false);
  };

  // Learner
  const loadLearner = async () => {
    try {
      const res = await fetch('/api/workshop/learner', { headers: apiHeaders() });
      const data = await res.json();
      setHints(data.hints || []);
      setLearnerStats(data.stats);
    } catch {}
  };

  // Load fleet/learner when switching tabs
  useEffect(() => {
    if (activeTab === 'fleet') loadFleet();
    if (activeTab === 'learner') loadLearner();
  }, [activeTab]);

  // === AUTH GATE ===
  if (!authed) {
    return (
      <div className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0a] flex items-center justify-center">
        <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-[#333] rounded-xl p-8 w-full max-w-md">
          <h1 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white mb-2">🐝 HEB 4.0 Workshop</h1>
          <p className="text-[#888] mb-6">Enter creator secret to continue</p>
          <input
            type="password"
            value={secretInput}
            onChange={e => setSecretInput(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleAuth()}
            placeholder="Creator secret"
            className="w-full bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-[#444] rounded-lg px-4 py-3 text-white mb-4 focus:border-[#f0c040] focus:outline-none"
          />
          <button
            onClick={handleAuth}
            className="w-full bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold py-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e0b030] transition"
          >
            Enter Workshop
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    );
  }

  // === MAIN LAYOUT ===
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-[#0a0a0a] text-white">
      {/* Top Navigation */}
      <header className="border-b border-[#222] px-6 py-4 flex items-center justify-between">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
          <span className="text-2xl">🐝</span>
          <h1 className="text-xl font-bold">HEB 4.0</h1>
          <span className="text-[#888] text-sm">Workshop + Factory</span>
        </div>
        <nav className="flex gap-1">
          {(['workshop', 'fleet', 'batch', 'learner'] as Tab[]).map(tab => (
            <button
              key={tab}
              onClick={() => setActiveTab(tab)}
              className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium transition ${
                activeTab === tab
                  ? 'bg-[#f0c040] text-black'
                  : 'text-[#888] hover:text-white hover:bg-[#1a1a1a]'
              }`}
            >
              {tab === 'workshop' ? '🔧 Workshop' :
               tab === 'fleet' ? '🏠 Fleet' :
               tab === 'batch' ? '📦 Batch' :
               '🧠 Learner'}
            </button>
          ))}
        </nav>
      </header>

      <main className="max-w-7xl mx-auto px-6 py-8">
        {/* === WORKSHOP TAB === */}
        {activeTab === 'workshop' && (
          <div>
            {/* Phase indicator */}
            <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-8 overflow-x-auto pb-2">
              {(['brainstorm', 'blueprint', 'generate', 'preview', 'break', 'ship', 'factory', 'complete'] as Phase[]).map((p, i) => (
                <div key={p} className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <div className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium whitespace-nowrap ${
                    phase === p ? 'bg-[#f0c040] text-black' :
                    (['brainstorm', 'blueprint', 'generate', 'preview', 'break', 'ship', 'factory', 'complete'].indexOf(phase) > i)
                      ? 'bg-[#2a3a2a] text-green-400' : 'bg-[#1a1a1a] text-[#555]'
                  }`}>
                    {p === 'brainstorm' ? '1. Brainstorm' :
                     p === 'blueprint' ? '2. Blueprint' :
                     p === 'generate' ? '3. Generate' :
                     p === 'preview' ? '4. Preview' :
                     p === 'break' ? '5. Break' :
                     p === 'ship' ? '6. Ship It' :
                     p === 'factory' ? '7. Factory' :
                     '8. Complete ✓'}
                  </div>
                  {i < 7 && <span className="text-[#333]">→</span>}
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>

            {/* === PHASE: BRAINSTORM === */}
            {phase === 'brainstorm' && !questions.length && (
              <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">
                <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-2">What do you want to build?</h2>
                <p className="text-[#888] mb-6">Dump your raw ideas. Fragments, contradictions, stream of consciousness — all welcome. HEB will extract the engine from the mess.</p>
                <textarea
                  value={brainstormInput}
                  onChange={e => setBrainstormInput(e.target.value)}
                  placeholder="I want an engine that helps families protect their recurring rituals from schedule erosion. Like Sunday pancakes with Dad, or Friday movie nights. No login wall. Make it feel warm, not corporate. Free forever. People should be able to share ritual cards with family members..."
                  className="w-full h-64 bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-[#333] rounded-xl p-6 text-white placeholder-[#555] resize-none focus:border-[#f0c040] focus:outline-none text-lg leading-relaxed"
                />
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center mt-4">
                  <span className="text-[#555] text-sm">{brainstormInput.length} characters</span>
                  <button
                    onClick={submitBrainstorm}
                    disabled={!brainstormInput.trim() || brainstormLoading}
                    className="bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold px-8 py-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e0b030] transition disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed"
                  >
                    {brainstormLoading ? 'Thinking...' : 'Extract Engine →'}
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* Brainstorm questions */}
            {phase === 'brainstorm' && questions.length > 0 && (
              <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">
                <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2">Quick decisions needed</h2>
                <p className="text-[#888] mb-6">HEB found {questions.length} decision point{questions.length > 1 ? 's' : ''} that would change the architecture.</p>
                {questions.map(q => (
                  <div key={q.id} className="bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-[#333] rounded-xl p-6 mb-4">
                    <p className="text-white font-medium mb-3">{q.question}</p>
                    <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mb-3">
                      {q.options.map(opt => (
                        <button
                          key={opt}
                          onClick={() => setAnswers(prev => ({ ...prev, [q.id]: opt }))}
                          className={`px-4 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm transition ${
                            answers[q.id] === opt
                              ? 'bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold'
                              : 'bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-[#444] text-[#ccc] hover:border-[#f0c040]'
                          }`}
                        >
                          {opt}
                        </button>
                      ))}
                    </div>
                    <input
                      type="text"
                      placeholder="Or type a different answer..."
                      value={answers[q.id] && !q.options.includes(answers[q.id]) ? answers[q.id] : ''}
                      onChange={e => setAnswers(prev => ({ ...prev, [q.id]: e.target.value }))}
                      className="w-full bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-[#333] rounded-lg px-4 py-2 text-white text-sm placeholder-[#555] focus:border-[#f0c040] focus:outline-none"
                    />
                  </div>
                ))}
                <button
                  onClick={submitAnswers}
                  disabled={Object.keys(answers).length < questions.length || brainstormLoading}
                  className="bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold px-8 py-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e0b030] transition disabled:opacity-50 mt-4"
                >
                  {brainstormLoading ? 'Refining...' : 'Finalize Blueprint →'}
                </button>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* === PHASE: BLUEPRINT === */}
            {phase === 'blueprint' && blueprint && (
              <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
                  <div>
                    <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold">Engine Blueprint</h2>
                    <p className="text-[#888]">Review and edit. Click Build when ready.</p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex gap-3">
                    <button
                      onClick={() => { setPhase('brainstorm'); setQuestions([]); }}
                      className="px-4 py-2 rounded-lg border border-[#444] text-[#888] hover:text-white transition"
                    >
                      ← Back to Brainstorm
                    </button>
                    <button
                      onClick={startGeneration}
                      className="bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold px-8 py-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e0b030] transition"
                    >
                      Build Engine →
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>
                <BlueprintCard
                  blueprint={blueprint}
                  onUpdate={setBlueprint}
                  editable={true}
                />
              </div>
            )}

            {/* === PHASE: GENERATE === */}
            {phase === 'generate' && (
              <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
                <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2">Building {blueprint?.name}...</h2>
                <p className="text-[#888] mb-4">Claude is generating your engine. Watch the stream.</p>

                {/* Progress bar */}
                <div className="w-full bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded-full h-3 mb-4 overflow-hidden">
                  <div
                    className="bg-[#f0c040] h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-300"
                    style={{ width: `${Math.round(genProgress * 100)}%` }}
                  />
                </div>
                <p className="text-[#888] text-sm mb-4">{Math.round(genProgress * 100)}% — {genFiles.length} files generated</p>

                {/* Log stream */}
                <div
                  ref={logRef}
                  className="bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-[#333] rounded-xl p-4 h-96 overflow-y-auto font-mono text-sm"
                >
                  {genLog.map((line, i) => (
                    <div
                      key={i}
                      className={`py-0.5 ${
                        line.startsWith('✓') ? 'text-green-400' :
                        line.startsWith('✅') ? 'text-green-300 font-bold' :
                        line.startsWith('❌') || line.startsWith('ERROR') || line.startsWith('FATAL') ? 'text-red-400' :
                        line.startsWith('[') ? 'text-[#888]' :
                        'text-[#ccc]'
                      }`}
                    >
                      {line}
                    </div>
                  ))}
                  {genProgress < 1 && (
                    <div className="text-[#f0c040] animate-pulse mt-1">▌</div>
                  )}
                </div>

                {/* File manifest */}
                {genFiles.length > 0 && (
                  <div className="mt-4 grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-3 gap-2">
                    {genFiles.map(f => (
                      <div key={f.path} className="bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-xs">
                        <span className="text-green-400">✓</span>{' '}
                        <span className="text-[#ccc]">{f.path}</span>{' '}
                        <span className="text-[#555]">{(f.size / 1024).toFixed(1)}K</span>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            )}

            {/* === PHASE: PREVIEW === */}
            {(phase === 'preview' || phase === 'break') && (
              <div>
                <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-4">
                  <div>
                    <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold">
                      {phase === 'break' ? '🔴 Break Mode' : '👁️ Preview'}
                    </h2>
                    <p className="text-[#888]">
                      {phase === 'break'
                        ? 'Flag issues. Click Fix All when done.'
                        : 'Click through your engine. Enter Break Mode to flag issues.'}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex gap-3">
                    {phase === 'preview' && (
                      <button
                        onClick={() => { setPhase('break'); setBreakModeActive(true); }}
                        className="px-4 py-2 rounded-lg bg-red-900 text-red-200 font-medium hover:bg-red-800 transition"
                      >
                        🔴 Enter Break Mode
                      </button>
                    )}
                    {phase === 'break' && (
                      <button
                        onClick={() => { setPhase('preview'); setBreakModeActive(false); }}
                        className="px-4 py-2 rounded-lg border border-[#444] text-[#888] hover:text-white transition"
                      >
                        Exit Break Mode
                      </button>
                    )}
                    {phase === 'preview' && flags.filter(f => f.status === 'open').length === 0 && (
                      <button
                        onClick={() => { setPhase('ship'); runPreFlight(); }}
                        className="bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold px-6 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e0b030] transition"
                      >
                        🚀 Ship It →
                      </button>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="grid grid-cols-1 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-6">
                  {/* Preview iframe */}
                  <div className="lg:col-span-2">
                    <PreviewFrame
                      stagingUrl={stagingUrl}
                      viewport={viewport}
                      language={previewLang}
                      breakModeActive={breakModeActive}
                      onViewportChange={setViewport}
                      onLanguageChange={setPreviewLang}
                    />
                  </div>

                  {/* Flag panel */}
                  <div>
                    {phase === 'break' && (
                      <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-red-900 rounded-xl p-4 mb-4">
                        <h3 className="text-sm font-bold text-red-300 mb-2">Flag an Issue</h3>
                        <input
                          type="text"
                          value={flagNote}
                          onChange={e => setFlagNote(e.target.value)}
                          onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && addFlag()}
                          placeholder="'header too small' or 'add share button'"
                          className="w-full bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-[#444] rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-white text-sm placeholder-[#555] focus:border-red-500 focus:outline-none mb-2"
                        />
                        <button
                          onClick={addFlag}
                          disabled={!flagNote.trim()}
                          className="w-full bg-red-800 text-red-100 py-2 rounded-lg text-sm font-medium hover:bg-red-700 transition disabled:opacity-50"
                        >
                          🔴 Flag It
                        </button>
                      </div>
                    )}

                    <FlagQueue
                      flags={flags}
                      onFixAll={fixAll}
                      fixing={fixingAll}
                    />

                    {/* Quick stats */}
                    <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded-xl p-4 mt-4">
                      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4 text-center">
                        <div>
                          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-red-400">{flags.filter(f => f.status === 'open').length}</div>
                          <div className="text-xs text-[#888]">Open</div>
                        </div>
                        <div>
                          <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-400">{flags.filter(f => f.status === 'fixed').length}</div>
                          <div className="text-xs text-[#888]">Fixed</div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            {/* === PHASE: SHIP IT === */}
            {phase === 'ship' && (
              <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">
                <ShipItGate
                  blueprint={blueprint}
                  preFlight={preFlightResult}
                  openFlags={flags.filter(f => f.status === 'open').length}
                  onShip={shipIt}
                  onBack={() => setPhase('preview')}
                  shipping={shipping}
                />
              </div>
            )}

            {/* === PHASE: FACTORY === */}
            {phase === 'factory' && (
              <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">
                <FactoryProgress
                  steps={factorySteps}
                  running={factoryRunning}
                  engineName={blueprint?.name || 'Engine'}
                />
              </div>
            )}

            {/* === PHASE: COMPLETE === */}
            {phase === 'complete' && (
              <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto text-center py-16">
                <div className="text-6xl mb-6">🎉</div>
                <h2 className="text-3xl font-bold mb-2">{blueprint?.name} is Live</h2>
                <a
                  href={finalUrl || `https://${blueprint?.slug}.hive.baby`}
                  target="_blank"
                  rel="noopener noreferrer"
                  className="text-[#f0c040] text-xl hover:underline"
                >
                  {finalUrl || `${blueprint?.slug}.hive.baby`}
                </a>
                <p className="text-[#888] mt-4 max-w-md mx-auto">
                  Your engine passed all governance checks, deployed to production, registered in the fleet, and is now being monitored.
                </p>
                <div className="flex gap-4 justify-center mt-8">
                  <button
                    onClick={() => {
                      setPhase('brainstorm');
                      setBrainstormInput('');
                      setBlueprint(null);
                      setGenLog([]);
                      setGenFiles([]);
                      setFlags([]);
                      setSessionId(null);
                    }}
                    className="bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold px-8 py-3 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e0b030] transition"
                  >
                    Build Another Engine
                  </button>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => setActiveTab('fleet')}
                    className="px-8 py-3 rounded-lg border border-[#444] text-[#888] hover:text-white transition"
                  >
                    View Fleet →
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        {/* === FLEET TAB === */}
        {activeTab === 'fleet' && (
          <div>
            <div className="flex justify-between items-center mb-6">
              <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold">🏠 Fleet</h2>
              <button
                onClick={loadFleet}
                disabled={fleetLoading}
                className="px-4 py-2 rounded-lg border border-[#444] text-[#888] hover:text-white transition"
              >
                {fleetLoading ? 'Loading...' : 'Refresh'}
              </button>
            </div>

            {fleet.length === 0 && !fleetLoading && (
              <div className="text-center text-[#888] py-16">
                <p className="text-lg">No engines in fleet yet.</p>
                <p className="text-sm mt-2">Build an engine or bulk-adopt existing ones.</p>
              </div>
            )}

            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 lg:grid-cols-3 gap-4">
              {fleet.map(engine => (
                <div key={engine.slug} className="bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-[#333] rounded-xl p-5">
                  <div className="flex justify-between items-start mb-3">
                    <h3 className="font-bold text-lg">{engine.name}</h3>
                    <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs font-bold ${
                      engine.governanceGrade === 'A' ? 'bg-green-900 text-green-300' :
                      engine.governanceGrade === 'B' ? 'bg-blue-900 text-blue-300' :
                      engine.governanceGrade === 'C' ? 'bg-yellow-900 text-yellow-300' :
                      'bg-red-900 text-red-300'
                    }`}>
                      {engine.governanceGrade}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  <a
                    href={`https://${engine.domain}`}
                    target="_blank"
                    rel="noopener noreferrer"
                    className="text-[#f0c040] text-sm hover:underline"
                  >
                    {engine.domain}
                  </a>
                  <div className="flex justify-between items-center mt-3 text-xs text-[#888]">
                    <span className={engine.status === 'healthy' ? 'text-green-400' : 'text-red-400'}>
                      ● {engine.status}
                    </span>
                    <span>{engine.lastDeploy}</span>
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex gap-2 mt-4">
                    <button
                      onClick={() => {
                        setActiveTab('workshop');
                        setPhase('brainstorm');
                        setBrainstormInput(`Upgrade ${engine.name}: `);
                      }}
                      className="flex-1 px-3 py-1.5 bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-[#444] rounded-lg text-xs text-[#ccc] hover:border-[#f0c040] transition"
                    >
                      Update
                    </button>
                    <button
                      className="flex-1 px-3 py-1.5 bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-[#444] rounded-lg text-xs text-[#ccc] hover:border-[#f0c040] transition"
                      onClick={() => {
                        fetch('/api/audit-engine', {
                          method: 'POST',
                          headers: apiHeaders(),
                          body: JSON.stringify({ slug: engine.slug }),
                        });
                      }}
                    >
                      Audit
                    </button>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* === BATCH TAB === */}
        {activeTab === 'batch' && (
          <div className="max-w-3xl mx-auto">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2">📦 Batch Operations</h2>
            <p className="text-[#888] mb-6">One instruction, applied intelligently across the fleet.</p>

            <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-[#333] rounded-xl p-6">
              <textarea
                value={batchInstruction}
                onChange={e => setBatchInstruction(e.target.value)}
                placeholder="Add multilingual ribbon to all engines that have AI calls"
                className="w-full h-32 bg-[#0a0a0a] border border-[#333] rounded-lg p-4 text-white placeholder-[#555] resize-none focus:border-[#f0c040] focus:outline-none"
              />
              <div className="flex justify-end mt-4">
                <button
                  onClick={planBatch}
                  disabled={!batchInstruction.trim() || batchRunning}
                  className="bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold px-6 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e0b030] transition disabled:opacity-50"
                >
                  {batchRunning ? 'Planning...' : 'Plan Batch →'}
                </button>
              </div>
            </div>

            {batchPlan && (
              <div className="mt-6 bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-[#333] rounded-xl p-6">
                <h3 className="font-bold mb-4">Batch Plan</h3>
                {batchPlan.actions?.map((action: any, i: number) => (
                  <div key={i} className="flex items-center gap-3 py-2 border-b border-[#222] last:border-0">
                    <span className={`text-sm ${
                      action.action === 'apply' ? 'text-green-400' :
                      action.action === 'skip' ? 'text-[#555]' :
                      'text-yellow-400'
                    }`}>
                      {action.action === 'apply' ? '✓' : action.action === 'skip' ? '—' : '⚠'}
                    </span>
                    <span className="font-medium">{action.engine}</span>
                    <span className="text-[#888] text-sm">{action.reason}</span>
                  </div>
                ))}
                <div className="flex gap-3 mt-4">
                  <button
                    onClick={executeBatch}
                    disabled={batchRunning}
                    className="bg-[#f0c040] text-black font-bold px-6 py-2 rounded-lg hover:bg-[#e0b030] transition disabled:opacity-50"
                  >
                    {batchRunning ? 'Executing...' : 'Apply All'}
                  </button>
                  <button
                    onClick={() => setBatchPlan(null)}
                    className="px-6 py-2 rounded-lg border border-[#444] text-[#888] hover:text-white transition"
                  >
                    Cancel
                  </button>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        )}

        {/* === LEARNER TAB === */}
        {activeTab === 'learner' && (
          <div className="max-w-4xl mx-auto">
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold mb-2">🧠 Learner</h2>
            <p className="text-[#888] mb-6">Patterns learned from {learnerStats?.totalDeploys || 0} deploys across {learnerStats?.totalEngines || 0} engines.</p>

            {learnerStats && (
              <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-4 mb-8">
                <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded-xl p-4 text-center">
                  <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-[#f0c040]">{learnerStats.totalDeploys || 0}</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-[#888]">Total Deploys</div>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded-xl p-4 text-center">
                  <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-green-400">{learnerStats.successRate || '—'}%</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-[#888]">Success Rate</div>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded-xl p-4 text-center">
                  <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{learnerStats.avgDuration || '—'}s</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-[#888]">Avg Duration</div>
                </div>
                <div className="bg-[#1a1a1a] rounded-xl p-4 text-center">
                  <div className="text-2xl font-bold text-blue-400">{hints.length}</div>
                  <div className="text-xs text-[#888]">Active Hints</div>
                </div>
              </div>
            )}

            <h3 className="font-bold text-lg mb-4">Prompt Hints</h3>
            {hints.length === 0 && (
              <p className="text-[#888] text-center py-8">No hints yet. Build and deploy engines to generate learning data.</p>
            )}
            {hints.map((hint, i) => (
              <div key={i} className="bg-[#1a1a1a] border border-[#333] rounded-xl p-4 mb-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-2">
                  <span className={`px-2 py-0.5 rounded text-xs font-bold ${
                    hint.type === 'AVOID' ? 'bg-red-900 text-red-300' : 'bg-green-900 text-green-300'
                  }`}>
                    {hint.type}
                  </span>
                  <span className="text-xs text-[#888]">{Math.round(hint.confidence * 100)}% confidence</span>
                </div>
                <p className="text-[#ccc] text-sm">{hint.suggestion}</p>
                {hint.pattern && (
                  <p className="text-[#555] text-xs mt-1 font-mono">{hint.pattern}</p>
                )}
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        )}
      </main>
    </div>
  );
}

```

## File: `components/BlueprintCard.tsx`

```tsx
'use client';

import { useState } from 'react';

interface BlueprintPage {
  name: string;
  route: string;
  description: string;
  components: string[];
  hasAICalls: boolean;
}

interface BlueprintRoute {
  path: string;
  method: string;
  purpose: string;
  usesAI: boolean;
}

interface PricingModel {
  type: string;
  year1Price: string;
  year2Price?: string;
  year3Price?: string;
  supportTier?: string;
}

interface RefinementQuestion {
  id: string;
  question: string;
  options: string[];
  answer?: string;
  impact: string;
}

interface Blueprint {
  id: string;
  engineSlug: string;
  engineName: string;
  purpose: string;
  pages: BlueprintPage[];
  apiRoutes: BlueprintRoute[];
  pricingModel: PricingModel;
  viralLoop: string;
  governanceFlags: string[];
  emotionalIntent: string;
  targetUser: string;
  assumptions: string[];
  contradictions: string[];
  refinementQuestions: RefinementQuestion[];
  status: string;
}

interface BlueprintCardProps {
  blueprint: Blueprint;
  onRefine: (answers: { questionId: string; answer: string }[], notes?: string) => void;
  onApprove: () => void;
  onEdit: (field: string, value: any) => void;
}

export default function BlueprintCard({ blueprint, onRefine, onApprove, onEdit }: BlueprintCardProps) {
  const [answers, setAnswers] = useState<Record<string, string>>({});
  const [additionalNotes, setAdditionalNotes] = useState('');
  const [editingField, setEditingField] = useState<string | null>(null);

  const hasQuestions = blueprint.refinementQuestions.length > 0;
  const hasContradictions = blueprint.contradictions.length > 0;
  const needsRefinement = hasQuestions || hasContradictions;

  const handleAnswer = (questionId: string, answer: string) => {
    setAnswers(prev => ({ ...prev, [questionId]: answer }));
  };

  const handleRefine = () => {
    const formattedAnswers = Object.entries(answers).map(([questionId, answer]) => ({ questionId, answer }));
    onRefine(formattedAnswers, additionalNotes || undefined);
  };

  const allQuestionsAnswered = blueprint.refinementQuestions.every(q => answers[q.id]);

  return (
    <div className="bg-zinc-900 border border-zinc-700 rounded-xl p-6 space-y-6">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
        <div>
          <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white">{blueprint.engineName}</h2>
          <p className="text-zinc-400 text-sm mt-1">{blueprint.engineSlug}.hive.baby</p>
        </div>
        <span className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-full text-xs font-medium ${
          blueprint.status === 'refined' ? 'bg-green-900 text-green-300' :
          blueprint.status === 'draft' ? 'bg-yellow-900 text-yellow-300' :
          'bg-zinc-700 text-zinc-300'
        }`}>
          {blueprint.status.toUpperCase()}
        </span>
      </div>

      {/* Purpose */}
      <div>
        <label className="text-xs font-medium text-zinc-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Purpose</label>
        <p className="text-white mt-1">{blueprint.purpose}</p>
      </div>

      {/* Two-column: Pages + API Routes */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-zinc-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Pages ({blueprint.pages.length})</label>
          <div className="mt-2 space-y-2">
            {blueprint.pages.map((page, i) => (
              <div key={i} className="bg-zinc-800 rounded-lg p-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className="text-white font-medium text-sm">{page.name}</span>
                  <span className="text-zinc-500 text-xs">{page.route}</span>
                  {page.hasAICalls && <span className="text-purple-400 text-xs">AI</span>}
                </div>
                <p className="text-zinc-400 text-xs mt-1">{page.description}</p>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-zinc-500 uppercase tracking-wide">API Routes ({blueprint.apiRoutes.length})</label>
          <div className="mt-2 space-y-2">
            {blueprint.apiRoutes.map((route, i) => (
              <div key={i} className="bg-zinc-800 rounded-lg p-3">
                <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                  <span className={`text-xs font-mono px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded ${
                    route.method === 'GET' ? 'bg-blue-900 text-blue-300' :
                    route.method === 'POST' ? 'bg-green-900 text-green-300' :
                    'bg-zinc-700 text-zinc-300'
                  }`}>{route.method}</span>
                  <span className="text-white text-sm font-mono">{route.path}</span>
                  {route.usesAI && <span className="text-purple-400 text-xs">AI</span>}
                </div>
                <p className="text-zinc-400 text-xs mt-1">{route.purpose}</p>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Pricing + Viral Loop */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-zinc-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Pricing</label>
          <div className="bg-zinc-800 rounded-lg p-3 mt-2">
            <p className="text-white text-sm">
              {blueprint.pricingModel.type === 'free' ? '🆓' : '💰'} {blueprint.pricingModel.year1Price}
              {blueprint.pricingModel.year2Price && ` → ${blueprint.pricingModel.year2Price}`}
            </p>
            {blueprint.pricingModel.supportTier && (
              <p className="text-zinc-400 text-xs mt-1">Support: {blueprint.pricingModel.supportTier}</p>
            )}
          </div>
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-zinc-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Viral Loop</label>
          <div className="bg-zinc-800 rounded-lg p-3 mt-2">
            <p className="text-white text-sm">🔄 {blueprint.viralLoop}</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Emotional Intent + Target User */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-4">
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-zinc-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Emotional Intent</label>
          <p className="text-zinc-300 text-sm mt-1">{blueprint.emotionalIntent}</p>
        </div>
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-zinc-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Target User</label>
          <p className="text-zinc-300 text-sm mt-1">{blueprint.targetUser}</p>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Governance Flags */}
      <div>
        <label className="text-xs font-medium text-zinc-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Governance</label>
        <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-2">
          {blueprint.governanceFlags.map((flag, i) => (
            <span key={i} className="bg-zinc-800 text-zinc-300 text-xs px-2 py-1 rounded-full">
              ✅ {flag}
            </span>
          ))}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Assumptions */}
      {blueprint.assumptions.length > 0 && (
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-yellow-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Assumptions (verify or override)</label>
          <div className="mt-2 space-y-1">
            {blueprint.assumptions.map((a, i) => (
              <p key={i} className="text-yellow-200 text-sm">⚠️ {a}</p>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Contradictions */}
      {hasContradictions && (
        <div>
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-red-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Contradictions (must resolve)</label>
          <div className="mt-2 space-y-1">
            {blueprint.contradictions.map((c, i) => (
              <p key={i} className="text-red-200 text-sm">❌ {c}</p>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Refinement Questions */}
      {hasQuestions && (
        <div className="border-t border-zinc-700 pt-4">
          <label className="text-xs font-medium text-amber-500 uppercase tracking-wide">Questions ({blueprint.refinementQuestions.length})</label>
          <div className="mt-3 space-y-4">
            {blueprint.refinementQuestions.map(q => (
              <div key={q.id} className="bg-zinc-800 rounded-lg p-4">
                <p className="text-white text-sm font-medium">{q.question}</p>
                <p className="text-zinc-500 text-xs mt-1">Impact: {q.impact}</p>
                <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2 mt-3">
                  {q.options.map((opt, i) => (
                    <button
                      key={i}
                      onClick={() => handleAnswer(q.id, opt)}
                      className={`px-3 py-1.5 rounded-lg text-sm transition-colors ${
                        answers[q.id] === opt
                          ? 'bg-amber-600 text-white'
                          : 'bg-zinc-700 text-zinc-300 hover:bg-zinc-600'
                      }`}
                    >
                      {opt}
                    </button>
                  ))}
                </div>
                {/* Free-text override */}
                <input
                  type="text"
                  placeholder="Or type your own answer..."
                  className="w-full mt-2 bg-zinc-900 border border-zinc-600 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder-zinc-500 focus:outline-none focus:border-amber-500"
                  onChange={e => { if (e.target.value) handleAnswer(q.id, e.target.value); }}
                />
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>

          <div className="mt-4">
            <textarea
              placeholder="Any additional notes for the blueprint..."
              value={additionalNotes}
              onChange={e => setAdditionalNotes(e.target.value)}
              className="w-full bg-zinc-900 border border-zinc-600 rounded-lg px-3 py-2 text-sm text-white placeholder-zinc-500 focus:outline-none focus:border-amber-500 h-20 resize-none"
            />
          </div>

          <button
            onClick={handleRefine}
            disabled={!allQuestionsAnswered}
            className="mt-3 px-6 py-2 bg-amber-600 text-white rounded-lg font-medium hover:bg-amber-500 disabled:opacity-40 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors"
          >
            Refine Blueprint
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* Approve Button (only when refined) */}
      {blueprint.status === 'refined' && (
        <div className="border-t border-zinc-700 pt-4 flex justify-end">
          <button
            onClick={onApprove}
            className="px-8 py-3 bg-green-600 text-white rounded-xl font-bold text-lg hover:bg-green-500 transition-colors flex items-center gap-2"
          >
            🔨 Build This Engine
          </button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

## File: `components/FactoryProgress.tsx`

```tsx
'use client';

import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

interface FactoryStep {
  number: number;
  name: string;
  status: 'pending' | 'running' | 'completed' | 'stopped' | 'skipped';
  startedAt?: string;
  completedAt?: string;
  detail?: string;
  error?: string;
}

interface FactoryRun {
  id: string;
  engineSlug: string;
  status: 'running' | 'completed' | 'stopped' | 'failed';
  currentStep: number;
  totalSteps: number;
  steps: FactoryStep[];
  startedAt: string;
  completedAt?: string;
  stoppedAt?: string;
  stopReason?: string;
}

interface FactoryProgressProps {
  run: FactoryRun;
  onReturnToWorkshop?: () => void;
  pollingInterval?: number;
  secretKey: string;
}

const stepIcons: Record<string, string> = {
  pending: '⏳',
  running: '🔄',
  completed: '✅',
  stopped: '🛑',
  skipped: '⏭️',
};

export default function FactoryProgress({ run: initialRun, onReturnToWorkshop, pollingInterval = 3000, secretKey }: FactoryProgressProps) {
  const [run, setRun] = useState<FactoryRun>(initialRun);

  useEffect(() => {
    if (run.status !== 'running') return;

    const interval = setInterval(async () => {
      try {
        const res = await fetch(`/api/workshop/factory?runId=${run.id}`, {
          headers: { 'x-heb-secret': secretKey },
        });
        if (res.ok) {
          const data = await res.json();
          if (data.run) setRun(data.run);
        }
      } catch {}
    }, pollingInterval);

    return () => clearInterval(interval);
  }, [run.id, run.status, pollingInterval, secretKey]);

  const completedSteps = run.steps.filter(s => s.status === 'completed').length;
  const progressPercent = (completedSteps / run.totalSteps) * 100;

  return (
    <div className="bg-zinc-900 border border-zinc-700 rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className={`px-6 py-4 border-b border-zinc-700 ${
        run.status === 'completed' ? 'bg-green-900/30' :
        run.status === 'stopped' || run.status === 'failed' ? 'bg-red-900/30' :
        'bg-zinc-800'
      }`}>
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-xl font-bold text-white flex items-center gap-2">
              🏭 Factory — {run.engineSlug}
            </h2>
            <p className="text-zinc-400 text-sm mt-1">
              {run.status === 'running' ? 'Processing...' :
               run.status === 'completed' ? 'Engine shipped successfully!' :
               run.status === 'stopped' ? `Stopped: ${run.stopReason}` :
               'Factory run failed'}
            </p>
          </div>
          <div className="text-right">
            <p className={`text-3xl font-black ${
              run.status === 'completed' ? 'text-green-400' :
              run.status === 'stopped' ? 'text-red-400' :
              'text-amber-400'
            }`}>
              {completedSteps}/{run.totalSteps}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        {/* Progress bar */}
        <div className="mt-3 h-2 bg-zinc-700 rounded-full overflow-hidden">
          <div
            className={`h-full rounded-full transition-all duration-500 ${
              run.status === 'completed' ? 'bg-green-500' :
              run.status === 'stopped' ? 'bg-red-500' :
              'bg-amber-500'
            }`}
            style={{ width: `${progressPercent}%` }}
          />
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Steps */}
      <div className="p-4 space-y-1">
        {run.steps.map((step) => (
          <div
            key={step.number}
            className={`flex items-start gap-3 px-3 py-2 rounded-lg ${
              step.status === 'running' ? 'bg-amber-900/20 border border-amber-800/50' :
              step.status === 'stopped' ? 'bg-red-900/20 border border-red-800/50' :
              step.status === 'completed' ? 'bg-zinc-800/30' :
              'bg-transparent'
            }`}
          >
            <span className={`text-sm mt-0.5 ${step.status === 'running' ? 'animate-spin' : ''}`}>
              {stepIcons[step.status]}
            </span>
            <div className="flex-1">
              <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                <span className={`text-sm font-medium ${
                  step.status === 'completed' ? 'text-zinc-400' :
                  step.status === 'running' ? 'text-amber-300' :
                  step.status === 'stopped' ? 'text-red-300' :
                  'text-zinc-500'
                }`}>
                  F{step.number}. {step.name}
                </span>
                <span className="text-zinc-600 text-xs">
                  {step.completedAt && step.startedAt
                    ? `${((new Date(step.completedAt).getTime() - new Date(step.startedAt).getTime()) / 1000).toFixed(1)}s`
                    : ''}
                </span>
              </div>
              {step.detail && (
                <p className="text-zinc-500 text-xs mt-0.5">{step.detail}</p>
              )}
              {step.error && (
                <p className="text-red-400 text-xs mt-0.5">Error: {step.error}</p>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Footer */}
      {(run.status === 'completed' || run.status === 'stopped') && (
        <div className="px-6 py-4 bg-zinc-800 border-t border-zinc-700 flex items-center justify-between">
          <span className="text-zinc-400 text-sm">
            {run.status === 'completed'
              ? `✅ Live at ${run.engineSlug}.hive.baby`
              : `🛑 Factory stopped — return to Workshop to fix`}
          </span>
          {onReturnToWorkshop && run.status === 'stopped' && (
            <button
              onClick={onReturnToWorkshop}
              className="px-4 py-2 bg-amber-600 text-white rounded-lg text-sm font-medium hover:bg-amber-500"
            >
              ← Return to Workshop
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}
```

```tsx
'use client';

interface Flag {
  id: string;
  type: 'bug' | 'design' | 'feature' | 'content';
  pageUrl: string;
  elementSelector: string;
  note: string;
  status: 'open' | 'fixing' | 'fixed' | 'dismissed' | 'failed';
  fixDiff?: string;
  fixError?: string;
  createdAt: string;
  resolvedAt?: string;
}

interface FlagQueueProps {
  flags: Flag[];
  onFixAll: () => void;
  onDismiss: (flagId: string) => void;
  isFixing: boolean;
}

const typeIcons: Record<string, string> = {
  bug: '🐛',
  design: '🎨',
  feature: '✨',
  content: '📝',
};

const statusColors: Record<string, string> = {
  open: 'border-red-600 bg-red-900/20',
  fixing: 'border-yellow-600 bg-yellow-900/20 animate-pulse',
  fixed: 'border-green-600 bg-green-900/20',
  dismissed: 'border-zinc-600 bg-zinc-800/50 opacity-60',
  failed: 'border-orange-600 bg-orange-900/20',
};

export default function FlagQueue({ flags, onFixAll, onDismiss, isFixing }: FlagQueueProps) {
  const openCount = flags.filter(f => f.status === 'open').length;
  const fixedCount = flags.filter(f => f.status === 'fixed').length;
  const failedCount = flags.filter(f => f.status === 'failed').length;

  if (flags.length === 0) {
    return (
      <div className="bg-zinc-900 border border-zinc-700 rounded-xl p-6 text-center">
        <p className="text-zinc-500 text-sm">No flags yet. Enable Break Mode in the preview to start flagging issues.</p>
      </div>
    );
  }

  return (
    <div className="bg-zinc-900 border border-zinc-700 rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
      {/* Header */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-3 bg-zinc-800 border-b border-zinc-700">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
          <h3 className="text-white font-medium text-sm">Flag Queue</h3>
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 text-xs">
            {openCount > 0 && <span className="text-red-400">{openCount} open</span>}
            {fixedCount > 0 && <span className="text-green-400">{fixedCount} fixed</span>}
            {failedCount > 0 && <span className="text-orange-400">{failedCount} need clarification</span>}
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {openCount > 0 && (
            <button
              onClick={onFixAll}
              disabled={isFixing}
              className="px-4 py-1.5 bg-amber-600 text-white rounded-lg text-sm font-medium hover:bg-amber-500 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed transition-colors flex items-center gap-1"
            >
              {isFixing ? (
                <>⏳ Fixing...</>
              ) : (
                <>🔧 Fix All ({openCount})</>
              )}
            </button>
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Flags list */}
      <div className="divide-y divide-zinc-800 max-h-96 overflow-y-auto">
        {flags.map(flag => (
          <div key={flag.id} className={`px-4 py-3 border-l-4 ${statusColors[flag.status]}`}>
            <div className="flex items-start justify-between">
              <div className="flex items-start gap-2 flex-1">
                <span className="text-lg">{typeIcons[flag.type] || '🔴'}</span>
                <div className="flex-1">
                  <p className="text-white text-sm">{flag.note}</p>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mt-1">
                    <span className="text-zinc-500 text-xs">
                      {new URL(flag.pageUrl).pathname || '/'}
                    </span>
                    <span className={`text-xs px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded ${
                      flag.status === 'open' ? 'bg-red-900 text-red-300' :
                      flag.status === 'fixed' ? 'bg-green-900 text-green-300' :
                      flag.status === 'failed' ? 'bg-orange-900 text-orange-300' :
                      flag.status === 'fixing' ? 'bg-yellow-900 text-yellow-300' :
                      'bg-zinc-700 text-zinc-400'
                    }`}>
                      {flag.status}
                    </span>
                  </div>
                  {flag.fixDiff && (
                    <p className="text-green-400 text-xs mt-1">✅ {flag.fixDiff}</p>
                  )}
                  {flag.fixError && (
                    <p className="text-orange-400 text-xs mt-1">❓ {flag.fixError}</p>
                  )}
                </div>
              </div>

              {flag.status === 'open' && (
                <button
                  onClick={() => onDismiss(flag.id)}
                  className="text-zinc-500 hover:text-zinc-300 text-xs ml-2"
                  title="Dismiss flag"
                >
                  ✕
                </button>
              )}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```tsx
'use client';

import { useState, useEffect, useRef } from 'react';

interface PreviewFrameProps {
  stagingUrl: string;
  breakModeActive: boolean;
  onFlag: (flag: { pageUrl: string; elementSelector: string; note: string; type?: string }) => void;
  onToggleBreakMode: () => void;
}

export default function PreviewFrame({ stagingUrl, breakModeActive, onFlag, onToggleBreakMode }: PreviewFrameProps) {
  const [viewport, setViewport] = useState<'desktop' | 'tablet' | 'mobile'>('desktop');
  const [language, setLanguage] = useState('en');
  const [flagNote, setFlagNote] = useState('');
  const [showFlagInput, setShowFlagInput] = useState(false);
  const [clickTarget, setClickTarget] = useState<{ x: number; y: number } | null>(null);
  const iframeRef = useRef<HTMLIFrameElement>(null);

  const viewportWidths = { desktop: 1280, tablet: 768, mobile: 375 };
  const viewportHeights = { desktop: 800, tablet: 1024, mobile: 812 };

  const currentUrl = language !== 'en'
    ? `${stagingUrl}?lang=${language}`
    : stagingUrl;

  const handleFlagSubmit = () => {
    if (!flagNote.trim()) return;
    onFlag({
      pageUrl: currentUrl,
      elementSelector: clickTarget ? `click@${clickTarget.x},${clickTarget.y}` : 'unknown',
      note: flagNote.trim(),
    });
    setFlagNote('');
    setShowFlagInput(false);
    setClickTarget(null);
  };

  return (
    <div className="bg-zinc-900 border border-zinc-700 rounded-xl overflow-hidden">
      {/* Toolbar */}
      <div className="flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 bg-zinc-800 border-b border-zinc-700">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {/* Viewport switcher */}
          {(['desktop', 'tablet', 'mobile'] as const).map(v => (
            <button
              key={v}
              onClick={() => setViewport(v)}
              className={`px-2 py-1 rounded text-xs font-medium transition-colors ${
                viewport === v ? 'bg-zinc-600 text-white' : 'text-zinc-400 hover:text-white'
              }`}
            >
              {v === 'desktop' ? '🖥️' : v === 'tablet' ? '📱' : '📲'} {v}
            </button>
          ))}

          <span className="text-zinc-600 mx-2">|</span>

          {/* Language switcher */}
          <select
            value={language}
            onChange={e => setLanguage(e.target.value)}
            className="bg-zinc-700 text-white text-xs rounded px-2 py-1 border border-zinc-600"
          >
            <option value="en">EN</option>
            <option value="ar">AR</option>
            <option value="fr">FR</option>
            <option value="es">ES</option>
            <option value="de">DE</option>
            <option value="zh">ZH</option>
            <option value="ja">JA</option>
            <option value="pt">PT</option>
            <option value="hi">HI</option>
          </select>
        </div>

        <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
          {/* Break Mode toggle */}
          <button
            onClick={onToggleBreakMode}
            className={`px-3 py-1 rounded-lg text-xs font-bold transition-colors ${
              breakModeActive
                ? 'bg-red-600 text-white animate-pulse'
                : 'bg-zinc-700 text-zinc-300 hover:bg-red-800 hover:text-white'
            }`}
          >
            {breakModeActive ? '🔴 BREAK MODE ON' : '🔴 Break Mode'}
          </button>

          {/* External link */}
          <a
            href={stagingUrl}
            target="_blank"
            rel="noopener noreferrer"
            className="text-zinc-400 hover:text-white text-xs"
          >
            🔗 Open
          </a>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Flag Input (shown when break mode active and user clicks) */}
      {showFlagInput && (
        <div className="px-4 py-3 bg-red-900/30 border-b border-red-800 flex items-center gap-2">
          <span className="text-red-400 text-sm">🔴</span>
          <input
            type="text"
            value={flagNote}
            onChange={e => setFlagNote(e.target.value)}
            onKeyDown={e => e.key === 'Enter' && handleFlagSubmit()}
            placeholder="What's wrong? (e.g., 'button does nothing', 'font too small', 'add share button here')"
            className="flex-1 bg-zinc-900 border border-red-700 rounded-lg px-3 py-1.5 text-sm text-white placeholder-zinc-500 focus:outline-none focus:border-red-400"
            autoFocus
          />
          <button
            onClick={handleFlagSubmit}
            className="px-3 py-1.5 bg-red-600 text-white rounded-lg text-sm font-medium hover:bg-red-500"
          >
            Flag
          </button>
          <button
            onClick={() => { setShowFlagInput(false); setClickTarget(null); }}
            className="text-zinc-400 hover:text-white text-sm"
          >
            ✕
          </button>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* iframe */}
      <div
        className="flex justify-center bg-zinc-950 p-4"
        style={{ minHeight: '600px' }}
      >
        <div
          className="relative transition-all duration-300 ease-in-out"
          style={{
            width: `${viewportWidths[viewport]}px`,
            maxWidth: '100%',
          }}
        >
          <iframe
            ref={iframeRef}
            src={currentUrl}
            className="w-full bg-white rounded-lg shadow-2xl"
            style={{
              height: `${viewportHeights[viewport]}px`,
              border: breakModeActive ? '2px solid #ef4444' : '1px solid #3f3f46',
              cursor: breakModeActive ? 'crosshair' : 'default',
            }}
            sandbox="allow-scripts allow-same-origin allow-forms allow-popups"
            onClick={(e) => {
              if (breakModeActive) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const rect = (e.target as HTMLElement).getBoundingClientRect();
                setClickTarget({ x: e.clientX - rect.left, y: e.clientY - rect.top });
                setShowFlagInput(true);
              }
            }}
          />
          {/* Break mode overlay for click capture */}
          {breakModeActive && (
            <div
              className="absolute inset-0 cursor-crosshair rounded-lg"
              style={{ background: 'rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.05)' }}
              onClick={(e) => {
                const rect = (e.target as HTMLElement).getBoundingClientRect();
                setClickTarget({ x: e.clientX - rect.left, y: e.clientY - rect.top });
                setShowFlagInput(true);
              }}
            />
          )}
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Status bar */}
      <div className="px-4 py-2 bg-zinc-800 border-t border-zinc-700 flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-zinc-500">
        <span>{viewport} ({viewportWidths[viewport]}x{viewportHeights[viewport]})</span>
        <span>{language.toUpperCase()} | {stagingUrl}</span>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```

```tsx
'use client';

interface PreFlightCheck {
  id: string;
  name: string;
  category: string;
  status: 'pass' | 'fail' | 'warn' | 'auto-fixable';
  detail: string;
  blocking: boolean;
}

interface ShipItGateProps {
  checks: PreFlightCheck[];
  grade: string;
  canShip: boolean;
  blockers: string[];
  warnings: string[];
  autoFixable: string[];
  onShip: () => void;
  onAutoFix: () => void;
  onBackToWorkshop: () => void;
  isShipping: boolean;
  engineName: string;
  domain: string;
  openFlagCount: number;
}

const statusIcons: Record<string, string> = {
  pass: '✅',
  fail: '❌',
  warn: '⚠️',
  'auto-fixable': '🔧',
};

const categoryLabels: Record<string, string> = {
  governance: '👑 Governance',
  quality: '✨ Quality',
  security: '🔒 Security',
  ux: '🎨 UX',
  metadata: '📋 Metadata',
};

export default function ShipItGate({
  checks, grade, canShip, blockers, warnings, autoFixable,
  onShip, onAutoFix, onBackToWorkshop, isShipping, engineName, domain, openFlagCount,
}: ShipItGateProps) {
  const passCount = checks.filter(c => c.status === 'pass').length;
  const totalCount = checks.length;
  const gradeColor = grade.startsWith('A') ? 'text-green-400' : grade === 'B' ? 'text-yellow-400' : 'text-red-400';

  // Group checks by category
  const grouped: Record<string, PreFlightCheck[]> = {};
  for (const check of checks) {
    if (!grouped[check.category]) grouped[check.category] = [];
    grouped[check.category].push(check);
  }

  return (
    <div className="bg-zinc-900 border-2 border-zinc-600 rounded-2xl overflow-hidden">
      {/* Ship It Header */}
      <div className="bg-gradient-to-r from-zinc-800 to-zinc-900 px-6 py-5 border-b border-zinc-700">
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
          <div>
            <h2 className="text-2xl font-bold text-white flex items-center gap-2">
              🚀 Ship It — {engineName}
            </h2>
            <p className="text-zinc-400 mt-1">{domain}</p>
          </div>
          <div className="text-right">
            <p className={`text-4xl font-black ${gradeColor}`}>{grade}</p>
            <p className="text-zinc-500 text-xs">{passCount}/{totalCount} checks</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>

      {/* Checks by category */}
      <div className="p-6 space-y-6">
        {Object.entries(grouped).map(([category, categoryChecks]) => (
          <div key={category}>
            <h3 className="text-sm font-medium text-zinc-400 mb-2">
              {categoryLabels[category] || category}
            </h3>
            <div className="space-y-1">
              {categoryChecks.map(check => (
                <div
                  key={check.id}
                  className={`flex items-center justify-between px-3 py-2 rounded-lg ${
                    check.status === 'fail' && check.blocking ? 'bg-red-900/30' :
                    check.status === 'fail' ? 'bg-yellow-900/20' :
                    check.status === 'auto-fixable' ? 'bg-blue-900/20' :
                    'bg-zinc-800/50'
                  }`}
                >
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
                    <span>{statusIcons[check.status]}</span>
                    <span className={`text-sm ${check.status === 'pass' ? 'text-zinc-300' : 'text-white'}`}>
                      {check.name}
                    </span>
                    {check.blocking && check.status === 'fail' && (
                      <span className="text-xs bg-red-800 text-red-200 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded">BLOCKING</span>
                    )}
                  </div>
                  <span className="text-zinc-500 text-xs max-w-xs truncate">{check.detail}</span>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Summary + Actions */}
      <div className="px-6 py-4 bg-zinc-800 border-t border-zinc-700">
        {/* Blockers */}
        {blockers.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mb-4 p-3 bg-red-900/30 border border-red-800 rounded-lg">
            <p className="text-red-300 text-sm font-medium">🚫 {blockers.length} Blocking Issue{blockers.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}</p>
            <ul className="mt-1 text-red-200 text-xs space-y-1">
              {blockers.map((b, i) => <li key={i}>• {b}</li>)}
            </ul>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Auto-fixable */}
        {autoFixable.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mb-4 p-3 bg-blue-900/30 border border-blue-800 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-between">
            <div>
              <p className="text-blue-300 text-sm font-medium">🔧 {autoFixable.length} Auto-Fixable</p>
              <p className="text-blue-200 text-xs mt-0.5">{autoFixable.join(', ')}</p>
            </div>
            <button
              onClick={onAutoFix}
              className="px-4 py-1.5 bg-blue-600 text-white rounded-lg text-sm hover:bg-blue-500"
            >
              Auto-Fix All
            </button>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Warnings */}
        {warnings.length > 0 && (
          <div className="mb-4 p-3 bg-yellow-900/20 border border-yellow-800/50 rounded-lg">
            <p className="text-yellow-300 text-sm font-medium">⚠️ {warnings.length} Warning{warnings.length > 1 ? 's' : ''} (non-blocking)</p>
            <p className="text-yellow-200 text-xs mt-0.5">{warnings.join(', ')}</p>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Action buttons */}
        <div className="flex items-center justify-between mt-2">
          <button
            onClick={onBackToWorkshop}
            className="px-4 py-2 text-zinc-400 hover:text-white text-sm transition-colors"
          >
            ← Back to Workshop
          </button>

          <button
            onClick={onShip}
            disabled={!canShip || isShipping}
            className={`px-8 py-3 rounded-xl font-bold text-lg transition-all flex items-center gap-2 ${
              canShip
                ? 'bg-green-600 text-white hover:bg-green-500 hover:scale-105'
                : 'bg-zinc-700 text-zinc-500 cursor-not-allowed'
            }`}
          >
            {isShipping ? (
              <>⏳ Shipping...</>
            ) : canShip ? (
              <>🚀 Ship It</>
            ) : (
              <>🔒 Blocked ({blockers.length})</>
            )}
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  );
}
```
